org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/platform/StitchPlatformGroupsScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.checkbox.Checkbox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.contextmenu.ContextMenu;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.contextmenu.MenuItem;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.notification.Notification.Position;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextArea;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.textfield.TextField;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveObserver;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchTabbedDetailsPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialogs;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchDirtyStateSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditableDetailPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchEditorModeController;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchTreeNav;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchTreeNodeAdapter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

public class StitchPlatformGroupsScreen extends StitchPage implements BeforeLeaveObserver {
  private final StitchPlatformGroupsProvider provider;
  private final StitchGroupsTreeAdapter treeAdapter = new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter();
  private final StitchGroupsOuEditor ouEditor = new StitchGroupsOuEditor();
  private final StitchGroupsGroupEditor groupEditor = new StitchGroupsGroupEditor();
  private final StitchEmptyState defaultNoSelectionState =
      new StitchEmptyState("No group selected", "Select an OU or Group to view details.");
  private final StitchEmptyState missingModelState =
      new StitchEmptyState(
          "Platform model unavailable", "Definition platform/platform was not found in DiscoveryCache.");

  private final StitchEditorModeController editorMode = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode> browserShell;
  private final StitchTreeNodeAdapter<StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode> nodeAdapter =
      new StitchTreeNodeAdapter<>() {
        @Override
        public String nodeId(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
          return node == null ? null : node.id();
        }

        @Override
        public StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode nodeById(String nodeId) {
          return nodeId == null ? null : snapshot.byId().get(nodeId);
        }
      };

  private final StitchEditableDetailPanel<StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode> detailPanel;
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH", event -> requestRefresh());
  private final Button addOuAction = iconAction(VaadinIcon.FOLDER_ADD, "Add organizational unit", this::openCreateOu);
  private final Button addGroupAction = iconAction(VaadinIcon.PLUS_CIRCLE_O, "Add group", this::openCreateGroup);

  private DefinitionPlatform loadedModel;
  private DefinitionPlatform workingModel;
  private StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeSnapshot snapshot =
      new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeSnapshot(List.of(), Map.of());

  public StitchPlatformGroupsScreen(
      StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig config, StitchPlatformGroupsProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle());
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    addClassName("stitch-groups-page");
    body().addClassName("stitch-groups-body");
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refreshAction);
    refreshAction.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh");
    addPageAction(refreshAction);

    detailPanel =
        new StitchEditableDetailPanel<>(
            editorMode,
            dirtyStateSupport,
            this::detailSectionTitle,
            this::buildDetailContent,
            node -> {},
            this::saveChanges,
            this::discardChanges);
    detailPanel
        .withReadOnlyActions(this::detailReadOnlyActions)
        .withEditActions(this::detailEditActions)
        .onStateChange(this::rerenderDetails);

    browserShell =
        new StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<>(
            nodeAdapter,
            dirtyStateSupport,
            editorMode::hasUnsavedChanges,
            this::saveChanges,
            this::discardChanges,
            this::onSelectionApplied);

    browserShell
        .setNavHeaderTitle("ORGANIZATION")
        .setDetailHeaderTitle("DETAILS")
        .setNoSelectionContent(defaultNoSelectionState)
        .setNoDetailsContent(new StitchEmptyState("No details", "No details available for this node."))
        .setChildResolver(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode::children)
        .setLabelResolver(this::treeLabel)
        .setNodeIconRenderer(this::treeIcon)
        .setNodeDecoratorRenderer(this::treeDecorator)
        .setDetailRenderer(detailPanel::render);
    browserShell.treeNav().setNodeLabelClassNameProvider(this::treeLabelClass);
    browserShell.treeNav().withNodeIconClickBehavior(StitchTreeNav.NodeIconClickBehavior.TOGGLE_EXPAND_COLLAPSE);
    browserShell.addToolbarActions(addOuAction, addGroupAction);

    addToBody(browserShell);
    browserShell.layout().addClassName("stitch-tree-layout--groups");
    browserShell.treeNav().addClassName("stitch-tree-nav--groups");
    reloadData(true);
  }

  @Override
  public void beforeLeave(BeforeLeaveEvent event) {
    browserShell.guardBeforeLeave(event);
  }

  private void onSelectionApplied(String nodeId) {
    editorMode.clear();
    rerenderDetails();
  }

  private void rerenderDetails() {
    browserShell.setDetailRenderer(detailPanel::render);
  }

  private void syncTreeSelectionAndDetails() {
    browserShell.syncSelection();
    rerenderDetails();
  }

  private void requestRefresh() {
    if (!editorMode.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      reloadData(false);
      return;
    }

    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        this::saveChanges,
        () -> reloadData(false),
        () -> {});
  }

  private void reloadData(boolean initialLoad) {
    Optional<DefinitionPlatform> resolved = provider.loadPlatformModel();
    if (resolved.isEmpty()) {
      loadedModel = null;
      workingModel = null;
      snapshot = new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeSnapshot(List.of(), Map.of());
      browserShell.setSelectedNodeId(null);
      editorMode.clear();
      browserShell.setRoots(List.of());
      browserShell.setNoSelectionContent(missingModelState);
      syncTreeSelectionAndDetails();
      if (!initialLoad) {
        Notification.show("Platform model not found", 2400, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      }
      return;
    }

    DefinitionPlatform fresh = treeAdapter.deepCopy(resolved.get());
    loadedModel = treeAdapter.deepCopy(fresh);
    workingModel = treeAdapter.deepCopy(fresh);
    snapshot = treeAdapter.snapshot(workingModel);
    browserShell.setNoSelectionContent(defaultNoSelectionState);
    editorMode.clear();

    if (browserShell.selectedNodeId() == null
        || !snapshot.byId().containsKey(browserShell.selectedNodeId())) {
      browserShell.setSelectedNodeId(null);
    }

    browserShell.setRoots(snapshot.roots());
    syncTreeSelectionAndDetails();
    if (!initialLoad) {
      Notification.show("Reloaded platform model", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
    }
  }

  private String detailSectionTitle(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return "DETAILS";
    }
    return node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU
        ? "OU DETAILS"
        : "GROUP DETAILS";
  }

  private List<Component> detailReadOnlyActions(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    actions.add(addMemberAction(node));
    actions.add(moreActions(node));
    return actions;
  }

  private List<Component> detailEditActions(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    actions.add(saveAction());
    actions.add(cancelAction());
    actions.add(addMemberAction(node));
    actions.add(moreActions(node));
    return actions;
  }

  private Button saveAction() {
    Button save = new Button("SAVE", event -> saveChanges());
    save.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(save);
    save.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Save changes");
    return save;
  }

  private Button cancelAction() {
    Button cancel = new Button("CANCEL", event -> cancelEditRequested());
    cancel.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(cancel);
    cancel.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Cancel editing");
    return cancel;
  }

  private void cancelEditRequested() {
    if (!editorMode.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      editorMode.clear();
      rerenderDetails();
      return;
    }
    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        this::saveChanges,
        () -> {
          discardChanges();
          editorMode.clear();
          rerenderDetails();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private Button addMemberAction(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    Button addMember = new Button("ADD MEMBER", event -> openAddMemberDialog(node));
    addMember.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(addMember);
    addMember.setEnabled(node != null && node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.GROUP);
    addMember.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Add member");
    return addMember;
  }

  private Component moreActions(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    Button more = new Button("MORE");
    more.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(more);
    more.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "More actions");
    ContextMenu menu = new ContextMenu(more);
    menu.setOpenOnClick(true);
    menu.addItem("Manage Organization", event -> openManageOrganizationDialog("create-ou", nodeId(node)));
    menu.addItem("Add OU", event -> openManageOrganizationDialog("create-ou", nodeId(node)));
    menu.addItem("Add Group", event -> openManageOrganizationDialog("create-group", nodeId(node)));
    menu.addItem("Rename", event -> openManageOrganizationDialog("rename", nodeId(node)));
    MenuItem deleteItem = menu.addItem("Delete", event -> openManageOrganizationDialog("delete", nodeId(node)));
    if (node != null && node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU && "ou:".equals(node.id())) {
      deleteItem.setEnabled(false);
    }
    return more;
  }

  private String nodeId(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    return node == null ? browserShell.selectedNodeId() : node.id();
  }

  private void openCreateOu() {
    openManageOrganizationDialog("create-ou", browserShell.selectedNodeId());
  }

  private void openCreateGroup() {
    openManageOrganizationDialog("create-group", browserShell.selectedNodeId());
  }

  private Component buildDetailContent(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node, boolean editMode) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU) {
      ouEditor.setReadOnly(!editMode);
      ouEditor.setNode(node, draft -> applyOuDraft(node.id(), draft));
      return ouEditor;
    }
    groupEditor.setReadOnly(!editMode);
    groupEditor.setNode(
        node,
        currentUsers(),
        currentServices(),
        draft -> applyGroupDraft(node.id(), draft));
    return groupEditor;
  }

  private void openAddMemberDialog(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null || node.kind() != StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.GROUP) {
      return;
    }
    List<MemberCandidate> candidates = availableMemberCandidates(node);
    if (candidates.isEmpty()) {
      Notification.show("No additional members available to add.", 1800, Position.BOTTOM_START);
      return;
    }

    ComboBox<MemberCandidate> picker = new ComboBox<>("Search Member");
    picker.setWidthFull();
    picker.setItems(candidates);
    picker.setItemLabelGenerator(MemberCandidate::label);
    picker.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    picker.setClearButtonVisible(true);
    picker.setPlaceholder("Type to search users or services");
    picker.setValue(candidates.get(0));

    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Add Member");
    dialog.addToBody(picker);
    dialog.addPrimaryAction(
        "ADD MEMBER",
        () -> {
          MemberCandidate candidate = picker.getValue();
          if (candidate == null) {
            Notification.show("Select a member first.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          if (candidate.kind() == MemberKind.HUMAN) {
            List<String> nextHumans = new ArrayList<>(node.userIds());
            if (!addDistinctIgnoreCase(nextHumans, candidate.id())) {
              Notification.show("Member already exists.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
              return;
            }
            updateGroupMembership(node.id(), node.name(), node.description(), nextHumans, node.serviceIds());
          } else {
            List<String> nextServices = new ArrayList<>(node.serviceIds());
            if (!addDistinctIgnoreCase(nextServices, candidate.id())) {
              Notification.show("Member already exists.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
              return;
            }
            updateGroupMembership(node.id(), node.name(), node.description(), node.userIds(), nextServices);
          }
          dialog.close();
          Notification.show("Member added.", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
        });
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Cancel", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private List<MemberCandidate> availableMemberCandidates(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    Set<String> existingHumans = lowerCaseSet(node.userIds());
    Set<String> existingServices = lowerCaseSet(node.serviceIds());
    List<MemberCandidate> candidates = new ArrayList<>();

    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> entry : currentUsers().entrySet()) {
      String id = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user = entry.getValue();
      if (id == null && user != null) {
        id = trimToNull(user.id());
      }
      if (id == null || existingHumans.contains(id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      String label =
          "Human - "
              + userDisplayName(id, user)
              + " ("
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.email()), id)
              + ")";
      candidates.add(new MemberCandidate(id, label, MemberKind.HUMAN));
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> entry : currentServices().entrySet()) {
      String id = trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService service = entry.getValue();
      if (id == null && service != null) {
        id = trimToNull(service.id());
      }
      if (id == null || existingServices.contains(id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      String label =
          "Service - "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(service == null ? null : service.displayName()), id)
              + " ("
              + id
              + ")";
      candidates.add(new MemberCandidate(id, label, MemberKind.SERVICE));
    }
    candidates.sort(Comparator.comparing(MemberCandidate::label, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(candidates);
  }

  private void updateGroupMembership(
      String nodeId, String groupName, String description, List<String> humanUsers, List<String> serviceUsers) {
    if (nodeId == null || workingModel == null) {
      return;
    }
    DefinitionPlatform next =
        treeAdapter.applyGroupEdits(
            workingModel,
            nodeId,
            new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.GroupUpdate(
                groupName, description, normalizeIds(humanUsers), normalizeIds(serviceUsers)));
    applyWorkingMutation(next, nodeId, true);
  }

  private void applyWorkingMutation(
      DefinitionPlatform nextModel, String preferredSelectionId, boolean markDirty) {
    if (nextModel == null) {
      return;
    }
    workingModel = nextModel;
    snapshot = treeAdapter.snapshot(workingModel);
    if (markDirty) {
      if (!editorMode.isEditMode()) {
        editorMode.enterEditMode();
      }
      editorMode.markDirty();
    }
    String selected = selectExistingNodeId(preferredSelectionId);
    browserShell.setRoots(snapshot.roots());
    browserShell.setSelectedNodeId(selected);
    syncTreeSelectionAndDetails();
  }

  private String selectExistingNodeId(String preferredSelectionId) {
    String preferred = trimToNull(preferredSelectionId);
    if (preferred != null && snapshot.byId().containsKey(preferred)) {
      return preferred;
    }
    String current = trimToNull(browserShell.selectedNodeId());
    if (current != null && snapshot.byId().containsKey(current)) {
      return current;
    }
    return snapshot.roots().isEmpty() ? null : snapshot.roots().get(0).id();
  }

  private void openManageOrganizationDialog(String initialTab, String preferredNodeId) {
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Manage Organization");
    dialog.setWidth("900px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("8vh");

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addClassName("stitch-groups-manage-tabs");
    tabs.addTab("create-ou", "CREATE OU", buildCreateOuTab(dialog, preferredNodeId));
    tabs.addTab("create-group", "CREATE GROUP", buildCreateGroupTab(dialog, preferredNodeId));
    tabs.addTab("rename", "RENAME", buildRenameTab(dialog, preferredNodeId));
    tabs.addTab("delete", "DELETE", buildDeleteTab(dialog, preferredNodeId));
    tabs.selectTab(Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(initialTab), "create-ou"));

    dialog.addToBody(tabs);
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("Close", dialog::close);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private Component buildCreateOuTab(StitchDialog dialog, String preferredNodeId) {
    List<NodeOption> ous = ouNodeOptions();
    ComboBox<NodeOption> parentOu = nodeOptionCombo("Parent OU", ous);
    parentOu.setValue(defaultParentOu(ous, preferredNodeId));

    TextField name = new TextField("OU Name");
    name.setWidthFull();
    TextArea description = new TextArea("Description (optional)");
    description.setWidthFull();
    description.setMinHeight("5.2rem");

    Button create = new Button("CREATE OU");
    create.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(create);
    create.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          NodeOption parent = parentOu.getValue();
          String ouName = trimToNull(name.getValue());
          if (parent == null || ouName == null || workingModel == null) {
            Notification.show("Parent OU and name are required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            DefinitionPlatform next =
                treeAdapter.createOu(workingModel, parent.id(), ouName, trimToNull(description.getValue()));
            applyWorkingMutation(next, parent.id(), true);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Created OU " + ouName, 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to create OU", error.getMessage());
          }
        });
    return manageTabLayout(name, parentOu, description, actionRow(create));
  }

  private Component buildCreateGroupTab(StitchDialog dialog, String preferredNodeId) {
    List<NodeOption> ous = ouNodeOptions();
    ComboBox<NodeOption> parentOu = nodeOptionCombo("Parent OU", ous);
    parentOu.setValue(defaultParentOu(ous, preferredNodeId));

    TextField name = new TextField("Group Name");
    name.setWidthFull();
    TextField type = new TextField("Group Type (optional)");
    type.setWidthFull();
    TextArea description = new TextArea("Description (optional)");
    description.setWidthFull();
    description.setMinHeight("5.2rem");

    Button create = new Button("CREATE GROUP");
    create.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(create);
    create.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          NodeOption parent = parentOu.getValue();
          String groupName = trimToNull(name.getValue());
          if (parent == null || groupName == null || workingModel == null) {
            Notification.show("Parent OU and name are required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            DefinitionPlatform next =
                treeAdapter.createGroup(
                    workingModel,
                    parent.id(),
                    groupName,
                    trimToNull(type.getValue()),
                    trimToNull(description.getValue()));
            applyWorkingMutation(next, parent.id(), true);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Created group " + groupName, 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to create group", error.getMessage());
          }
        });
    return manageTabLayout(name, parentOu, type, description, actionRow(create));
  }

  private Component buildRenameTab(StitchDialog dialog, String preferredNodeId) {
    List<NodeOption> nodeOptions = allNodeOptions(true);
    ComboBox<NodeOption> target = nodeOptionCombo("Target", nodeOptions);
    target.setValue(defaultNodeOption(nodeOptions, preferredNodeId));

    TextField name = new TextField("Name");
    name.setWidthFull();
    TextArea description = new TextArea("Description");
    description.setWidthFull();
    description.setMinHeight("5.2rem");

    Runnable sync = () -> {
      NodeOption option = target.getValue();
      StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node = option == null ? null : snapshot.byId().get(option.id());
      if (node == null) {
        name.clear();
        description.clear();
        return;
      }
      name.setValue(valueOrEmpty(node.name()));
      description.setValue(valueOrEmpty(node.description()));
    };
    target.addValueChangeListener(event -> sync.run());
    sync.run();

    Button apply = new Button("APPLY");
    apply.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(apply);
    apply.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          NodeOption selected = target.getValue();
          String newName = trimToNull(name.getValue());
          if (selected == null || newName == null || workingModel == null) {
            Notification.show("Target and name are required.", 1600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            DefinitionPlatform next =
                treeAdapter.renameNode(
                    workingModel, selected.id(), newName, trimToNull(description.getValue()));
            applyWorkingMutation(next, selected.id(), true);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Updated " + newName, 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to rename", error.getMessage());
          }
        });

    return manageTabLayout(target, name, description, actionRow(apply));
  }

  private Component buildDeleteTab(StitchDialog dialog, String preferredNodeId) {
    List<NodeOption> nodeOptions = allNodeOptions(false);
    ComboBox<NodeOption> target = nodeOptionCombo("Target", nodeOptions);
    target.setValue(defaultNodeOption(nodeOptions, preferredNodeId));

    Div impact = new Div();
    impact.addClassName("stitch-groups-delete-impact");
    Checkbox confirm = new Checkbox("I understand this action cannot be undone.");
    Button delete = new Button("DELETE");
    delete.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyDanger(delete);
    delete.setEnabled(false);
    confirm.addValueChangeListener(event -> delete.setEnabled(Boolean.TRUE.equals(event.getValue())));

    Runnable refreshImpact = () -> {
      NodeOption option = target.getValue();
      StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node = option == null ? null : snapshot.byId().get(option.id());
      if (node == null) {
        impact.setText("Select a target to view impact.");
      } else if (node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.GROUP) {
        impact.setText(
            "This group contains " + node.userIds().size() + " human and " + node.serviceIds().size() + " service members.");
      } else {
        impact.setText(
            "This OU subtree contains " + node.groupCountInSubtree() + " groups and " + node.principalCountInSubtree() + " members.");
      }
    };
    target.addValueChangeListener(event -> refreshImpact.run());
    refreshImpact.run();

    delete.addClickListener(
        event -> {
          NodeOption selected = target.getValue();
          if (selected == null || workingModel == null) {
            Notification.show("Select a target to delete.", 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
            return;
          }
          try {
            DefinitionPlatform next = treeAdapter.deleteNode(workingModel, selected.id());
            applyWorkingMutation(next, treeAdapter.parentOuNodeId(selected.id()), true);
            dialog.close();
            Notification.show("Deleted " + selected.label(), 1500, Position.BOTTOM_START);
          } catch (Exception error) {
            StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to delete", error.getMessage());
          }
        });

    return manageTabLayout(target, impact, confirm, actionRow(delete));
  }

  private ComboBox<NodeOption> nodeOptionCombo(String label, List<NodeOption> options) {
    ComboBox<NodeOption> combo = new ComboBox<>(label);
    combo.setWidthFull();
    combo.setItems(options);
    combo.setItemLabelGenerator(NodeOption::label);
    combo.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    return combo;
  }

  private List<NodeOption> ouNodeOptions() {
    List<NodeOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node : snapshot.byId().values()) {
      if (node == null || node.kind() != StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU) {
        continue;
      }
      options.add(new NodeOption(node.id(), valueOrDash(node.pathLabel())));
    }
    options.sort(Comparator.comparing(NodeOption::label, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private List<NodeOption> allNodeOptions(boolean includeRoot) {
    List<NodeOption> options = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node : snapshot.byId().values()) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!includeRoot && node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU && "ou:".equals(node.id())) {
        continue;
      }
      String prefix = node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU ? "OU - " : "GROUP - ";
      options.add(new NodeOption(node.id(), prefix + valueOrDash(node.pathLabel())));
    }
    options.sort(Comparator.comparing(NodeOption::label, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER));
    return List.copyOf(options);
  }

  private NodeOption defaultParentOu(List<NodeOption> options, String preferredNodeId) {
    if (options.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    String preferred = trimToNull(preferredNodeId);
    if (preferred != null) {
      StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node = snapshot.byId().get(preferred);
      String parentOuId =
          node == null
              ? "ou:"
              : node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU
                  ? node.id()
                  : treeAdapter.parentOuNodeId(node.id());
      for (NodeOption option : options) {
        if (option.id().equals(parentOuId)) {
          return option;
        }
      }
    }
    return options.get(0);
  }

  private NodeOption defaultNodeOption(List<NodeOption> options, String preferredNodeId) {
    if (options.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    String preferred = trimToNull(preferredNodeId);
    if (preferred != null) {
      for (NodeOption option : options) {
        if (option.id().equals(preferred)) {
          return option;
        }
      }
    }
    return options.get(0);
  }

  private static VerticalLayout manageTabLayout(Component... components) {
    VerticalLayout layout = new VerticalLayout();
    layout.setPadding(false);
    layout.setSpacing(false);
    layout.setWidthFull();
    layout.getStyle().set("gap", "0.72rem");
    layout.addClassName("stitch-groups-manage-tab");
    if (components != null) {
      layout.add(components);
    }
    return layout;
  }

  private static HorizontalLayout actionRow(Component... components) {
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.setJustifyContentMode(JustifyContentMode.END);
    row.addClassName("stitch-groups-manage-actions");
    if (components != null) {
      row.add(components);
    }
    return row;
  }

  private boolean saveChanges() {
    if (workingModel == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      provider.savePlatformModel(workingModel);
      loadedModel = treeAdapter.deepCopy(workingModel);
      workingModel = treeAdapter.deepCopy(workingModel);
      snapshot = treeAdapter.snapshot(workingModel);
      editorMode.clear();
      if (browserShell.selectedNodeId() == null
          || !snapshot.byId().containsKey(browserShell.selectedNodeId())) {
        browserShell.setSelectedNodeId(null);
      }
      browserShell.setRoots(snapshot.roots());
      syncTreeSelectionAndDetails();
      toastUpdated(workingModel.envelope());
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo(
          "Unable to update platform model",
          error.getMessage() == null ? "Save failed." : error.getMessage());
      return false;
    }
  }

  private void discardChanges() {
    if (loadedModel == null) {
      return;
    }
    workingModel = treeAdapter.deepCopy(loadedModel);
    snapshot = treeAdapter.snapshot(workingModel);
    editorMode.clear();
    if (browserShell.selectedNodeId() == null
        || !snapshot.byId().containsKey(browserShell.selectedNodeId())) {
      browserShell.setSelectedNodeId(null);
    }
    browserShell.setRoots(snapshot.roots());
    syncTreeSelectionAndDetails();
    Notification.show("Discarded unsaved changes", 1700, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private void applyOuDraft(String nodeId, StitchGroupsOuEditor.OuDraft draft) {
    if (!editorMode.isEditMode() || nodeId == null || workingModel == null) {
      return;
    }
    workingModel =
        treeAdapter.applyOuEdits(
            workingModel,
            nodeId,
            new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.OuUpdate(draft.name(), draft.description()));
    editorMode.markDirty();
  }

  private void applyGroupDraft(String nodeId, StitchGroupsGroupEditor.GroupDraft draft) {
    if (!editorMode.isEditMode() || nodeId == null || workingModel == null) {
      return;
    }
    workingModel =
        treeAdapter.applyGroupEdits(
            workingModel,
            nodeId,
            new StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.GroupUpdate(
                draft.name(), draft.description(), draft.humanUsers(), draft.serviceUsers()));
    editorMode.markDirty();
  }

  private Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser> currentUsers() {
    if (workingModel == null || workingModel.users() == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    return workingModel.users();
  }

  private Map<String, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformService> currentServices() {
    if (workingModel == null || workingModel.services() == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    return workingModel.services();
  }

  private String treeLabel(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String display = trimToNull(node.displayName());
    if (display != null) {
      return display;
    }
    String name = trimToNull(node.name());
    if (name != null) {
      return name;
    }
    String nodeName = trimToNull(node.nodeName());
    return nodeName == null ? "node" : nodeName;
  }

  private String treeLabelClass(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU
        ? "stitch-groups-tree-label--ou"
        : "stitch-groups-tree-label--group";
  }

  private Component treeDecorator(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Span count = new Span();
    count.addClassName("stitch-groups-tree-count");
    if (node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU) {
      count.setText(String.valueOf(node.groupCountInSubtree()));
      count
          .getElement()
          .setAttribute(
              "title",
              node.groupCountInSubtree()
                  + " groups, "
                  + node.principalCountInSubtree()
                  + " members in subtree");
    } else {
      count.setText(String.valueOf(node.userIds().size() + node.serviceIds().size()));
      count
          .getElement()
          .setAttribute(
              "title",
              node.userIds().size() + " human members, " + node.serviceIds().size() + " service members");
    }
    return count;
  }

  private Component treeIcon(StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType =
        node == null || node.kind() == StitchGroupsTreeAdapter.NodeKind.OU
            ? VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O
            : VaadinIcon.USERS;
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private Button iconAction(VaadinIcon icon, String ariaLabel, Runnable action) {
    Button button = new Button(icon.create(), event -> action.run());
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY_INLINE, ButtonVariant.LUMO_ICON, ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    button.addClassName("stitch-groups-tree-action");
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    return button;
  }

  private String userDisplayName(String userId, DefinitionPlatform.PlatformUser user) {
    String first = trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.firstName());
    String last = trimToNull(user == null ? null : user.lastName());
    if (first != null && last != null) {
      return first + " " + last;
    }
    if (first != null) {
      return first;
    }
    if (last != null) {
      return last;
    }
    return valueOrDash(userId);
  }

  private static Set<String> lowerCaseSet(List<String> values) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (values == null) {
      return normalized;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        normalized.add(trimmed.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeIds(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String trimmed = trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed != null) {
        normalized.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static boolean addDistinctIgnoreCase(List<String> values, String value) {
    String normalized = trimToNull(value);
    if (values == null || normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String existing : values) {
      if (existing != null && existing.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    values.add(normalized);
    return true;
  }

  private static String valueOrDash(String value) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(trimToNull(value), "-");
  }

  private static String valueOrEmpty(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value;
  }

  private void toastUpdated(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    String updated = envelope == null ? null : trimToNull(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    String uuid = envelope == null ? null : trimToNull(envelope.uuid());
    String message;
    if (updated == null && uuid == null) {
      message = "Updated platform model";
    } else if (updated != null && uuid != null) {
      message = "Updated platform model (" + updated + " | " + uuid + ")";
    } else {
      message = "Updated platform model (" + (updated == null ? uuid : updated) + ")";
    }
    Notification.show(message, 2600, Position.BOTTOM_START);
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  private enum MemberKind {
    HUMAN,
    SERVICE
  }

  private record MemberCandidate(String id, String label, MemberKind kind) {}

  private record NodeOption(String id, String label) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.platform;

import java.util.Objects;

public final class StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "Groups";
      this.routePath = "admin/security/groups";
      this.pageTitle = "Groups - Security";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Edit platform organizational units, groups, and memberships.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder merge(Builder overrides) {
      if (overrides == null) {
        return this;
      }
      this.label = Objects.requireNonNullElse(overrides.label, this.label);
      this.routePath = Objects.requireNonNullElse(overrides.routePath, this.routePath);
      this.pageTitle = Objects.requireNonNullElse(overrides.pageTitle, this.pageTitle);
      this.pageSubtitle = Objects.requireNonNullElse(overrides.pageSubtitle, this.pageSubtitle);
      this.order = overrides.order;
      this.enabled = overrides.enabled;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchPlatformGroupsScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusColumn.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.util.Locale;

public record StitchStatusColumn(String key, String label) {
  public StitchStatusColumn {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("key is required");
    }
    key = key.trim();
    label = (label == null || label.isBlank()) ? toDisplayLabel(key) : label.trim();
  }

  private static String toDisplayLabel(String key) {
    String normalized = key.replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').replace('.', ' ').trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + normalized.substring(1);
  }
}

import java.util.List;

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusDataProviders.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.StatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.data.DataStatusRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.data.DataStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusRow;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;

@Component
public class StitchStatusDataProviders {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchStatusDataProvider appsProvider;
  private final StitchStatusDataProvider servicesProvider;
  private final StitchStatusDataProvider dataProvider;

  public StitchStatusDataProviders(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.appsProvider =
        new SimpleProvider(
            StitchStatusFeature.APPS,
            this::loadAppsRows,
            Map.of(
                "instance", "Instance",
                "host", "Host",
                "type", "Type",
                "uptime", "Uptime",
                "runtimeType", "Runtime",
                "state", "Raw State",
                "pid", "PID",
                "user", "User"));
    this.servicesProvider =
        new SimpleProvider(
            StitchStatusFeature.SERVICES,
            this::loadServicesRows,
            Map.of(
                "instance", "Instance",
                "host", "Host",
                "runtime", "Runtime",
                "cpu", "CPU",
                "heap", "Heap",
                "uptime", "Uptime",
                "state", "Raw State",
                "pid", "PID",
                "user", "User"));
    this.dataProvider =
        new SimpleProvider(
            StitchStatusFeature.DATA,
            this::loadDataRows,
            Map.of(
                "instance", "Instance",
                "type", "Type",
                "datasetId", "Dataset",
                "producerId", "Resource Id",
                "host", "Host",
                "message", "Message",
                "state", "Raw State"));
  }

  public StitchStatusDataProvider provider(String sourceId) {
    String normalized = sourceId == null ? "" : sourceId.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case StitchStatusFeature.APPS -> appsProvider;
      case StitchStatusFeature.SERVICES -> servicesProvider;
      case StitchStatusFeature.DATA -> dataProvider;
      default -> throw new IllegalStateException("Unknown status source: " + sourceId);
    };
  }

  private List<StitchStatusRow> loadAppsRows() {
    SessionImpl session = session();
    StatusCache statusCache = session.internal().statusCache();
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    List<DefinitionStatusApp> snapshot = collectAppStatusDefinitions(statusCache);
    Map<String, DefinitionStatusApp> latestByApp = latestAppStatusByLogicalKey(snapshot);
    Map<String, DefinitionApp> configuredApps = configuredAppsByLogicalKey(discoveryCache);

    List<StitchStatusRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> consumed = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionApp> entry : configuredApps.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (key.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      consumed.add(key);
      DefinitionApp definition = entry.getValue();
      DefinitionStatusApp status = latestByApp.get(key);
      if (status != null) {
        rows.add(toAppRow(status, definition, now));
        continue;
      }
      StitchStatusRow noStatus = toNoStatusAppRow(definition);
      if (noStatus != null) {
        rows.add(noStatus);
      }
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, DefinitionStatusApp> entry : latestByApp.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (key.isBlank() || consumed.contains(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      DefinitionStatusApp status = entry.getValue();
      if (status == null) {
        continue;
      }
      rows.add(toAppRow(status, null, now));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static List<DefinitionStatusApp> collectAppStatusDefinitions(StatusCache statusCache) {
    List<DefinitionStatusApp> primaryStatusCache = new ArrayList<>();
    if (statusCache != null) {
      primaryStatusCache.addAll(safe(statusCache.listLatestStatusAppInstances()));
    }
    Map<StitchStatusSourceSelection.Identity, DefinitionStatusApp> primarySelected =
        StitchStatusSourceSelection.selectLatestByIdentity(
            primaryStatusCache,
            StitchStatusDataProviders::resolveAppGroup,
            StitchStatusDataProviders::resolveAppName,
            DefinitionStatusApp::instance,
            DefinitionStatusApp::lastHeartbeatEpochMs,
            DefinitionStatusApp::lastStartEpochMs,
            value -> StitchStatusSourceSelection.reflectiveEpoch(value, "lastStateChangeEpochMs"),
            value -> StitchStatusSourceSelection.reflectiveEpoch(value, "startedAtEpochMs"));
    return List.copyOf(primarySelected.values());
  }

  private static Map<String, DefinitionApp> configuredAppsByLogicalKey(DiscoveryCache discoveryCache) {
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    List<DefinitionApp> definitions = safe(discoveryCache.list(DefinitionApp.class));
    if (definitions.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, DefinitionApp> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DefinitionApp definition : definitions) {
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireDefinitionEnvelope(definition);
      String group = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.group(), "app.envelope.group");
      String name = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.name(), "app.envelope.name");
      selected.putIfAbsent(group + "::" + name, definition);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(selected);
  }

  private static Map<String, DefinitionStatusApp> latestAppStatusByLogicalKey(
      List<DefinitionStatusApp> statuses) {
    if (statuses == null || statuses.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, DefinitionStatusApp> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DefinitionStatusApp status : statuses) {
      String group = resolveAppGroup(status);
      String name = resolveAppName(status);
      String key = group + "::" + name;
      DefinitionStatusApp current = selected.get(key);
      if (current == null || isAppStatusNewer(status, current)) {
        selected.put(key, status);
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(selected);
  }

  private static boolean isAppStatusNewer(DefinitionStatusApp left, DefinitionStatusApp right) {
    long leftHeartbeat = normalizeEpoch(left == null ? null : left.lastHeartbeatEpochMs());
    long rightHeartbeat = normalizeEpoch(right == null ? null : right.lastHeartbeatEpochMs());
    if (leftHeartbeat != rightHeartbeat) {
      return leftHeartbeat > rightHeartbeat;
    }
    long leftStart = normalizeEpoch(left == null ? null : left.lastStartEpochMs());
    long rightStart = normalizeEpoch(right == null ? null : right.lastStartEpochMs());
    if (leftStart != rightStart) {
      return leftStart > rightStart;
    }
    long leftState =
        normalizeEpoch(
            left == null
                ? null
                : StitchStatusSourceSelection.reflectiveEpoch(left, "lastStateChangeEpochMs"));
    long rightState =
        normalizeEpoch(
            right == null
                ? null
                : StitchStatusSourceSelection.reflectiveEpoch(right, "lastStateChangeEpochMs"));
    return leftState > rightState;
  }

  private StitchStatusRow toAppRow(DefinitionStatusApp status, DefinitionApp definition, long now) {
    String group = resolveAppGroup(status, definition);
    String name = resolveAppName(status, definition);
    String instance = normalize(status == null ? null : status.instance());
    Map<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("instance", instance);
    fields.put("host", firstNonBlank(normalize(status == null ? null : status.host()), resolveDefinitionHost(definition)));
    fields.put(
        "runtimeType",
        firstNonBlank(
            status == null || status.runtimeType() == null ? "" : status.runtimeType().name(),
            normalize(definition == null ? null : definition.sessionType())));
    fields.put(
        "type",
        firstNonBlank(
            normalize(status == null ? null : status.appType()),
            normalize(definition == null ? null : definition.appType()),
            normalize(fields.get("runtimeType") == null ? null : fields.get("runtimeType").toString())));
    fields.put("state", status == null || status.state() == null ? "" : status.state().name());
    fields.put(
        "pid",
        firstNonBlank(
            normalize(tag(status == null ? null : status.tags(), "pid")),
            normalize(tag(status == null ? null : status.tags(), "processId"))));
    fields.put(
        "user",
        firstNonBlank(
            normalize(tag(status == null ? null : status.tags(), "user")),
            normalize(tag(status == null ? null : status.tags(), "username"))));
    fields.put("uptime", formatUptime(resolveUptimeMillis(status, now)));

    return new StitchStatusRow(
        joinId("app", group, name, instance),
        normalizeAppBand(status, now),
        group,
        name,
        toInstant(status == null ? null : status.lastHeartbeatEpochMs()),
        fields,
        status);
  }

  private StitchStatusRow toNoStatusAppRow(DefinitionApp definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireDefinitionEnvelope(definition);
    String group = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.group(), "app.envelope.group");
    String name = Strings.requireNonBlank(envelope.name(), "app.envelope.name");
    String instance = resolveDefinitionInstance(definition);
    Map<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    fields.put("instance", instance);
    fields.put("host", resolveDefinitionHost(definition));
    fields.put("runtimeType", normalize(definition.sessionType()));
    fields.put(
        "type",
        firstNonBlank(normalize(definition.appType()), normalize(definition.sessionType())));
    fields.put("state", "NO STATUS");
    fields.put("pid", "");
    fields.put("user", "");
    fields.put("uptime", "-");
    return new StitchStatusRow(
        joinId("app", group, name, instance),
        "NO STATUS",
        group,
        name,
        toInstantUtc(envelope),
        fields,
        definition);
  }

  private static String resolveAppName(DefinitionStatusApp status, DefinitionApp definition) {
    if (status != null) {
      return Strings.requireNonBlank(
          requireStatusEnvelope(status).name(), "status.app.envelope.name");
    }
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(
        definition == null || definition.envelope() == null ? null : definition.envelope().name(),
        "app.envelope.name");
  }

  private static String resolveAppName(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
    return resolveAppName(status, null);
  }

  private static String resolveAppGroup(DefinitionStatusApp status, DefinitionApp definition) {
    if (status != null) {
      return Strings.requireNonBlank(
          requireStatusEnvelope(status).group(), "status.app.envelope.group");
    }
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(
        definition == null || definition.envelope() == null ? null : definition.envelope().group(),
        "app.envelope.group");
  }

  private static String resolveAppGroup(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
    return resolveAppGroup(status, null);
  }

  private static String resolveDefinitionHost(DefinitionApp definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.instances() == null || definition.instances().instance1() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return normalize(definition.instances().instance1().host());
  }

  private static String resolveDefinitionInstance(DefinitionApp definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.instances() == null || definition.instances().instance1() == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return "instance1";
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope requireDefinitionEnvelope(DefinitionApp definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("app.envelope is required");
    }
    return definition.envelope();
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope requireStatusEnvelope(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
    if (status == null || status.envelope() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("status.app.envelope is required");
    }
    return status.envelope();
  }

  private static Instant toInstantUtc(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String updated = normalize(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    if (!updated.isBlank()) {
      try {
        return Instant.parse(updated);
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
    String created = normalize(envelope.createdTimeUtc());
    if (!created.isBlank()) {
      try {
        return Instant.parse(created);
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Long resolveUptimeMillis(DefinitionStatusApp status, long nowMs) {
    if (status == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (status.metrics() != null
        && status.metrics().process() != null
        && status.metrics().process().uptimeMs() != null
        && status.metrics().process().uptimeMs() > 0L) {
      return status.metrics().process().uptimeMs();
    }
    Long lastStart = status.lastStartEpochMs();
    if (lastStart != null && lastStart > 0L && nowMs > lastStart) {
      return nowMs - lastStart;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String formatUptime(Long uptimeMs) {
    if (uptimeMs == null || uptimeMs <= 0L) {
      return "-";
    }
    return StitchStatusTimeFormat.formatDurationMillis(uptimeMs);
  }

  private static <T> List<T> safe(List<T> values) {
    return values == null ? List.of() : values;
  }

  private static List<ServiceStatusRow> latestServiceRows(List<ServiceStatusRow> rows) {
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, ServiceStatusRow> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (ServiceStatusRow row : rows) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = normalize(row.group());
      String name = normalize(row.name());
      if (group.isBlank() || name.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = group + "::" + name;
      ServiceStatusRow current = selected.get(key);
      if (current == null || isServiceRowNewer(row, current)) {
        selected.put(key, row);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(selected.values());
  }

  private static boolean isServiceRowNewer(ServiceStatusRow left, ServiceStatusRow right) {
    long leftHeartbeat = toEpochMillis(left == null ? null : left.lastHeartbeatUtc());
    long rightHeartbeat = toEpochMillis(right == null ? null : right.lastHeartbeatUtc());
    if (leftHeartbeat != rightHeartbeat) {
      return leftHeartbeat > rightHeartbeat;
    }
    long leftSeen = toEpochMillis(left == null ? null : left.lastSeenUtc());
    long rightSeen = toEpochMillis(right == null ? null : right.lastSeenUtc());
    return leftSeen > rightSeen;
  }

  private static List<DataStatusRow> latestDataRows(List<DataStatusRow> rows) {
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, DataStatusRow> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DataStatusRow row : rows) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = normalize(row.group());
      String name = normalize(row.name());
      if (group.isBlank() || name.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = group + "::" + name;
      DataStatusRow current = selected.get(key);
      if (current == null || isDataRowNewer(row, current)) {
        selected.put(key, row);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(selected.values());
  }

  private static boolean isDataRowNewer(DataStatusRow left, DataStatusRow right) {
    long leftHeartbeat = toEpochMillis(left == null ? null : left.lastHeartbeatUtc());
    long rightHeartbeat = toEpochMillis(right == null ? null : right.lastHeartbeatUtc());
    if (leftHeartbeat != rightHeartbeat) {
      return leftHeartbeat > rightHeartbeat;
    }
    long leftSeen = toEpochMillis(left == null ? null : left.lastSeenUtc());
    long rightSeen = toEpochMillis(right == null ? null : right.lastSeenUtc());
    return leftSeen > rightSeen;
  }

  private static long toEpochMillis(Instant value) {
    return value == null ? Long.MIN_VALUE : value.toEpochMilli();
  }

  private static long normalizeEpoch(Long value) {
    return value == null || value <= 0L ? Long.MIN_VALUE : value;
  }

  private List<StitchStatusRow> loadServicesRows() {
    ServiceStatusCache serviceStatusCache = session().internal().serviceStatusCache();
    if (serviceStatusCache == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ServiceStatusRow> snapshot = latestServiceRows(serviceStatusCache.snapshot());
    if (snapshot == null || snapshot.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchStatusRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (ServiceStatusRow row : snapshot) {
      if (row == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String group = normalize(row.group());
      String name = normalize(row.name());
      String instance = normalize(row.instanceName());
      Map<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      fields.put("instance", instance);
      fields.put("host", normalize(row.host()));
      fields.put("runtime", normalize(row.runtime()));
      fields.put("cpu", normalize(row.cpu()));
      fields.put("heap", normalize(row.heap()));
      fields.put("uptime", normalize(row.uptime()));
      fields.put("state", normalize(row.state()));
      fields.put("pid", normalize(row.pid()));
      fields.put("user", normalize(row.user()));

      rows.add(
          new StitchStatusRow(
              joinId("service", group, name, instance),
              normalizeStateBand(row.state()),
              group,
              name,
              row.lastHeartbeatUtc() == null ? row.lastSeenUtc() : row.lastHeartbeatUtc(),
              fields,
              row));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private List<StitchStatusRow> loadDataRows() {
    SessionImpl session = session();
    List<StitchStatusRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();

    DataStatusCache dataStatusCache = session.internal().dataStatusCache();
    List<DataStatusRow> dataSnapshot =
        dataStatusCache == null ? List.of() : latestDataRows(dataStatusCache.snapshot());
    if (!dataSnapshot.isEmpty()) {
      for (DataStatusRow row : dataSnapshot) {
        if (row == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String group = normalize(row.group());
        String name = normalize(row.name());
        String instance = normalize(row.instanceName());
        Map<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        fields.put("instance", instance);
        fields.put("type", normalize(row.producerType()));
        fields.put("datasetId", normalize(row.datasetId()));
        fields.put("producerId", normalize(row.producerId()));
        fields.put("host", normalize(row.host()));
        fields.put("message", normalize(row.message()));
        fields.put("state", normalize(row.state()));
        rows.add(
            new StitchStatusRow(
                joinId("data", group, name, instance),
                normalizeStateBand(row.state()),
                group,
                name,
                row.lastHeartbeatUtc() == null ? row.lastSeenUtc() : row.lastHeartbeatUtc(),
                fields,
                row));
      }
    }

    ServiceStatusCache serviceStatusCache = session.internal().serviceStatusCache();
    if (serviceStatusCache != null) {
      Map<ServiceKey, String> datasetsByService = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      List<DefinitionStatusService> definitions = serviceStatusCache.snapshotDefinitions();
      if (definitions != null) {
        for (DefinitionStatusService definition : definitions) {
          if (definition == null || definition.tags() == null) {
            continue;
          }
          String datasetIds = normalize(definition.tags().get("datasetIds"));
          if (datasetIds.isBlank()) {
            continue;
          }
          ServiceKey key = ServiceKey.of(definition.group(), definition.name(), definition.instance());
          if (key != null) {
            datasetsByService.put(key, datasetIds);
          }
        }
      }
      List<ServiceStatusRow> snapshot = latestServiceRows(serviceStatusCache.snapshot());
      if (snapshot != null) {
        for (ServiceStatusRow row : snapshot) {
          if (row == null) {
            continue;
          }
          ServiceKey key = ServiceKey.of(row.group(), row.name(), row.instanceName());
          if (key == null) {
            continue;
          }
          String datasetIds = datasetsByService.get(key);
          if (datasetIds == null) {
            continue;
          }
          String group = normalize(row.group());
          String name = "service/" + normalize(row.name());
          String instance = normalize(row.instanceName());
          Map<String, Object> fields = new LinkedHashMap<>();
          fields.put("instance", instance);
          fields.put("type", "SERVICE");
          fields.put("datasetId", datasetIds);
          fields.put("producerId", "service:" + group + "/" + normalize(row.name()));
          fields.put("host", normalize(row.host()));
          fields.put("message", "serving datasets");
          fields.put("state", normalize(row.state()));
          rows.add(
              new StitchStatusRow(
                  joinId("data-service", group, name, instance),
                  normalizeStateBand(row.state()),
                  group,
                  name,
                  row.lastHeartbeatUtc() == null ? row.lastSeenUtc() : row.lastHeartbeatUtc(),
                  fields,
                  row));
        }
      }
    }

    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private SessionImpl session() {
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (current instanceof SessionImpl resolved) {
      return resolved;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
  }

  private static String normalizeAppBand(DefinitionStatusApp status, long nowMs) {
    String fallback =
        normalizeStateBand(status == null || status.state() == null ? null : status.state().name());
    if (status == null) {
      return fallback;
    }
    if (!isOnlineState(status.state() == null ? null : status.state().name())) {
      return fallback;
    }
    Long heartbeat = status.lastHeartbeatEpochMs();
    if (heartbeat == null || heartbeat <= 0L) {
      return "ONLINE";
    }
    long timeoutSeconds =
        Math.max(15L, status.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds() == null ? 0L : status.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds());
    long cutoff = nowMs - (timeoutSeconds * 1000L);
    if (heartbeat < cutoff) {
      return "STALE";
    }
    return "ONLINE";
  }

  private static boolean isOnlineState(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return normalized.equals("ONLINE")
        || normalized.equals("RUNNING")
        || normalized.equals("STARTED")
        || normalized.equals("READY")
        || normalized.equals("CONNECTED")
        || normalized.equals("SUCCESS")
        || normalized.equals("ENABLED");
  }

  private static String normalizeStateBand(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    if (normalized.equals("ONLINE")
        || normalized.equals("RUNNING")
        || normalized.equals("STARTED")
        || normalized.equals("READY")
        || normalized.equals("CONNECTED")
        || normalized.equals("SUCCESS")
        || normalized.equals("ENABLED")) {
      return "ONLINE";
    }
    if (normalized.equals("STALE")
        || normalized.equals("DEGRADED")
        || normalized.equals("WARNING")
        || normalized.equals("WARN")
        || normalized.equals("PARTIAL")
        || normalized.equals("PENDING")) {
      return "STALE";
    }
    if (normalized.equals("UNKNOWN") || normalized.equals("UNAVAILABLE")) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    if (normalized.equals("OFFLINE")
        || normalized.equals("STOPPED")
        || normalized.equals("DISCONNECTED")
        || normalized.equals("DISABLED")
        || normalized.equals("DOWN")) {
      return "OFFLINE";
    }
    if (normalized.equals("ERROR") || normalized.equals("FAILED")) {
      return "ERROR";
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static Instant toInstant(Long epochMs) {
    if (epochMs == null || epochMs <= 0L) {
      return null;
    }
    return Instant.ofEpochMilli(epochMs);
  }

  private static String tag(Map<String, String> tags, String key) {
    if (tags == null || key == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String value = tags.get(key);
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim();
  }

  private static String joinId(String prefix, String group, String name, String instance) {
    return String.join(
        "::",
        normalize(prefix),
        normalize(group),
        normalize(name),
        normalize(instance));
  }

  private static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return "";
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      String normalized = normalize(value);
      if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
        return normalized;
      }
    }
    return "";
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  private record ServiceKey(String group, String name, String instance) {
    private static ServiceKey of(String group, String name, String instance) {
      String g = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      String n = Strings.trimToNull(name);
      String i = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
      if (g == null || n == null || i == null) {
        return null;
      }
      return new ServiceKey(g, n, i);
    }
  }

  private record SimpleProvider(
      String id, Supplier<List<StitchStatusRow>> loader, Map<String, String> labels)
      implements StitchStatusDataProvider {
    private SimpleProvider {
      Objects.requireNonNull(id, "id");
      Objects.requireNonNull(loader, "loader");
      labels = labels == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(labels);
    }

    @Override
    public List<StitchStatusRow> loadRows() {
      List<StitchStatusRow> rows = loader.get();
      return rows == null ? List.of() : rows;
    }

    @Override
    public Map<String, String> fieldLabels() {
      return labels;
    }
  }
}
