===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusDetailsDialog.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;

public class StitchStatusDetailsDialog extends StitchDialog {
  public StitchStatusDetailsDialog(
      StitchStatusScreenConfig config, StitchStatusRow row, Map<String, String> providerLabels) {
    super("Details");
    Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    Objects.requireNonNull(row, "row");

    String target = StitchDetailsDialogSupport.joinPath(row.group(), row.name());
    setDialogTitle("Details - " + target);

    Map<String, String> labels = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    labels.put("status", "Status");
    labels.put("group", "Group");
    labels.put("name", "Name");
    labels.put("timestamp", "Last Seen");
    for (StitchStatusColumn column : config.additionalColumns()) {
      labels.put(column.key(), column.label());
    }
    if (providerLabels != null) {
      labels.putAll(providerLabels);
    }
    if (!config.summaryFields().isEmpty()) {
      labels.put("summary", StitchDetailsDialogSupport.defaultSummaryLabel(config.summaryLabel()));
    }

    Map<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("status", StitchDetailsDialogSupport.trimToEmpty(row.field("status")));
    values.put("group", StitchDetailsDialogSupport.trimToEmpty(row.group()));
    values.put("name", StitchDetailsDialogSupport.trimToEmpty(row.name()));
    values.put("timestamp", row.field("timestamp"));
    values.putAll(row.flattenedFields());
    if (!config.summaryFields().isEmpty()) {
      values.put("summary", summarize(row, config.summaryFields()));
    }

    addToBody(StitchDetailsDialogSupport.buildForm(orderedKeys(config, values), values, labels));
    withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> row.sourceObject() == null ? row : row.sourceObject());
    addSecondaryAction("Close", this::close);
  }

  private static List<String> orderedKeys(StitchStatusScreenConfig config, Map<String, String> values) {
    List<String> defaults = new java.util.ArrayList<>();
    defaults.add("status");
    defaults.add("group");
    defaults.add("name");
    for (StitchStatusColumn column : config.additionalColumns()) {
      defaults.add(column.key());
    }
    if (!config.summaryFields().isEmpty()) {
      defaults.add("summary");
    }
    defaults.add("timestamp");
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.orderedKeys(config.detailFields(), defaults, values);
  }

  private static String summarize(StitchStatusRow row, List<String> keys) {
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.summarize(keys, row::field);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusFeature.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.StitchFeatureSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuEntry;

public final class StitchStatusFeature implements StitchFeatureSet {
  public static final String FEATURE_ID = "status";
  public static final String APPS = "apps";
  public static final String SERVICES = "services";
  public static final String DATA = "data";
  public static final String ENTRY_APPS = "status.apps";
  public static final String ENTRY_SERVICES = "status.services";
  public static final String ENTRY_DATA = "status.data";

  private final String menuLabel;
  private final int order;
  private final Map<String, StitchStatusScreenConfig> screens;

  private StitchStatusFeature(Builder builder) {
    this.menuLabel = require(builder.menuLabel, "menuLabel");
    this.order = builder.order;
    Map<String, StitchStatusScreenConfig> configured = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    configured.put(APPS, defaultApps(builder.appsOverrides.build()));
    configured.put(SERVICES, defaultServices(builder.servicesOverrides.build()));
    configured.put(DATA, defaultData(builder.dataOverrides.build()));
    this.screens = Map.copyOf(configured);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String id() {
    return FEATURE_ID;
  }

  @Override
  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public String menuLabel() {
    return menuLabel;
  }

  public List<StitchStatusScreenConfig> screens() {
    List<StitchStatusScreenConfig> values = new ArrayList<>(screens.values());
    values.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(StitchStatusScreenConfig::order)
            .thenComparing(config -> config.label().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    return List.copyOf(values);
  }

  public Optional<StitchStatusScreenConfig> screen(String id) {
    if (id == null || id.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(screens.get(id.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
  }

  @Override
  public List<StitchMenuEntry> menuEntries() {
    List<StitchMenuEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchStatusScreenConfig screen : screens()) {
      if (!screen.enabled()) {
        continue;
      }
      entries.add(
          StitchMenuEntry.builder(entryIdForScreen(screen.id()))
              .withLabel(screen.label())
              .withRoutePath(screen.routePath())
              .withOrder(screen.order())
              .build());
    }
    return List.copyOf(entries);
  }

  private static String entryIdForScreen(String screenId) {
    if (APPS.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId)) {
      return ENTRY_APPS;
    }
    if (SERVICES.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId)) {
      return ENTRY_SERVICES;
    }
    if (DATA.equalsIgnoreCase(screenId)) {
      return ENTRY_DATA;
    }
    return FEATURE_ID + "." + screenId;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static StitchStatusScreenConfig defaultApps(ScreenOverrides overrides) {
    return baseConfig(
        APPS,
        "Apps",
        "status/apps",
        "Status Apps",
        "Application runtime status",
        10,
        false,
        List.of(
            new StitchStatusColumn("host", "Host"),
            new StitchStatusColumn("pid", "PID"),
            new StitchStatusColumn("uptime", "Uptime")),
        "Summary",
        List.of("host", "instance", "uptime"),
        List.of(
            "status",
            "group",
            "name",
            "instance",
            "host",
            "type",
            "uptime",
            "runtimeType",
            "state",
            "pid",
            "user"),
        overrides);
  }

  private static StitchStatusScreenConfig defaultServices(ScreenOverrides overrides) {
    return baseConfig(
        SERVICES,
        "Services",
        "status/services",
        "Status Services",
        "Service runtime status",
        20,
        true,
        List.of(
            new StitchStatusColumn("host", "Host"),
            new StitchStatusColumn("runtime", "Runtime")),
        "Resources",
        List.of("cpu", "heap", "uptime"),
        List.of(
            "status",
            "group",
            "name",
            "instance",
            "host",
            "runtime",
            "cpu",
            "heap",
            "uptime",
            "state",
            "pid",
            "user",
            "timestamp"),
        overrides);
  }

  private static StitchStatusScreenConfig defaultData(ScreenOverrides overrides) {
    return baseConfig(
        DATA,
        "Data",
        "status/data",
        "Status Data",
        "Data producer and service resource status",
        30,
        true,
        List.of(
            new StitchStatusColumn("type", "Type"),
            new StitchStatusColumn("datasetId", "Dataset")),
        "Summary",
        List.of("producerId", "host", "message"),
        List.of(
            "status",
            "group",
            "name",
            "instance",
            "type",
            "datasetId",
            "producerId",
            "host",
            "message",
            "state",
            "timestamp"),
        overrides);
  }

  private static StitchStatusScreenConfig baseConfig(
      String id,
      String label,
      String routePath,
      String pageTitle,
      String pageSubtitle,
      int order,
      boolean timestampVisible,
      List<StitchStatusColumn> defaultAdditionalColumns,
      String summaryLabel,
      List<String> defaultSummaryFields,
      List<String> defaultDetailFields,
      ScreenOverrides overrides) {
    int resolvedOrder = overrides != null && overrides.orderOverride() != null ? overrides.orderOverride() : order;
    List<StitchStatusColumn> mergedAdditional =
        mergeAdditionalColumns(defaultAdditionalColumns, overrides == null ? null : overrides.additionalFields());
    List<String> mergedSummary =
        mergeSummaryFields(defaultSummaryFields, overrides == null ? null : overrides.summaryFieldsOverride());
    List<String> mergedDetail = mergeDetailFields(defaultDetailFields, mergedAdditional);

    return StitchStatusScreenConfig.builder(id)
        .withLabel(label)
        .withRoutePath(routePath)
        .withPageTitle(pageTitle)
        .withPageSubtitle(pageSubtitle)
        .withOrder(resolvedOrder)
        .withTimestampVisible(timestampVisible)
        .withAdditionalColumns(mergedAdditional)
        .withSummaryLabel(summaryLabel)
        .withSummaryFields(mergedSummary)
        .withDetailFields(mergedDetail)
        .build();
  }

  private static List<StitchStatusColumn> mergeAdditionalColumns(
      List<StitchStatusColumn> defaults, List<String> extraFields) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, StitchStatusColumn> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (defaults != null) {
      for (StitchStatusColumn column : defaults) {
        if (column == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = normalizeFieldKey(column.key());
        if (isReservedLeadingField(key) || key.isBlank()) {
          continue;
        }
        merged.putIfAbsent(key, new StitchStatusColumn(key, column.label()));
      }
    }
    if (extraFields != null) {
      for (String field : extraFields) {
        String key = normalizeFieldKey(field);
        if (isReservedLeadingField(key) || key.isBlank()) {
          continue;
        }
        merged.putIfAbsent(key, new StitchStatusColumn(key, null));
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(merged.values());
  }

  private static List<String> mergeSummaryFields(List<String> defaults, List<String> override) {
    if (override != null) {
      return normalizeFieldKeys(override);
    }
    return normalizeFieldKeys(defaults);
  }

  private static List<String> mergeDetailFields(
      List<String> defaults, List<StitchStatusColumn> additionalColumns) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> merged = new LinkedHashSet<>(normalizeFieldKeys(defaults));
    if (additionalColumns != null) {
      for (StitchStatusColumn column : additionalColumns) {
        if (column != null) {
          String key = normalizeFieldKey(column.key());
          if (!key.isBlank()) {
            merged.add(key);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(merged);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeFieldKeys(List<String> keys) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = normalizeFieldKey(key);
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeFieldKey(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static boolean isReservedLeadingField(String key) {
    return switch (normalizeFieldKey(key).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case "status", "group", "name", "instance", "timestamp", "summary", "actions" -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String menuLabel = "Status";
    private int order = 10;
    private final ScreenOverridesBuilder appsOverrides = new ScreenOverridesBuilder();
    private final ScreenOverridesBuilder servicesOverrides = new ScreenOverridesBuilder();
    private final ScreenOverridesBuilder dataOverrides = new ScreenOverridesBuilder();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMenuLabel(String value) {
      this.menuLabel = require(value, "menuLabel");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder apps(Consumer<ScreenOverridesBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(appsOverrides);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder services(Consumer<ScreenOverridesBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(servicesOverrides);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder data(Consumer<ScreenOverridesBuilder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(dataOverrides);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchStatusFeature build() {
      return new StitchStatusFeature(this);
    }
  }

  private record ScreenOverrides(
      List<String> additionalFields, List<String> summaryFieldsOverride, Integer orderOverride) {}

  public static final class ScreenOverridesBuilder {
    private final List<String> additionalFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<String> summaryFieldsOverride = new ArrayList<>();
    private boolean summaryOverrideSet;
    private Integer orderOverride;

    public ScreenOverridesBuilder addFields(String... fields) {
      if (fields == null) {
        return this;
      }
      for (String field : fields) {
        String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(field);
        if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
          additionalFields.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public ScreenOverridesBuilder withSummaryFields(String... fields) {
      summaryOverrideSet = true;
      summaryFieldsOverride.clear();
      if (fields != null) {
        for (String field : fields) {
          String normalized = normalizeFieldKey(field);
          if (!normalized.isBlank()) {
            summaryFieldsOverride.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public ScreenOverridesBuilder withOrder(int value) {
      this.orderOverride = value;
      return this;
    }

    private ScreenOverrides build() {
      List<String> normalizedAdditional = normalizeFieldKeys(additionalFields);
      List<String> normalizedSummary =
          summaryOverrideSet ? normalizeFieldKeys(summaryFieldsOverride) : null;
      return new ScreenOverrides(normalizedAdditional, normalizedSummary, orderOverride);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusRow.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record StitchStatusRow(
    String id,
    String status,
    String group,
    String name,
    Instant timestampUtc,
    Map<String, Object> fields,
    Object sourceObject) {

  public StitchStatusRow {
    id = normalize(id);
    status = normalize(status);
    group = normalize(group);
    name = normalize(name);
    fields = fields == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(fields);
  }

  public String field(String key) {
    if (key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    String normalizedKey = key.trim();
    return switch (normalizedKey.toLowerCase()) {
      case "status" -> StitchStatusSort.displayStatus(status);
      case "group" -> group;
      case "name" -> name;
      case "timestamp", "timestamputc", "lastupdated", "updated" ->
          StitchStatusTimeFormat.formatElapsedSince(timestampUtc);
      case "uptime" -> onlineStatus() ? normalize(stringValue(resolveFieldValue(normalizedKey))) : "";
      default -> normalize(stringValue(resolveFieldValue(normalizedKey)));
    };
  }

  public Map<String, String> detailFields() {
    Map<String, String> values = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    values.put("status", StitchStatusSort.displayStatus(status));
    values.put("group", group);
    values.put("name", name);
    values.put("timestamp", field("timestamp"));
    values.putAll(flattenedFields());
    return Map.copyOf(values);
  }

  public Map<String, String> flattenedFields() {
    Map<String, String> flattened = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Object> entry : fields.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalize(entry.getKey());
      if (key.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      flattenValue(key, entry.getValue(), flattened);
    }
    if (!onlineStatus()) {
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : flattened.entrySet()) {
        if ("uptime".equalsIgnoreCase(entry.getKey())) {
          entry.setValue("");
        }
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(flattened);
  }

  private boolean onlineStatus() {
    return "ONLINE".equalsIgnoreCase(StitchStatusSort.normalizeStatus(status));
  }

  private Object resolveFieldValue(String key) {
    Object direct = findInMap(fields, key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    if (!key.contains(".")) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] path = key.split("\\.");
    if (path.length == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    Object current = findInMap(fields, path[0]);
    if (current == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (int i = 1; i < path.length; i++) {
      current = resolvePathSegment(current, path[i]);
      if (current == null) {
        return null;
      }
    }
    return current;
  }

  private static Object resolvePathSegment(Object current, String segment) {
    if (current instanceof Map<?, ?> values) {
      return findInMap(values, segment);
    }
    if (current == null || segment == null || segment.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }

    Class<?> type = current.getClass();
    if (type.isRecord()) {
      try {
        for (java.lang.reflect.RecordComponent component : type.getRecordComponents()) {
          if (component.getName().equalsIgnoreCase(segment)) {
            java.lang.reflect.Method accessor = component.getAccessor();
            accessor.setAccessible(true);
            return accessor.invoke(current);
          }
        }
      } catch (ReflectiveOperationException ignored) {
      }
    }

    String suffix = Character.toUpperCase(segment.charAt(0)) + segment.substring(1);
    for (String methodName : new String[] {"get" + suffix, "is" + suffix}) {
      try {
        java.lang.reflect.Method method = type.getMethod(methodName);
        method.setAccessible(true);
        return method.invoke(current);
      } catch (ReflectiveOperationException ignored) {
      }
    }

    Class<?> cursor = type;
    while (cursor != null && cursor != Object.class) {
      for (java.lang.reflect.Field field : cursor.getDeclaredFields()) {
        if (field.getName().equalsIgnoreCase(segment)) {
          try {
            field.setAccessible(true);
            return field.get(current);
          } catch (IllegalAccessException ignored) {
            return null;
          }
        }
      }
      cursor = cursor.getSuperclass();
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static Object findInMap(Map<?, ?> map, String key) {
    if (map == null || key == null || key.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    Object direct = map.get(key);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String normalizedKey = key.trim();
    for (Map.Entry<?, ?> entry : map.entrySet()) {
      if (!(entry.getKey() instanceof String candidate)) {
        continue;
      }
      if (candidate.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedKey)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static void flattenValue(String path, Object value, Map<String, String> target) {
    if (value instanceof Map<?, ?> nestedMap) {
      for (Map.Entry<?, ?> nestedEntry : nestedMap.entrySet()) {
        if (!(nestedEntry.getKey() instanceof String nestedKey)) {
          continue;
        }
        String nextPath = path + "." + nestedKey.trim();
        flattenValue(nextPath, nestedEntry.getValue(), target);
      }
      return;
    }
    target.put(path, normalize(stringValue(value)));
  }

  private static String stringValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    return String.valueOf(value);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGridColumn;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchRowActions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchDetailsDialogSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchGroupedResultsPage;

public class StitchStatusScreen extends StitchGroupedResultsPage<StitchStatusRow> {
  private final StitchStatusScreenConfig config;
  private final StitchStatusDataProvider provider;

  public StitchStatusScreen(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchStatusScreenConfig config,
      StitchStatusDataProvider provider) {
    super(
        runtimeContext,
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Type to filter results...",
        "Search status rows");
    this.config = config;
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    initializeResultsScreen("No status rows", "No matching status rows were found.", "Refresh status rows");
  }

  @Override
  protected void configureGrid(StitchGrid<StitchStatusRow> grid) {
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.component("Status", this::statusBadge)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.STATUS)
            .key("status")
            .autoWidth(false)
            .width("8.25rem")
            .resizable(true)
            .flexGrow(0));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Group", StitchStatusRow::group)
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.GROUP)
            .key("group"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.text("Name", StitchStatusRow::name).kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.NAME).key("name"));
    grid.addColumn(
        StitchGridColumn.<StitchStatusRow>text("Instance", row -> row.field("instance"))
            .key("instance")
            .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));

    for (StitchStatusColumn column : filteredAdditionalColumns()) {
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<StitchStatusRow>text(column.label(), row -> row.field(column.key()))
              .key(column.key())
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    }

    if (!config.summaryFields().isEmpty()) {
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<StitchStatusRow>text(
                  summaryLabel(), row -> summarize(row, config.summaryFields()))
              .key("summary")
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP));
    }

    if (config.timestampVisible()) {
      Grid.Column<StitchStatusRow> lastSeenColumn =
          grid.addColumn(
              StitchGridColumn.<StitchStatusRow>text("Last Seen", row -> row.field("timestamp"))
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.TIMESTAMP)
              .key("timestamp"));
      lastSeenColumn.setComparator(
          row -> row == null || row.timestampUtc() == null ? Long.MIN_VALUE : row.timestampUtc().toEpochMilli());
    }

    if (grid.getColumnByKey("status-actions") == null) {
      StitchRowActions<StitchStatusRow> rowActions = new StitchRowActions<>();
      rowActions.addAction(
          StitchRowActions.Action.icon(
              VaadinIcon.INFO_CIRCLE_O,
              "Details",
              row -> new StitchStatusDetailsDialog(config, row, provider.fieldLabels()).open()));
      rowActions.addColumn(grid).setKey("status-actions");
    }
  }

  @Override
  protected List<StitchStatusRow> loadRows() {
    return provider.loadRows();
  }

  @Override
  protected Comparator<StitchStatusRow> rowComparator() {
    return StitchStatusSort.defaultComparator();
  }

  @Override
  protected String groupValue(StitchStatusRow row) {
    return row == null ? null : row.group();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean matchesSearch(StitchStatusRow row, String query) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (contains(row.field("status"), query) || contains(row.group(), query) || contains(row.name(), query)) {
      return true;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : row.flattenedFields().entrySet()) {
      if (contains(entry.getValue(), query)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private StitchStatusBadge statusBadge(StitchStatusRow row) {
    String text = StitchStatusSort.displayStatus(row == null ? null : row.status());
    return new StitchStatusBadge(text, StitchStatusBadge.toneForValue(text));
  }

  private List<StitchStatusColumn> filteredAdditionalColumns() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> seen = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    List<StitchStatusColumn> filtered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchStatusColumn column : config.additionalColumns()) {
      if (column == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = normalizeFieldKey(column.key());
      if (key.isBlank() || isStandardLeadingColumn(key) || !seen.add(key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      filtered.add(new StitchStatusColumn(key, column.label()));
    }
    return List.copyOf(filtered);
  }

  private static boolean isStandardLeadingColumn(String key) {
    return switch (normalizeFieldKey(key).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
      case "status", "group", "name", "instance" -> true;
      default -> false;
    };
  }

  private static String normalizeFieldKey(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private String summarize(StitchStatusRow row, List<String> keys) {
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = normalize(row == null ? null : row.field(key));
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        values.add(value);
      }
    }
    return String.join(" | ", values);
  }

  private String summaryLabel() {
    return StitchDetailsDialogSupport.defaultSummaryLabel(config.summaryLabel());
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

public final class StitchStatusScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final List<StitchStatusColumn> additionalColumns;
  private final String summaryLabel;
  private final List<String> summaryFields;
  private final List<String> detailFields;
  private final boolean timestampVisible;

  private StitchStatusScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.additionalColumns = List.copyOf(builder.additionalColumns);
    this.summaryLabel = optional(builder.summaryLabel);
    this.summaryFields = List.copyOf(builder.summaryFields);
    this.detailFields = List.copyOf(builder.detailFields);
    this.timestampVisible = builder.timestampVisible;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public List<StitchStatusColumn> additionalColumns() {
    return additionalColumns;
  }

  public String summaryLabel() {
    return summaryLabel;
  }

  public List<String> summaryFields() {
    return summaryFields;
  }

  public List<String> detailFields() {
    return detailFields;
  }

  public boolean timestampVisible() {
    return timestampVisible;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;
    private final List<StitchStatusColumn> additionalColumns = new ArrayList<>();
    private String summaryLabel;
    private final List<String> summaryFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private final List<String> detailFields = new ArrayList<>();
    private boolean timestampVisible = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = toDisplay(id);
      this.routePath = "status/" + this.id.toLowerCase();
      this.pageTitle = "Status " + this.label;
      this.pageSubtitle = "Status view for " + this.label;
      this.summaryLabel = "Summary";
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAdditionalColumns(List<StitchStatusColumn> columns) {
      additionalColumns.clear();
      if (columns != null) {
        additionalColumns.addAll(columns.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList());
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addColumn(String key, String label) {
      additionalColumns.add(new StitchStatusColumn(key, label));
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryLabel(String value) {
      summaryLabel = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSummaryFields(List<String> keys) {
      summaryFields.clear();
      if (keys != null) {
        for (String key : keys) {
          String normalized = optional(key);
          if (normalized != null) {
            summaryFields.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDetailFields(List<String> keys) {
      detailFields.clear();
      if (keys != null) {
        for (String key : keys) {
          String normalized = optional(key);
          if (normalized != null) {
            detailFields.add(normalized);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTimestampVisible(boolean value) {
      this.timestampVisible = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder customize(Consumer<Builder> customizer) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(customizer, "customizer").accept(this);
      return this;
    }

    public StitchStatusScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchStatusScreenConfig(this);
    }

    private static String toDisplay(String value) {
      String normalized = value.replace('-', ' ').replace('_', ' ').trim();
      if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
        return value;
      }
      return Character.toUpperCase(normalized.charAt(0)) + normalized.substring(1);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusServicesView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

@Route(value = "status/services", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStatusServicesView extends StitchStatusView {

      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, Stitch stitch, StitchStatusDataProviders providers) {

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusSort.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Locale;

public final class StitchStatusSort {
  private StitchStatusSort() {}

  public static Comparator<StitchStatusRow> defaultComparator() {
    return Comparator.comparingInt((StitchStatusRow row) -> rank(row == null ? null : row.status()))
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.group()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.name()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
        .thenComparing(row -> normalize(row == null ? null : row.id()), String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
  }

  public static int rank(String value) {
    String normalized = normalizeStatus(value);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "ONLINE" -> 0;
      case "STALE" -> 1;
      case "OFFLINE", "ERROR" -> 2;
      case "UNKNOWN", "NO STATUS" -> 3;
      default -> 9;
    };
  }

  public static String displayStatus(String value) {
    return normalizeStatus(value);
  }

  public static String normalizeStatus(String value) {
    String normalized = normalize(value).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return "";
    }
    return value.trim();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusSourceSelection.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.lang.reflect.Method;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Shared selection utility for status sources keyed by group/name/instance identity. */
public final class StitchStatusSourceSelection {
  private StitchStatusSourceSelection() {}

  public static <T> Map<Identity, T> selectLatestByIdentity(
      Collection<T> values,
      Function<T, String> groupFn,
      Function<T, String> nameFn,
      Function<T, String> instanceFn,
      Function<T, Long> heartbeatFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStartFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStateChangeFn,
      Function<T, Long> startedAtFn) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(groupFn, "groupFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(nameFn, "nameFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(instanceFn, "instanceFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(heartbeatFn, "heartbeatFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(lastStartFn, "lastStartFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(lastStateChangeFn, "lastStateChangeFn");
    Objects.requireNonNull(startedAtFn, "startedAtFn");

    Map<Identity, T> selected = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }

    for (T value : values) {
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Identity identity = Identity.of(groupFn.apply(value), nameFn.apply(value), instanceFn.apply(value));
      if (identity == null) {
        continue;
      }
      T current = selected.get(identity);
      if (current == null
          || compareRecency(value, current, heartbeatFn, lastStartFn, lastStateChangeFn, startedAtFn) > 0) {
        selected.put(identity, value);
      }
    }
    return Map.copyOf(selected);
  }

  public static <T> Map<Identity, T> selectPreferredByIdentity(
      Collection<T> primaryValues,
      Collection<T> fallbackValues,
      Function<T, String> groupFn,
      Function<T, String> nameFn,
      Function<T, String> instanceFn,
      Function<T, Long> heartbeatFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStartFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStateChangeFn,
      Function<T, Long> startedAtFn) {
    Map<Identity, T> primary =
        selectLatestByIdentity(
            primaryValues,
            groupFn,
            nameFn,
            instanceFn,
            heartbeatFn,
            lastStartFn,
            lastStateChangeFn,
            startedAtFn);

    Map<Identity, T> fallback =
        selectLatestByIdentity(
            fallbackValues,
            groupFn,
            nameFn,
            instanceFn,
            heartbeatFn,
            lastStartFn,
            lastStateChangeFn,
            startedAtFn);

    if (fallback.isEmpty()) {
      return primary;
    }
    if (primary.isEmpty()) {
      return fallback;
    }

    Map<Identity, T> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>(primary);
    for (Map.Entry<Identity, T> entry : fallback.entrySet()) {
      merged.putIfAbsent(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
    }
    return Map.copyOf(merged);
  }

  public static Long reflectiveEpoch(Object source, String methodName) {
    if (source == null || methodName == null || methodName.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      Method method = source.getClass().getMethod(methodName.trim());
      Object value = method.invoke(source);
      if (value instanceof Number number) {
        long epoch = number.longValue();
        return epoch > 0L ? epoch : null;
      }
      if (value instanceof String text) {
        String trimmed = text.trim();
        if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
          long epoch = Long.parseLong(trimmed);
          return epoch > 0L ? epoch : null;
        }
      }
    } catch (ReflectiveOperationException | NumberFormatException ignored) {
      return null;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static <T> int compareRecency(
      T left,
      T right,
      Function<T, Long> heartbeatFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStartFn,
      Function<T, Long> lastStateChangeFn,
      Function<T, Long> startedAtFn) {
    int heartbeatCompare = compareNullableLong(heartbeatFn.apply(left), heartbeatFn.apply(right));
    if (heartbeatCompare != 0) {
      return heartbeatCompare;
    }
    int lastStartCompare = compareNullableLong(lastStartFn.apply(left), lastStartFn.apply(right));
    if (lastStartCompare != 0) {
      return lastStartCompare;
    }
    int stateChangeCompare =
        compareNullableLong(lastStateChangeFn.apply(left), lastStateChangeFn.apply(right));
    if (stateChangeCompare != 0) {
      return stateChangeCompare;
    }
    return compareNullableLong(startedAtFn.apply(left), startedAtFn.apply(right));
  }

  private static int compareNullableLong(Long left, Long right) {
    long l = left == null ? Long.MIN_VALUE : left;
    long r = right == null ? Long.MIN_VALUE : right;
    return Long.compare(l, r);
  }

  public record Identity(String group, String name, String instance) {
    public static Identity of(String group, String name, String instance) {
      String normalizedGroup = normalize(group);
      String normalizedName = normalize(name);
      if (normalizedGroup.isBlank() || normalizedName.isBlank()) {
        return null;
      }
      return new Identity(normalizedGroup, normalizedName, normalize(instance));
    }

    public String appKey() {
      return group + "::" + name;
    }
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusTimeFormat.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

final class StitchStatusTimeFormat {
  private StitchStatusTimeFormat() {}

  static String formatElapsedSince(Instant value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    long elapsedMs = Math.max(0L, Instant.now().toEpochMilli() - value.toEpochMilli());
    return formatDurationMillis(elapsedMs);
  }

  static String formatDurationMillis(Long durationMs) {
    if (durationMs == null || durationMs <= 0L) {
      return "< 1 min";
    }
    long totalMinutes = durationMs / 60_000L;
    if (totalMinutes <= 0L) {
      return "< 1 min";
    }
    long days = totalMinutes / (24 * 60);
    long remainder = totalMinutes % (24 * 60);
    long hours = remainder / 60;
    long minutes = remainder % 60;
    List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>(3);
    if (days > 0) {
      parts.add(days + (days == 1 ? " day" : " days"));
    }
    if (hours > 0) {
      parts.add(hours + (hours == 1 ? " hour" : " hours"));
    }
    if (minutes > 0) {
      parts.add(minutes + (minutes == 1 ? " min" : " mins"));
    }
    if (parts.isEmpty()) {
      return "< 1 min";
    }
    return String.join(", ", parts);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/status/StitchStatusView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.status;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

abstract class StitchStatusView extends StitchStatusScreen {
  protected StitchStatusView(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      Stitch stitch,
      StitchStatusDataProviders providers,
      String sourceId) {
    super(runtimeContext, requireConfig(stitch, sourceId), requireProvider(providers, sourceId));
  }

  private static StitchStatusScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch, String sourceId) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .status()
        .flatMap(feature -> feature.screen(sourceId))
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private static StitchStatusDataProvider requireProvider(
      StitchStatusDataProviders providers, String sourceId) {
    return providers.provider(sourceId);
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/storage/StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.sql.ResultSet;
import java.sql.ResultSetMetaData;
import java.sql.Statement;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3.S3Connection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3.S3ObjectContent;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3.S3ObjectMetadata;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3.S3ObjectSummary;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.s3.S3ReadObjectRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.DuckdbEngine;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.DuckdbSession;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;

public final class StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider {
  private static final String DEFAULT_CONNECTION = "s3-fabric";
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final long PREVIEW_BYTES = 256L * 1024L;
  private static final int PARQUET_QUERY_LIMIT = 1200;

  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter keyAdapter = new StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter();

  public StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
  }

  public List<String> listConnections() {
    LinkedHashSet<String> names = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (ConnectionRef ref : listConnectionRefs()) {
      if (ref != null && ref.name() != null) {
        names.add(ref.name());
      }
    }
    return names.stream().sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER).toList();
  }

  public TreeModel loadTree(String connectionName) {
    String resolvedConnection = resolvedConnectionName(connectionName);
    try (S3Connection connection = openConnection(resolvedConnection)) {
      List<S3ObjectSummary> listedObjects = connection.listObjects("", true);
      List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
      LinkedHashMap<String, ObjectSummary> objectsByKey = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (S3ObjectSummary object : listedObjects) {
        if (object == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String relative = toRelative(object.key(), connection.basePrefix());
        if (relative == null || relative.isBlank() || relative.endsWith("/")) {
          continue;
        }
        String normalized = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(relative);
        if (normalized == null) {
          continue;
        }
        keys.add(normalized);
        objectsByKey.put(
            normalized,
            new ObjectSummary(
                normalized,
                Math.max(0L, object.sizeBytes()),
                iso(object.lastModified()),
                trimToEmpty(object.eTag()),
                trimToEmpty(object.storageClass())));
      }

      StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.Model model = keyAdapter.build(keys);
      return new TreeModel(
          resolvedConnection,
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucket()),
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucketUri()),
          model.roots(),
          model.byId(),
          Map.copyOf(objectsByKey));
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to load S3 browser tree for "
              + resolvedConnection
              + ": "
              + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error),
          error);
    }
  }

  public ObjectDetails loadObjectDetails(String connectionName, String objectKey) {
    String resolvedConnection = resolvedConnectionName(connectionName);
    String key = requireObjectKey(objectKey);
    try (S3Connection connection = openConnection(resolvedConnection)) {
      S3ObjectMetadata metadata = connection.admin().headObject(key);
      long fullSize = Math.max(0L, metadata.sizeBytes());
      boolean parquetPayload = isParquetObject(key, metadata.contentType());
      long readBytes = parquetPayload ? 0L : Math.min(fullSize, PREVIEW_BYTES);
      boolean truncated = !parquetPayload && readBytes < fullSize;

      byte[] bytes = new byte[0];
      if (!parquetPayload && fullSize > 0L) {
        S3ReadObjectRequest.Builder read = S3ReadObjectRequest.builder().withKey(key);
        if (truncated && readBytes > 0L) {
          read.withRange(0L, readBytes - 1L);
        }
        S3ObjectContent content = connection.admin().readObject(read.build());
        bytes = content == null ? new byte[0] : content.bytes();
      }

      boolean textPayload = !parquetPayload && isTextType(metadata.contentType());
      String encoding = parquetPayload ? "none" : (textPayload ? "text" : "base64");
      String preview =
          parquetPayload
              ? ""
              : (textPayload
                  ? new String(bytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8)
                  : Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(bytes));

      return new ObjectDetails(
          resolvedConnection,
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucket()),
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucketUri()),
          key,
          fullSize,
          truncated,
          encoding,
          preview,
          trimToEmpty(metadata.contentType()),
          trimToEmpty(metadata.contentEncoding()),
          trimToEmpty(metadata.contentLanguage()),
          trimToEmpty(metadata.eTag()),
          iso(metadata.lastModified()),
          metadata.metadata() == null ? Map.of() : metadata.metadata());
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to load S3 object " + key + ": " + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error), error);
    }
  }

  public ParquetInspection inspectParquet(String connectionName, String objectKey) {
    String resolvedConnection = resolvedConnectionName(connectionName);
    String key = requireObjectKey(objectKey);
    try (S3Connection connection = openConnection(resolvedConnection);
        DuckdbEngine engine = new DuckdbEngine();
        DuckdbSession duckdb = engine.openSession()) {
      connection.admin().configureDuckdbSession(duckdb);

      String resolvedObjectKey = connection.admin().resolveKey(key);
      String objectUri = "s3://" + connection.bucket() + "/" + resolvedObjectKey;
      String escapedObjectUri = escapeSqlLiteral(objectUri);

      List<String> warnings = new ArrayList<>();
      QueryTable fileMetadata =
          queryDuckdbTable(
              duckdb,
              "select * from parquet_file_metadata('" + escapedObjectUri + "')",
              warnings,
              "file metadata");
      QueryTable metadata =
          queryDuckdbTable(
              duckdb,
              "select * from parquet_metadata('" + escapedObjectUri + "') limit " + PARQUET_QUERY_LIMIT,
              warnings,
              "metadata");
      QueryTable schema =
          queryDuckdbTable(
              duckdb,
              "select * from parquet_schema('" + escapedObjectUri + "') limit " + PARQUET_QUERY_LIMIT,
              warnings,
              "schema");

      String failure = "";
      if (metadata.rows().isEmpty() && schema.rows().isEmpty() && fileMetadata.rows().isEmpty()) {
        failure =
            warnings.isEmpty()
                ? "DuckDB did not return parquet metadata for this object."
                : "DuckDB parquet inspection failed: " + String.join("; ", warnings);
      }

      LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = parquetSummary(objectUri, fileMetadata, metadata, schema);
      return new ParquetInspection(
          resolvedConnection,
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucket()),
          trimToEmpty(connection.bucketUri()),
          key,
          objectUri,
          Map.copyOf(summary),
          metadata,
          schema,
          List.copyOf(warnings),
          failure);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to inspect parquet object " + key + ": " + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error),
          error);
    }
  }

  private List<ConnectionRef> listConnectionRefs() {
    LinkedHashMap<String, ConnectionRef> byName = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    String sessionGroup = Strings.trimToNull(session.context() == null ? null : session.context().getGroup());
    DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (cache != null) {
      addS3ConnectionsForGroup(cache, sessionGroup, byName, true);
      addS3ConnectionsForGroup(cache, PLATFORM_GROUP, byName, false);
    }
    if (byName.isEmpty()) {
      byName.put(
          DEFAULT_CONNECTION.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT),
          new ConnectionRef(PLATFORM_GROUP, DEFAULT_CONNECTION));
    }
    return byName.values().stream()
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(
                    (ConnectionRef ref) -> Strings.firstNonBlank(ref.group(), ""),
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(
                    ref -> Strings.firstNonBlank(ref.name(), ""),
                    String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  private S3Connection openConnection(String connectionName) {
    return session.connections().s3(resolvedConnectionName(connectionName));
  }

  private static void addS3ConnectionsForGroup(
      DiscoveryCache cache,
      String group,
      Map<String, ConnectionRef> byName,
      boolean replaceExisting) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    if (cache == null || normalizedGroup == null || byName == null) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionConnection definition : cache.list(DefinitionConnection.class, normalizedGroup)) {
      if (definition == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (definition.connectionType() != DefinitionConnection.ConnectionType.S3 && definition.s3() == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String name =
          Strings.trimToNull(definition.envelope() == null ? null : definition.envelope().name());
      if (name == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = name.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (replaceExisting || !byName.containsKey(key)) {
        byName.put(key, new ConnectionRef(normalizedGroup, name));
      }
    }
  }

  private static String resolvedConnectionName(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? DEFAULT_CONNECTION : normalized;
  }

  private static String requireObjectKey(String value) {
    String normalized = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Object key is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String toRelative(String key, String basePrefix) {
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalizedKey == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalizedBase = Strings.trimToNull(basePrefix);
    if (normalizedBase == null) {
      return normalizedKey;
    }
    if (normalizedKey.equals(normalizedBase)) {
      return "";
    }
    String prefixed = normalizedBase.endsWith("/") ? normalizedBase : normalizedBase + "/";
    if (normalizedKey.startsWith(prefixed)) {
      return normalizedKey.substring(prefixed.length());
    }
    return normalizedKey;
  }

  private static String trimToEmpty(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  private static String iso(Instant value) {
    return value == null ? "" : DateTimeFormatter.ISO_INSTANT.format(value);
  }

  private static boolean isTextType(String contentType) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(contentType);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.startsWith("text/")
        || lower.contains("json")
        || lower.contains("xml")
        || lower.contains("csv")
        || lower.contains("yaml")
        || lower.contains("javascript");
  }

  private static boolean isParquetObject(String key, String contentType) {
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalizedKey != null && normalizedKey.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).endsWith(".parquet")) {
      return true;
    }
    String normalizedType = Strings.trimToNull(contentType);
    return normalizedType != null && normalizedType.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("parquet");
  }

  private static QueryTable queryDuckdbTable(
      DuckdbSession session, String sql, List<String> warnings, String label) {
    try (Statement statement = session.createStatement();
        ResultSet resultSet = statement.executeQuery(sql)) {
      ResultSetMetaData metadata = resultSet.getMetaData();
      int columnCount = metadata.getColumnCount();
      List<String> columns = new ArrayList<>(columnCount);
      for (int index = 1; index <= columnCount; index++) {
        String name = Strings.trimToNull(metadata.getColumnLabel(index));
        columns.add(name == null ? "column_" + index : name);
      }

      List<Map<String, String>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
      while (resultSet.next()) {
        LinkedHashMap<String, String> row = new LinkedHashMap<>();
        for (int index = 1; index <= columnCount; index++) {
          row.put(columns.get(index - 1), stringify(resultSet.getObject(index)));
        }
        rows.add(Map.copyOf(row));
      }
      return new QueryTable(List.copyOf(columns), List.copyOf(rows));
    } catch (Exception error) {
      if (warnings != null) {
        warnings.add(
            Strings.firstNonBlank(label, "query")
                + ": "
                + StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error));
      }
      return QueryTable.empty();
    }
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, String> parquetSummary(
      String objectUri, QueryTable fileMetadata, QueryTable metadata, QueryTable schema) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Object URI", Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(objectUri), "-"));
    String rows = firstValue(fileMetadata, Set.of("num_rows", "rows", "row_count"), Set.of());
    if ("-".equals(rows)) {
      rows = rowCountFromMetadata(metadata);
    }
    summary.put("Rows", rows);

    String rowGroups = firstValue(fileMetadata, Set.of("num_row_groups", "row_groups"), Set.of());
    if ("-".equals(rowGroups)) {
      rowGroups = rowGroupCountFromMetadata(metadata);
    }
    summary.put("Row Groups", rowGroups);
    summary.put("Schema Fields", schemaFieldCount(schema));
    summary.put(
        "Format Version",
        firstValue(fileMetadata, Set.of("format_version", "version"), Set.of()));
    summary.put("Created By", firstValue(fileMetadata, Set.of("created_by"), Set.of()));
    summary.put("Compression", compressionSummary(metadata));
    return summary;
  }

  private static String rowCountFromMetadata(QueryTable metadata) {
    if (metadata == null || metadata.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, Long> rowsByGroup = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map<String, String> row : metadata.rows()) {
      String group = lookup(row, Set.of("row_group_id", "row_group"));
      String rowCount = lookup(row, Set.of("row_group_num_rows", "num_rows"));
      if (Strings.isBlank(group) || Strings.isBlank(rowCount)) {
        continue;
      }
      try {
        rowsByGroup.putIfAbsent(group, Long.parseLong(rowCount));
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
    if (rowsByGroup.isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    long total = 0L;
    for (Long value : rowsByGroup.values()) {
      if (value != null && value > 0) {
        total += value;
      }
    }
    return total <= 0 ? "-" : String.valueOf(total);
  }

  private static String rowGroupCountFromMetadata(QueryTable metadata) {
    if (metadata == null || metadata.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Map<String, String> row : metadata.rows()) {
      String group = lookup(row, Set.of("row_group_id", "row_group"));
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(group)) {
        groups.add(group);
      }
    }
    return groups.isEmpty() ? "-" : String.valueOf(groups.size());
  }

  private static String firstValue(
      QueryTable table, Set<String> preferredKeys, Set<String> fallbackKeys) {
    if (table == null || table.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    for (Map<String, String> row : table.rows()) {
      String value = lookup(row, preferredKeys);
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(value)) {
        return value;
      }
    }
    if (fallbackKeys != null && !fallbackKeys.isEmpty()) {
      for (Map<String, String> row : table.rows()) {
        String value = lookup(row, fallbackKeys);
        if (Strings.isNotBlank(value)) {
          return value;
        }
      }
    }
    return "-";
  }

  private static String schemaFieldCount(QueryTable schema) {
    if (schema == null || schema.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    int count = 0;
    for (Map<String, String> row : schema.rows()) {
      String name = lookup(row, Set.of("name", "column_name", "path"));
      if (Strings.isBlank(name) || "schema".equalsIgnoreCase(name) || "root".equalsIgnoreCase(name)) {
        continue;
      }
      count++;
    }
    return count <= 0 ? String.valueOf(schema.rows().size()) : String.valueOf(count);
  }

  private static String compressionSummary(QueryTable metadata) {
    if (metadata == null || metadata.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> values = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (Map<String, String> row : metadata.rows()) {
      String compression = lookup(row, Set.of("compression", "codec"));
      if (Strings.isNotBlank(compression)) {
        values.add(compression);
      }
    }
    if (values.isEmpty()) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (values.size() <= 3) {
      return String.join(", ", values);
    }
    List<String> sampled = values.stream().limit(3).toList();
    return String.join(", ", sampled) + " +" + (values.size() - sampled.size());
  }

  private static String lookup(Map<String, String> row, Set<String> keys) {
    if (row == null || row.isEmpty() || keys == null || keys.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : row.entrySet()) {
      String column = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      if (column == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String normalized = column.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (keys.contains(normalized)) {
        return Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String stringify(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String text = String.valueOf(value);
    if (text.length() <= 220) {
      return text;
    }
    return text.substring(0, 217) + "...";
  }

  private static String escapeSqlLiteral(String value) {
    return value.replace("'", "''");
  }

  public record ConnectionRef(String group, String name) {}

  public record TreeModel(
      String connectionName,
      String bucket,
      String bucketUri,
      List<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> roots,
      Map<String, StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> byId,
      Map<String, ObjectSummary> objectsByKey) {}

  public record ObjectSummary(
      String key, long sizeBytes, String lastModifiedIso, String eTag, String storageClass) {}

  public record ObjectDetails(
      String connectionName,
      String bucket,
      String bucketUri,
      String key,
      long sizeBytes,
      boolean truncated,
      String encoding,
      String preview,
      String contentType,
      String contentEncoding,
      String contentLanguage,
      String eTag,
      String lastModifiedIso,
      Map<String, String> metadata) {}

  public record QueryTable(List<String> columns, List<Map<String, String>> rows) {
    public QueryTable {
      columns = columns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columns);
      rows = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
    }

    public static QueryTable empty() {
      return new QueryTable(List.of(), List.of());
    }
  }

  public record ParquetInspection(
      String connectionName,
      String bucket,
      String bucketUri,
      String key,
      String objectUri,
      Map<String, String> summary,
      QueryTable metadataTable,
      QueryTable schemaTable,
      List<String> warnings,
      String failure) {
    public ParquetInspection {
      summary = summary == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(summary);
      metadataTable = metadataTable == null ? QueryTable.empty() : metadataTable;
      schemaTable = schemaTable == null ? QueryTable.empty() : schemaTable;
      warnings = warnings == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(warnings);
      failure = failure == null ? "" : failure;
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/storage/StitchStorageS3BrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.combobox.ComboBox;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.details.Details;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.GridVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Pre;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.Icon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
