import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;

@Route(value = "data/s3-browser", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStorageS3BrowserScreen extends StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen {
  private static final StitchEmptyState NO_SELECTION =
      new StitchEmptyState("No path selected", "Select a folder or object from the S3 path tree.");
  private static final StitchEmptyState EMPTY_BROWSER =
      new StitchEmptyState(
          "No objects found", "Select a connection and refresh to load available object keys.");
  private static final StitchEmptyState NO_CONNECTION =
      new StitchEmptyState("No S3 connection available", "No S3 connections were discovered.");

  private final StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider provider;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final ComboBox<String> connectionSelector = new ComboBox<>();
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRequested());

  private StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.TreeModel treeModel =
      new StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.TreeModel("", "", "", List.of(), Map.of(), Map.of());
  private final Map<String, StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails> detailCache = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<String, StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection> parquetCache =
      new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private String currentConnection;
  private boolean suppressConnectionEvents;

  public StitchStorageS3BrowserScreen(Stitch stitch, StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), provider);
  }

  private StitchStorageS3BrowserScreen(
      StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig config, StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        config.pageSubtitle() == null ? "" : config.pageSubtitle(),
        "Refresh S3 browser",
        "Refresh S3 browser",
        "Preview",
        "S3 object preview");
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");

    actions().removeAll();
    configureConnectionSelector();
    configureFiltersBar();
    configureInspectorPanel();
    addToBody(filtersBar);

    initBrowser(
        new BrowserConfig(
            "S3 Paths",
            "Object Inspector",
            NO_SELECTION,
            EMPTY_BROWSER,
            "Search paths",
            "Search S3 object paths",
            this::nodeIcon,
            this::nodeDecorator),
        new EditConfig(() -> false, this::saveNoOp, this::discardNoOp, node -> false),
        this::detailTitle,
        this::buildDetailContent,
        this::readOnlyActions,
        nodeId -> {});
    addClassName("stitch-s3-browser-screen");
    browserShell().layout().addClassName("stitch-tree-layout--s3");
    browserShell().treeNav().addClassName("stitch-tree-nav--s3");
    browserShell().layout().withAutoNavSizing(320, 640);
    loadConnections();
  }

  @Override
  protected void refreshRequested() {
    if (currentConnection == null) {
      loadConnections();
      return;
    }
    loadConnection(currentConnection, true);
  }

  private static StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::s3Browser)
        .filter(StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private void configureConnectionSelector() {
    connectionSelector.setLabel("Connection");
    connectionSelector.setPlaceholder("S3 Connection");
    connectionSelector.setWidth("clamp(18rem, 34vw, 30rem)");
    connectionSelector.setAllowCustomValue(false);
    connectionSelector.setClearButtonVisible(false);
    connectionSelector.addClassName("stitch-s3-connection-select");
    connectionSelector.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "S3 connection selector");
    connectionSelector.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressConnectionEvents) {
            requestConnectionChange(event.getValue());
          }
        });
  }

  private void configureFiltersBar() {
    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refreshAction);
    refreshAction.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh S3 browser");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh S3 browser");

    filtersBar.addClassName("stitch-s3-browser-filters");
    filtersBar.withFilter(connectionSelector).withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  private void configureInspectorPanel() {
    inspectorPanel().previewField().setMinHeight("20rem");
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewReadOnly(true);
    inspectorPanel().setPreviewAriaLabel("S3 object preview");
    inspectorPanel().addClassName("stitch-s3-object-inspector");
  }

  private void loadConnections() {
    List<String> connections = provider.listConnections();
    connectionSelector.setItems(connections);
    if (connections.isEmpty()) {
      currentConnection = null;
      clearTree(NO_CONNECTION, EMPTY_BROWSER);
      return;
    }
    String preferred =
        currentConnection != null && connections.contains(currentConnection)
            ? currentConnection
            : connections.get(0);
    setConnectionSelectorValue(preferred);
    loadConnection(preferred, false);
  }

  private void requestConnectionChange(String requestedConnection) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(requestedConnection);
    if (Objects.equals(currentConnection, resolved)) {
      return;
    }
    loadConnection(resolved, false);
  }

  private void loadConnection(String requestedConnection, boolean preserveSelection) {
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(requestedConnection);
    if (resolved == null) {
      currentConnection = null;
      clearTree(NO_CONNECTION, EMPTY_BROWSER);
      return;
    }
    String desiredSelection = preserveSelection ? browserShell().selectedNodeId() : null;
    try {
      treeModel = provider.loadTree(resolved);
      currentConnection = treeModel.connectionName();
      detailCache.clear();
      parquetCache.clear();
      setConnectionSelectorValue(currentConnection);

      applyTree(
          treeModel.roots(),
          treeModel.byId(),
          treeModel.roots().isEmpty() ? EMPTY_BROWSER : NO_SELECTION,
          EMPTY_BROWSER,
          desiredSelection,
          StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode::payloadNode);
      Notification.show(
          "Loaded " + treeModel.objectsByKey().size() + " object(s) from " + currentConnection,
          1800,
          Position.BOTTOM_START);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      currentConnection = resolved;
      setConnectionSelectorValue(resolved);
      clearTree(EMPTY_BROWSER, EMPTY_BROWSER);
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load S3 objects", rootMessage(error));
    }
  }

  private List<Component> readOnlyActions(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
    if (node != null && node.payloadNode()) {
      Button json =
          inspectorPanel().createJsonAction(() -> openJsonDialog(node), "Open selected object as JSON");
      actions.add(json);

      Button copy =
          inspectorPanel()
              .createCopyAction("Copied preview", "Nothing to copy", "Copy selected object preview");
      copy.setEnabled(hasPreview(node) && !isParquetKey(node.fullKey()));
      actions.add(copy);
    }

    Button close =
        inspectorPanel()
            .createCloseAction(() -> browserShell().applySelectionById(null), "Close object inspector");
    actions.add(close);
    return List.copyOf(actions);
  }

  private String detailTitle(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return "Object Inspector";
    }
    return node.payloadNode() ? "Object Details" : "Path Summary";
  }

  private Component buildDetailContent(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node, boolean editMode) {
    if (node == null) {
      return NO_SELECTION;
    }
    if (!node.payloadNode()) {
      return buildPrefixInspector(node);
    }
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details = resolveDetails(node.fullKey());
    if (details == null) {
      return new StitchEmptyState("Unable to load object", "Object details could not be loaded.");
    }
    if (isParquetObject(details)) {
      return buildParquetInspector(details);
    }
    return buildObjectInspector(details);
  }

  private Component buildPrefixInspector(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    String prefix = node == null ? "" : Strings.firstNonBlank(node.fullKey(), node.id());
    int childCount = node == null || node.children() == null ? 0 : node.children().size();
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("Connection", Strings.firstNonBlank(currentConnection, "-"));
    metadata.put("Bucket", Strings.firstNonBlank(treeModel.bucket(), "-"));
    metadata.put(
        "Summary",
        childCount == 0
            ? "Select a leaf object node to inspect payload content."
            : "Contains " + childCount + " immediate child node(s).");
    inspectorPanel()
        .setContext("Prefix", Strings.firstNonBlank(prefix, "(root)"))
        .setMetadata(metadata)
        .setPreviewVisible(false)
        .setPreviewValue("");
    return inspectorPanel();
  }

  private Component buildObjectInspector(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details) {
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectSummary summary = treeModel.objectsByKey().get(details.key());
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> metadata = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    metadata.put("Connection", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.connectionName(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Bucket", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.bucket(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Bucket URI", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.bucketUri(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Object Key", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.key(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Size", formatBytes(details.sizeBytes()));
    metadata.put("Last Modified", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.lastModifiedIso(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Storage Class", Strings.firstNonBlank(summary == null ? null : summary.storageClass(), "-"));
    metadata.put("Content Type", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.contentType(), "-"));

    inspectorPanel()
        .setContext("Object", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.key(), "-"))
        .setMetadata(metadata)
        .setPreviewVisible(true)
        .setPreviewReadOnly(true)
        .setPreviewAriaLabel(
            ("base64".equalsIgnoreCase(details.encoding()) ? "Base64 " : "")
                + "preview for "
                + details.key())
        .setPreviewValue(details.preview());
    return inspectorPanel();
  }

  private Component buildParquetInspector(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details) {
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection = resolveParquetInspection(details.key());

    StitchSection section = new StitchSection("Parquet Inspector");
    section.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-section");

    StitchSummaryStrip summaryStrip = new StitchSummaryStrip();
    summaryStrip.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-summary");
    summaryStrip.setItems(parquetSummary(details, inspection));

    Span narrative =
        new Span(
            "This object is parquet. Metadata and schema are queried through DuckDB for business-readable inspection.");
    narrative.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-narrative");

    StitchTabbedDetailsPanel tabs = new StitchTabbedDetailsPanel();
    tabs.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-tabs");
    tabs.addTab("metadata", "METADATA", buildParquetMetadataTab(details, inspection));
    tabs.addTab("schema", "SCHEMA", buildParquetSchemaTab(details, inspection));
    tabs.selectTab("metadata");

    section.addToBody(summaryStrip, narrative, tabs);
    return section;
  }

  private Component buildParquetMetadataTab(
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details,
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    if (inspection == null) {
      return parquetUnavailableState("Unable to inspect parquet", "DuckDB parquet inspection was not available.");
    }
    if (isInspectionFailed(inspection)) {
      return parquetFailurePanel(
          "Unable to inspect parquet metadata",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(inspection.failure()),
              "DuckDB did not return parquet metadata for this object."),
          inspection);
    }
    List<ParquetMetadataRow> rows = toMetadataRows(inspection.metadataTable());
    if (rows.isEmpty()) {
      return parquetUnavailableState(
          "No parquet metadata rows",
          "DuckDB returned no metadata rows for "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(details.key(), "the selected object")
              + ".");
    }
    Grid<ParquetMetadataRow> grid = createMetadataGrid(rows);
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    content.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-tab-content");
    if (!inspection.warnings().isEmpty()) {
      content.add(warningPill(inspection.warnings()));
    }
    content.add(grid);
    return content;
  }

  private Component buildParquetSchemaTab(
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details,
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    if (inspection == null) {
      return parquetUnavailableState("Unable to inspect parquet", "DuckDB parquet inspection was not available.");
    }
    if (isInspectionFailed(inspection)) {
      return parquetFailurePanel(
          "Unable to inspect parquet schema",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(inspection.failure()),
              "DuckDB did not return parquet schema for this object."),
          inspection);
    }
    List<ParquetSchemaRow> rows = toSchemaRows(inspection.schemaTable());
    if (rows.isEmpty()) {
      return parquetUnavailableState(
          "No parquet schema rows",
          "DuckDB returned no schema rows for "
              + Strings.firstNonBlank(details.key(), "the selected object")
              + ".");
    }
    Grid<ParquetSchemaRow> grid = createSchemaGrid(rows);
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    content.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-tab-content");
    if (!inspection.warnings().isEmpty()) {
      content.add(warningPill(inspection.warnings()));
    }
    content.add(grid);
    return content;
  }

  private StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection resolveParquetInspection(String objectKey) {
    String normalized = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(objectKey);
    if (normalized == null || currentConnection == null) {
      return null;
    }
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection cached = parquetCache.get(normalized);
    if (cached != null) {
      return cached;
    }
    try {
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection loaded =
          provider.inspectParquet(currentConnection, normalized);
      parquetCache.put(normalized, loaded);
      return loaded;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to inspect parquet", rootMessage(error));
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static LinkedHashMap<String, String> parquetSummary(
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details,
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    summary.put("Connection", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.connectionName(), "-"));
    summary.put("Bucket", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.bucket(), "-"));
    summary.put("Object", Strings.firstNonBlank(details.key(), "-"));
    summary.put("Size", formatBytes(details.sizeBytes()));
    if (inspection != null && inspection.summary() != null) {
      addSummaryValue(summary, "Rows", inspection.summary().get("Rows"));
      addSummaryValue(summary, "Row Groups", inspection.summary().get("Row Groups"));
      addSummaryValue(summary, "Schema Fields", inspection.summary().get("Schema Fields"));
      addSummaryValue(summary, "Compression", inspection.summary().get("Compression"));
      addSummaryValue(summary, "Created By", inspection.summary().get("Created By"));
    }
    return summary;
  }

  private static void addSummaryValue(LinkedHashMap<String, String> summary, String key, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized != null) {
      summary.put(key, normalized);
    }
  }

  private static boolean isInspectionFailed(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    if (inspection == null) {
      return true;
    }
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(inspection.failure())) {
      return true;
    }
    return inspection.metadataTable().rows().isEmpty() && inspection.schemaTable().rows().isEmpty();
  }

  private static List<ParquetMetadataRow> toMetadataRows(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.QueryTable table) {
    if (table == null || table.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ParquetMetadataRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map<String, String> source : table.rows()) {
      rows.add(
          new ParquetMetadataRow(
              valueOf(source, "row_group_id", "row_group"),
              valueOf(source, "column_id", "column"),
              valueOf(source, "path_in_schema", "path", "name"),
              valueOf(source, "type", "physical_type"),
              valueOf(source, "compression", "codec"),
              valueOf(source, "row_group_num_rows", "num_rows"),
              valueOf(source, "num_values", "values"),
              valueOf(source, "stats_null_count", "null_count"),
              clipped(valueOf(source, "stats_min", "min", "min_value"), 70),
              clipped(valueOf(source, "stats_max", "max", "max_value"), 70)));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static List<ParquetSchemaRow> toSchemaRows(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.QueryTable table) {
    if (table == null || table.rows().isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ParquetSchemaRow> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map<String, String> source : table.rows()) {
      String name = valueOf(source, "name", "column_name");
      String path = valueOf(source, "path", "name");
      if ("schema".equalsIgnoreCase(name) || "root".equalsIgnoreCase(name)) {
        continue;
      }
      String repetition = valueOf(source, "repetition_type", "repetition");
      rows.add(
          new ParquetSchemaRow(
              name,
              path,
              valueOf(source, "logical_type", "converted_type"),
              valueOf(source, "type", "physical_type"),
              nullableLabel(repetition),
              repetition,
              valueOf(source, "duckdb_type", "logical"),
              valueOf(source, "field_id", "id")));
    }
    return List.copyOf(rows);
  }

  private static String nullableLabel(String repetition) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(repetition);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    if ("REQUIRED".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return "No";
    }
    if ("OPTIONAL".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return "Yes";
    }
    return "-";
  }

  private static Grid<ParquetMetadataRow> createMetadataGrid(List<ParquetMetadataRow> rows) {
    Grid<ParquetMetadataRow> grid = new Grid<>(ParquetMetadataRow.class, false);
    grid.addClassNames("stitch-results-grid", "stitch-s3-parquet-grid");
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_NO_BORDER);
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setHeight("21rem");
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::path).setHeader("Path").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::rowGroup).setHeader("Row Group").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::columnId).setHeader("Column").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::physicalType).setHeader("Physical Type").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::compression).setHeader("Compression").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::rowCount).setHeader("Rows").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::values).setHeader("Values").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::nullCount).setHeader("Nulls").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::minValue).setHeader("Min").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetMetadataRow::maxValue).setHeader("Max").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.setItems(rows);
    return grid;
  }

  private static Grid<ParquetSchemaRow> createSchemaGrid(List<ParquetSchemaRow> rows) {
    Grid<ParquetSchemaRow> grid = new Grid<>(ParquetSchemaRow.class, false);
    grid.addClassNames("stitch-results-grid", "stitch-s3-parquet-grid");
    grid.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_NO_BORDER);
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setHeight("21rem");
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::field).setHeader("Field").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::path).setHeader("Path").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::logicalType).setHeader("Logical Type").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::physicalType).setHeader("Physical Type").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::nullable).setHeader("Nullable").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::repetition).setHeader("Repetition").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::duckdbType).setHeader("DuckDB Type").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(ParquetSchemaRow::fieldId).setHeader("Field Id").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.setItems(rows);
    return grid;
  }

  private static Component parquetUnavailableState(String title, String description) {
    StitchEmptyState empty =
        new StitchEmptyState(
            Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(title), "No parquet details available"),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(
                Strings.trimToNull(description), "DuckDB did not return parquet details."));
    empty.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-empty");
    return empty;
  }

  private static Component parquetFailurePanel(
      String title, String description, StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    VerticalLayout content = new VerticalLayout();
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.getStyle().set("gap", "0.6rem");
    content.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-error");

    content.add(parquetUnavailableState(title, description));

    String technical = inspectionDetails(inspection);
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(technical)) {
      Pre detailsText = new Pre(technical);
      detailsText.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-error-text");
      Details technicalDisclosure = new Details("Inspection details", detailsText);
      technicalDisclosure.setOpened(false);
      technicalDisclosure.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-disclosure");
      content.add(technicalDisclosure);
    }
    return content;
  }

  private static Span warningPill(List<String> warnings) {
    Span warning =
        new Span(
            "DuckDB returned partial parquet details. "
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(String.join(" | ", warnings)), ""));
    warning.addClassName("stitch-s3-parquet-warning");
    return warning;
  }

  private static String inspectionDetails(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ParquetInspection inspection) {
    if (inspection == null) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> lines = new ArrayList<>();
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(inspection.failure())) {
      lines.add("Failure: " + inspection.failure());
    }
    if (inspection.warnings() != null) {
      for (String warning : inspection.warnings()) {
        String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(warning);
        if (normalized != null) {
          lines.add("- " + normalized);
        }
      }
    }
    return lines.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(System.lineSeparator(), lines);
  }

  private static String valueOf(Map<String, String> row, String... keys) {
    if (row == null || row.isEmpty() || keys == null || keys.length == 0) {
      return "-";
    }
    for (String key : keys) {
      String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (normalizedKey == null) {
        continue;
      }
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : row.entrySet()) {
        String column = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        if (column == null) {
          continue;
        }
        if (column.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedKey)) {
          return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue()), "-");
        }
      }
    }
    return "-";
  }

  private static String clipped(String value, int maxLength) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "-");
    if (maxLength <= 4 || normalized.length() <= maxLength) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, maxLength - 3) + "...";
  }

  private static boolean isParquetObject(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details) {
    if (details == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (isParquetKey(details.key())) {
      return true;
    }
    String contentType = Strings.trimToNull(details.contentType());
    return contentType != null && contentType.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).contains("parquet");
  }

  private static boolean isParquetKey(String key) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).endsWith(".parquet");
  }

  private StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails resolveDetails(String objectKey) {
    String normalized = StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.normalizeKey(objectKey);
    if (normalized == null || currentConnection == null) {
      return null;
    }
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails cached = detailCache.get(normalized);
    if (cached != null) {
      return cached;
    }
    try {
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails loaded =
          provider.loadObjectDetails(currentConnection, normalized);
      detailCache.put(normalized, loaded);
      return loaded;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      StitchDialogs.openInfo("Unable to load object", rootMessage(error));
      return null;
    }
  }

  private void openJsonDialog(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details =
        resolveDetails(node == null ? null : node.fullKey());
    if (details == null) {
      return;
    }
    new StitchJsonDialog("Raw JSON - " + details.key(), asDialogPayload(details)).open();
  }

  private boolean hasPreview(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details =
        resolveDetails(node == null ? null : node.fullKey());
    return details != null && Strings.isNotBlank(details.preview());
  }

  private Map<String, Object> asDialogPayload(StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectDetails details) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, Object> payload = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    payload.put("connection", details.connectionName());
    payload.put("bucket", details.bucket());
    payload.put("bucketUri", details.bucketUri());
    payload.put("key", details.key());
    payload.put("sizeBytes", details.sizeBytes());
    payload.put("truncated", details.truncated());
    payload.put("encoding", details.encoding());
    payload.put("contentType", details.contentType());
    payload.put("contentEncoding", details.contentEncoding());
    payload.put("contentLanguage", details.contentLanguage());
    payload.put("lastModifiedIso", details.lastModifiedIso());
    payload.put("eTag", details.eTag());
    payload.put("metadata", details.metadata());
    payload.put("preview", toJsonOrText(details.preview()));
    return payload;
  }

  private Object toJsonOrText(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "";
    }
    try {
      JsonNode parsed = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().readTree(normalized);
      return parsed == null ? normalized : parsed;
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return normalized;
    }
  }

  private Component nodeIcon(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType =
        node == null || !node.payloadNode() ? VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O : VaadinIcon.FILE_O;
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private Component nodeDecorator(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (node.payloadNode()) {
      StitchStorageS3BrowserProvider.ObjectSummary summary = treeModel.objectsByKey().get(node.fullKey());
      if (summary == null) {
        return null;
      }
      return new StitchStatusBadge(formatBytes(summary.sizeBytes()), StitchStatusBadge.Tone.INFO);
    }
    int childCount = node.children() == null ? 0 : node.children().size();
    if (childCount <= 0) {
      return null;
    }
    return new StitchStatusBadge(String.valueOf(childCount), StitchStatusBadge.Tone.NEUTRAL);
  }

  private void setConnectionSelectorValue(String value) {
    suppressConnectionEvents = true;
    if (value == null) {
      connectionSelector.clear();
    } else {
      connectionSelector.setValue(value);
    }
    suppressConnectionEvents = false;
  }

  private record ParquetMetadataRow(
      String rowGroup,
      String columnId,
      String path,
      String physicalType,
      String compression,
      String rowCount,
      String values,
      String nullCount,
      String minValue,
      String maxValue) {}

  private record ParquetSchemaRow(
      String field,
      String path,
      String logicalType,
      String physicalType,
      String nullable,
      String repetition,
      String duckdbType,
      String fieldId) {}

  private boolean saveNoOp() {
    return true;
  }

  private void discardNoOp() {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

public final class StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "S3 Browser";
      this.routePath = "data/s3-browser";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - S3 Browser";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Browse S3 objects by hierarchical path and inspect object payloads.";
      this.order = 10;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchStorageS3BrowserScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/storage/StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.access.AccessManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.RowResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.TabularManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.TabularManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security.StitchIdentityContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.data.StitchDatasetProviderSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class StitchStorageS3QueryProvider {
  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.class);
  private static final Pattern DATASET_FUNCTION_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("(?i)dataset\\s*\\(\\s*'((?:''|[^'])+)'\\s*\\)");
  private static final Pattern TABLE_REFERENCE_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile(
          "(?i)\\b(?:from|join)\\s+((?:\"[^\"]+\"|[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*)(?:\\s*\\.\\s*(?:\"[^\"]+\"|[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9_]*))?)");
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final SessionImpl session;
  private final AccessManager accessManager;
  private final StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter keyAdapter = new StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter();

  public StitchStorageS3QueryProvider(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    Fabric.Session current = this.runtimeContext.session();
    if (!(current instanceof SessionImpl resolved)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session implementation must support internal access");
    }
    this.session = resolved;
    this.accessManager = resolved.access();
  }

  public TreeModel loadTree(List<String> scopedGroups) {
    List<DatasetRef> datasets = listAccessibleDatasets(scopedGroups);
    if (datasets.isEmpty()) {
      return TreeModel.empty();
    }
    List<String> keys = datasets.stream().map(DatasetRef::pathKey).toList();
    StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.Model tree = keyAdapter.build(keys);
    LinkedHashMap<String, DatasetRef> byPath = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (DatasetRef ref : datasets) {
      byPath.put(ref.pathKey(), ref);
    }
    return new TreeModel(tree.roots(), tree.byId(), Map.copyOf(byPath));
  }

  public QueryResult executeSql(String sql) {
    return executeSql(sql, null, null);
  }

  public QueryResult executeSql(String sql, Integer limit) {
    return executeSql(sql, limit, null);
  }

  public QueryResult executeSql(String sql, Integer limit, List<String> scopedGroups) {
    String normalized = sanitizeSql(sql);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("SQL is required");
    }
    String plannedSql = applyLimitWrapper(normalized, limit);
    List<DatasetRef> accessibleDatasets = listAccessibleDatasets(scopedGroups);
    QueryExecutionPlan executionPlan =
        prepareExecutionPlan(plannedSql, accessibleDatasets, scopedGroups);
    String subject = currentSubject();

    LOG.info(
        "[Stitch][S3Query] execute subject={} limit={} rawSql={} plannedSql={} resolvedSql={} datasets={}",
        subject,
        limit,
        normalized,
        plannedSql,
        executionPlan.resolvedSql(),
        executionPlan.datasetIds().stream().map(DatasetId::toString).toList());

    try {
      LinkedHashSet<DatasetId> installIds = new LinkedHashSet<>(executionPlan.datasetIds());
      LOG.info(
          "[Stitch][S3Query] install-datasets count={} scopedGroups={} datasetIds={}",
          installIds.size(),
          scopedGroups == null ? List.of() : scopedGroups,
          installIds.stream().map(DatasetId::toString).toList());

      RowResult result =
          StitchDatasetProviderSupport.runAsSubject(
              subject,
              () -> {
                TabularManager directTabular = session.data().direct().tabular();
                if (directTabular instanceof TabularManagerImpl directManager) {
                  for (DatasetId datasetId : installIds) {
                    directManager.installDataset(datasetId.toString());
                  }
                }
                return session.data().direct().rows().querySql(executionPlan.resolvedSql());
              });
      List<String> columns = result.columns() == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(result.columns());
      List<Map<String, Object>> rows = toRows(columns, result.rows());
      if (rows.isEmpty()) {
        LOG.warn(
            "[Stitch][S3Query] empty-result subject={} limit={} columns={} sql={}",
            subject,
            limit,
            columns.size(),
            executionPlan.resolvedSql());
      } else {
        LOG.info(
            "[Stitch][S3Query] success subject={} rows={} columns={} limit={}",
            subject,
            rows.size(),
            columns.size(),
            limit);
      }
      return new QueryResult(columns, rows);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      LOG.error(
          "[Stitch][S3Query] failure subject={} limit={} sql={} message={}",
          subject,
          limit,
          executionPlan.resolvedSql(),
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), error.getClass().getName()),
          error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private static String sanitizeSql(String sql) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(sql);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    int end = normalized.length();
    while (end > 0 && normalized.charAt(end - 1) == ';') {
      end--;
    }
    String stripped = Strings.trimToNull(normalized.substring(0, end));
    return stripped == null ? null : stripped;
  }

  private static String applyLimitWrapper(String sql, Integer limit) {
    if (limit == null || limit <= 0) {
      return sql;
    }
    if (containsLimitClause(sql)) {
      return sql;
    }
    return sql + " limit " + limit;
  }

  private static boolean containsLimitClause(String sql) {
    return sql != null && sql.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).matches("(?s).*\\blimit\\b\\s+\\d+.*");
  }

  private QueryExecutionPlan prepareExecutionPlan(
      String sql, List<DatasetRef> accessibleDatasets, List<String> scopedGroups) {
    QueryExecutionPlan functionRewrite = rewriteDatasetFunctions(sql);
    return rewriteAndResolveTableReferences(
        functionRewrite.resolvedSql(),
        functionRewrite.datasetIds(),
        accessibleDatasets,
        scopedGroups);
  }

  private QueryExecutionPlan rewriteDatasetFunctions(String sql) {
    Matcher matcher = DATASET_FUNCTION_PATTERN.matcher(sql);
    StringBuilder rewritten = new StringBuilder();
    List<DatasetId> datasetIds = new ArrayList<>();
    int cursor = 0;
    while (matcher.find()) {
      rewritten.append(sql, cursor, matcher.start());
      DatasetRefPath refPath = parseDatasetRefPath(matcher.group(1));
      DatasetId datasetId = DatasetId.parse("dataset:" + refPath.group() + "/" + refPath.namespace() + "/" + refPath.name());
      datasetIds.add(datasetId);
      rewritten.append(quoteIdentifier(refPath.namespace())).append(".").append(quoteIdentifier(refPath.name()));
      cursor = matcher.end();
    }
    if (cursor == 0) {
      return new QueryExecutionPlan(sql, List.of());
    }
    rewritten.append(sql.substring(cursor));
    return new QueryExecutionPlan(rewritten.toString(), List.copyOf(datasetIds));
  }

  private QueryExecutionPlan rewriteAndResolveTableReferences(
      String sql,
      List<DatasetId> seedDatasetIds,
      List<DatasetRef> accessibleDatasets,
      List<String> scopedGroups) {
    LinkedHashSet<DatasetId> resolvedDatasetIds = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (seedDatasetIds != null) {
      resolvedDatasetIds.addAll(seedDatasetIds);
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(sql) == null || accessibleDatasets == null || accessibleDatasets.isEmpty()) {
      return new QueryExecutionPlan(sql, List.copyOf(resolvedDatasetIds));
    }

    List<TableReferenceMatch> references = extractTableReferenceMatches(sql);
    if (references.isEmpty()) {
      return new QueryExecutionPlan(sql, List.copyOf(resolvedDatasetIds));
    }

    boolean singleScopedGroup = scopedGroups != null && scopedGroups.size() == 1;
    String scopedGroup = singleScopedGroup ? Strings.trimToNull(scopedGroups.getFirst()) : null;

    StringBuilder rewritten = new StringBuilder(sql.length() + 32);
    int cursor = 0;
    for (TableReferenceMatch match : references) {
      TableReference reference = match.reference();
      List<DatasetRef> matches = findDatasetMatches(reference, accessibleDatasets, scopedGroup);
      if (matches.size() > 1) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Ambiguous table reference '"
                + reference.render()
                + "'. Select a single Group or qualify as namespace.table.");
      }
      rewritten.append(sql, cursor, match.start());
      if (matches.isEmpty()) {
        rewritten.append(sql, match.start(), match.end());
      } else {
        DatasetRef dataset = matches.getFirst();
        resolvedDatasetIds.add(datasetIdOf(dataset));
        if (reference.namespace() == null) {
          rewritten
              .append(quoteIdentifier(dataset.namespace()))
              .append(".")
              .append(quoteIdentifier(dataset.name()));
        } else {
          rewritten.append(sql, match.start(), match.end());
        }
      }
      cursor = match.end();
    }
    rewritten.append(sql, cursor, sql.length());
    return new QueryExecutionPlan(rewritten.toString(), List.copyOf(resolvedDatasetIds));
  }

  private static DatasetRefPath parseDatasetRefPath(String rawLiteral) {
    String literal = Strings.trimToNull(unescapeSqlLiteral(rawLiteral));
    if (literal == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("dataset(...) reference is missing a dataset path");
    }
    String[] parts = literal.split("\\.");
    if (parts.length != 3) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "dataset(...) must use 'group.namespace.name' format: " + literal);
    }
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(parts[0]);
    String namespace = Strings.trimToNull(parts[1]);
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(parts[2]);
    if (group == null || namespace == null || name == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "dataset(...) must use non-blank 'group.namespace.name' segments: " + literal);
    }
    return new DatasetRefPath(group, namespace, name);
  }

  private static String unescapeSqlLiteral(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.replace("''", "'");
  }

  private static String quoteIdentifier(String value) {
    return "\"" + value.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  private List<DatasetRef> listAccessibleDatasets(List<String> scopedGroups) {
    DiscoveryCache discoveryCache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
    if (discoveryCache == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> normalizedGroups = normalizeGroups(scopedGroups);
    String subject = currentSubject();
    Map<String, DatasetRef> indexed = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Definition definition : discoveryCache.allDefinitions()) {
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionDataset dataset)) {
        continue;
      }
      DatasetRef ref = toRef(dataset);
      if (ref == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!normalizedGroups.isEmpty()
          && !normalizedGroups.contains(ref.group().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        continue;
      }
      if (!accessManager.canQueryDataset(subject, ref.resourceId())) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = indexKey(ref.resourceId());
      DatasetRef existing = indexed.get(key);
      if (existing == null || ref.recencyEpochMs() > existing.recencyEpochMs()) {
        indexed.put(key, ref);
      }
    }
    if (indexed.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return indexed.values().stream()
        .sorted(
            Comparator.comparing(DatasetRef::group, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(DatasetRef::namespace, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                .thenComparing(DatasetRef::name, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .toList();
  }

  private static DatasetId datasetIdOf(DatasetRef ref) {
    return DatasetId.parse("dataset:" + ref.group() + "/" + ref.namespace() + "/" + ref.name());
  }

  private static LinkedHashSet<DatasetId> inferDatasetsForSql(
      String sql, List<DatasetRef> accessibleDatasets, List<String> scopedGroups) {
    LinkedHashSet<DatasetId> resolved = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (Strings.trimToNull(sql) == null || accessibleDatasets == null || accessibleDatasets.isEmpty()) {
      return resolved;
    }
    List<TableReference> references = extractTableReferences(sql);
    if (references.isEmpty()) {
      return resolved;
    }
    boolean singleScopedGroup = scopedGroups != null && scopedGroups.size() == 1;
    String scopedGroup =
        singleScopedGroup ? Strings.trimToNull(scopedGroups.getFirst()) : null;

    for (TableReference reference : references) {
      List<DatasetRef> matches = findDatasetMatches(reference, accessibleDatasets, scopedGroup);
      if (matches.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (matches.size() > 1) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Ambiguous table reference '"
                + reference.render()
                + "'. Select a single Group or qualify as namespace.table.");
      }
      resolved.add(datasetIdOf(matches.getFirst()));
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  private static List<DatasetRef> findDatasetMatches(
      TableReference reference, List<DatasetRef> accessibleDatasets, String scopedGroup) {
    List<DatasetRef> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DatasetRef candidate : accessibleDatasets) {
      if (candidate == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (scopedGroup != null && !scopedGroup.equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.group())) {
        continue;
      }
      if (reference.namespace() == null) {
        if (reference.table().equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.name())) {
          matches.add(candidate);
        }
      } else if (reference.namespace().equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.namespace())
          && reference.table().equalsIgnoreCase(candidate.name())) {
        matches.add(candidate);
      }
    }
    return matches;
  }

  private static List<TableReference> extractTableReferences(String sql) {
    LinkedHashMap<String, TableReference> ordered = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (TableReferenceMatch match : extractTableReferenceMatches(sql)) {
      TableReference reference = match.reference();
      if (reference == null) {
        continue;
      }
      ordered.putIfAbsent(reference.key(), reference);
    }
    return List.copyOf(ordered.values());
  }

  private static List<TableReferenceMatch> extractTableReferenceMatches(String sql) {
    Matcher matcher = TABLE_REFERENCE_PATTERN.matcher(sql);
    List<TableReferenceMatch> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    while (matcher.find()) {
      TableReference reference = parseTableReferenceToken(matcher.group(1));
      if (reference == null) {
        continue;
      }
      matches.add(new TableReferenceMatch(reference, matcher.start(1), matcher.end(1)));
    }
    return List.copyOf(matches);
  }

  private static TableReference parseTableReferenceToken(String token) {
    String raw = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (raw == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String[] parts = raw.split("\\.");
    if (parts.length == 1) {
      String table = normalizeIdentifier(parts[0]);
      return table == null ? null : new TableReference(null, table);
    }
    if (parts.length == 2) {
      String namespace = normalizeIdentifier(parts[0]);
      String table = normalizeIdentifier(parts[1]);
      if (namespace == null || table == null) {
        return null;
      }
      return new TableReference(namespace, table);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String normalizeIdentifier(String token) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(token);
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value.startsWith("\"") && value.endsWith("\"") && value.length() >= 2) {
      value = value.substring(1, value.length() - 1).replace("\"\"", "\"");
    }
    value = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return value;
  }

  private static List<Map<String, Object>> toRows(List<String> columns, List<List<Object>> rows) {
    if (columns == null || rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<Map<String, Object>> mapped = new ArrayList<>(rows.size());
    for (List<Object> row : rows) {
      LinkedHashMap<String, Object> values = new LinkedHashMap<>(columns.size());
      for (int index = 0; index < columns.size(); index++) {
        Object value = row != null && index < row.size() ? row.get(index) : null;
        values.put(columns.get(index), value);
      }
      mapped.add(Map.copyOf(values));
    }
    return List.copyOf(mapped);
  }

  private DatasetRef toRef(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.envelope() == null) {
      return null;
    }
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definition.envelope();
    String group = normalize(envelope.group());
    String namespace = normalize(definition.namespace());
    String envelopeName = normalize(envelope.name());
    String datasetName = envelopeName;
    int slash = envelopeName.indexOf('/');
    if (slash > 0 && slash < envelopeName.length() - 1) {
      String namespaceFromEnvelope = normalize(envelopeName.substring(0, slash));
      if (!namespace.equals(namespaceFromEnvelope)) {
        return null;
      }
      datasetName = normalize(envelopeName.substring(slash + 1));
    }
    if (group.isBlank() || namespace.isBlank() || datasetName.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String resourceId = DataEntitlements.canonicalDatasetResourceId(group, namespace, datasetName);
    String pathKey = group + "/" + namespace + "/" + datasetName;
    String qualifiedName = group + "." + namespace + "." + datasetName;
    long recency = recencyEpoch(envelope);
    return new DatasetRef(group, namespace, datasetName, resourceId, pathKey, qualifiedName, recency);
  }

  private static Set<String> normalizeGroups(List<String> groups) {
    if (groups == null || groups.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String group : groups) {
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Set.of() : Set.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static long recencyEpoch(DefinitionEnvelope envelope) {
    if (envelope == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    long updated = parseEpoch(envelope.updatedTimeUtc());
    if (updated > Long.MIN_VALUE) {
      return updated;
    }
    return parseEpoch(envelope.createdTimeUtc());
  }

  private static long parseEpoch(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
    try {
      return Instant.parse(normalized).toEpochMilli();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return Long.MIN_VALUE;
    }
  }

  private String currentSubject() {
    return StitchIdentityContext.resolveSubject(runtimeContext.settings().sso().fallbackSubject());
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  private static String indexKey(String value) {
    return normalize(value).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public record TreeModel(
      List<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> roots,
      Map<String, StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> byId,
      Map<String, DatasetRef> datasetsByPath) {
    public static TreeModel empty() {
      return new TreeModel(List.of(), Map.of(), Map.of());
    }
  }

  public record DatasetRef(
      String group,
      String namespace,
      String name,
      String resourceId,
      String pathKey,
      String qualifiedName,
      long recencyEpochMs) {}

  public record QueryResult(List<String> columns, List<Map<String, Object>> rows) {
    public QueryResult {
      columns = columns == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(columns);
      rows = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
    }
  }

  private record QueryExecutionPlan(String resolvedSql, List<DatasetId> datasetIds) {
    private QueryExecutionPlan {
      resolvedSql = Strings.requireNonBlank(resolvedSql, "resolvedSql");
      datasetIds = datasetIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(datasetIds);
    }
  }

  private record DatasetRefPath(String group, String namespace, String name) {}

  private record TableReference(String namespace, String table) {
    private String key() {
      return (namespace == null ? "" : namespace.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT) + ".")
          + table.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    }

    private String render() {
      return namespace == null ? table : namespace + "." + table;
    }
  }

  private record TableReferenceMatch(TableReference reference, int start, int end) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
