@Route(value = "data/s3-query", layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
public class StitchStorageS3QueryScreen extends StitchPage {
  private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchStorageS3QueryScreen.class);
  private static final int DEFAULT_LIMIT = 10;
  private static final int MIN_LIMIT = 1;
  private static final int MAX_LIMIT = 10_000;

  private final StitchStorageS3QueryProvider provider;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchGroupFilter groupFilter;
  private final Button refreshAction = new Button("REFRESH", event -> loadTree(true));
  private final StitchTreeLayout<org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode>
      treeLayout = new StitchTreeLayout<>();

  private final VerticalLayout queryWorkspace = new VerticalLayout();
  private final TextArea sqlEditor = new TextArea("SQL");
  private final IntegerField limitField = new IntegerField("Limit");
  private final Button executeInlineAction = new Button("EXECUTE", event -> executeQuery());
  private final Span queryStatus = new Span("Ready.");
  private final StitchResultsView<Map<String, Object>> results = new StitchResultsView<>();

  private StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.TreeModel treeModel = StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.TreeModel.empty();
  private List<String> configuredColumns = List.of();
  private boolean autoGeneratedSql;
  private String autoGeneratedDatasetPathKey;
  private boolean suppressSqlEvents;
  private boolean suppressLimitEvents;
  private int currentLimit = DEFAULT_LIMIT;

  public StitchStorageS3QueryScreen(
      Stitch stitch, StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext, StitchStorageS3QueryProvider provider) {
    this(requireConfig(stitch), runtimeContext, provider);
  }

  private StitchStorageS3QueryScreen(
      StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig config,
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      StitchStorageS3QueryProvider provider) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config").pageTitle(),
        Strings.firstNonBlank(config.pageSubtitle(), ""));
    this.provider = Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider");
    this.groupFilter = new StitchGroupFilter(Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext"));

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    addClassName("stitch-s3-query-screen");

    configureFiltersBar();
    configureWorkspace();
    configureTreeLayout();

    addToBody(filtersBar, treeLayout);
    body().setFlexGrow(1, treeLayout);
    loadTree(false);
  }

  private static StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig requireConfig(Stitch stitch) {
    return stitch
        .features()
        .data()
        .map(StitchDataFeature::s3Query)
        .filter(StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig::enabled)
        .orElseThrow(NotFoundException::new);
  }

  private void configureFiltersBar() {
    groupFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> loadTree(false));

    refreshAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.styleSecondaryAction(refreshAction);
    refreshAction.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-refresh-action");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Refresh datasets");
    refreshAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Refresh datasets");

    filtersBar.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-filters");
    filtersBar.withGroupSelector(groupFilter).withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  private void configureTreeLayout() {
    treeLayout.addClassName("stitch-tree-layout--s3-query");
    treeLayout.withAutoNavSizing(300, 720);
    treeLayout.setNavHeaderTitle("DATASETS");
    treeLayout.setDetailHeaderTitle("SQL WORKSPACE");
    treeLayout.setNoSelectionContent(queryWorkspace);
    treeLayout.setNoDetailsContent(queryWorkspace);
    treeLayout.setDetailRenderer(node -> queryWorkspace);
    treeLayout.setChildResolver(
        org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode::children);
    treeLayout.setLabelResolver(
        org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode::label);
    treeLayout.setNodeIconRenderer(this::treeNodeIcon);
    treeLayout.treeNav().withNodeIconClickBehavior(StitchTreeNav.NodeIconClickBehavior.TOGGLE_EXPAND_COLLAPSE);
    treeLayout.treeNav().searchField().setPlaceholder("Search datasets");
    treeLayout.treeNav().searchField().setAriaLabel("Search datasets");
    treeLayout.treeNav().onSelectionChange(this::handleTreeSelection);
  }

  private void configureWorkspace() {
    queryWorkspace.setSizeFull();
    queryWorkspace.setPadding(false);
    queryWorkspace.setSpacing(false);
    queryWorkspace.getStyle().set("gap", "0.55rem");
    queryWorkspace.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-workspace");

    sqlEditor.setWidthFull();
    sqlEditor.setMinHeight("14rem");
    sqlEditor.setMaxHeight("24rem");
    sqlEditor.setPlaceholder("SELECT * FROM namespace.table LIMIT 10;");
    sqlEditor.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-editor");
    sqlEditor.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!suppressSqlEvents && event.isFromClient()) {
            autoGeneratedSql = false;
            autoGeneratedDatasetPathKey = null;
          }
        });

    limitField.setMin(MIN_LIMIT);
    limitField.setMax(MAX_LIMIT);
    limitField.setStepButtonsVisible(true);
    limitField.setValue(DEFAULT_LIMIT);
    limitField.setWidth("7.5rem");
    limitField.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-limit");
    limitField.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (suppressLimitEvents) {
            return;
          }
          int normalized = normalizeLimit(event.getValue());
          currentLimit = normalized;
          if (!Objects.equals(event.getValue(), normalized)) {
            suppressLimitEvents = true;
            limitField.setValue(normalized);
            suppressLimitEvents = false;
          }
          if (autoGeneratedSql) {
            StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.DatasetRef dataset =
                treeModel.datasetsByPath().get(autoGeneratedDatasetPathKey);
            if (dataset != null) {
              applyAutoSql(dataset);
            }
          }
        });

    executeInlineAction.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(executeInlineAction);
    executeInlineAction.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-execute-inline");
    executeInlineAction.setDisableOnClick(false);
    executeInlineAction.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Execute SQL query");
    executeInlineAction.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Execute SQL query");

    HorizontalLayout controls = new HorizontalLayout(limitField, executeInlineAction);
    controls.setPadding(false);
    controls.setSpacing(false);
    controls.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.END);
    controls.getStyle().set("gap", "0.5rem");
    controls.setWidthFull();
    controls.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-controls");
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(10, 25, 50, 100);
    results.setPageSize(10);
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.toolbar().setVisible(false);
    results.setEmptyState("No results", "Execute a SQL query to view rows.");
    results.grid().setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.NONE);
    results.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "S3 query results");

    queryStatus.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-status");
    results.setStatus(queryStatus);
    results.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-results");

    queryWorkspace.add(sqlEditor, controls, results);
    queryWorkspace.setFlexGrow(1, results);
  }

  private void loadTree(boolean preserveSelection) {
    String desiredSelection =
        preserveSelection && treeLayout.treeNav().selectedItem() != null
            ? treeLayout.treeNav().selectedItem().id()
            : null;
    try {
      treeModel = provider.loadTree(groupFilter.effectiveGroups());
      treeLayout.setRoots(treeModel.roots());
      treeLayout.treeNav().collapseAll();
      if (desiredSelection != null
          && treeLayout.treeNav().selectFirstMatching(node -> desiredSelection.equals(node.id()))) {
        return;
      }
      treeLayout.treeNav().select(null);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      treeModel = StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.TreeModel.empty();
      treeLayout.setRoots(List.of());
      treeLayout.treeNav().select(null);
      Notification.show("Unable to load datasets", 2200, Position.BOTTOM_START);
    }
  }

  private void handleTreeSelection(
      org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!node.payloadNode()) {
      return;
    }
    StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.DatasetRef dataset = treeModel.datasetsByPath().get(node.fullKey());
    if (dataset == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (Strings.trimToNull(sqlEditor.getValue()) == null) {
      applyAutoSql(dataset);
    }
  }

  private void applyAutoSql(StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.DatasetRef dataset) {
    if (dataset == null) {
      return;
    }
    String sql = buildAutoSql(dataset, currentLimit);
    suppressSqlEvents = true;
    sqlEditor.setValue(sql);
    suppressSqlEvents = false;
    autoGeneratedSql = true;
    autoGeneratedDatasetPathKey = dataset.pathKey();
  }

  private void executeQuery() {
    String rawSql = sqlEditor.getValue();
    LOG.info(
        "[Stitch][S3Query][UI] execute-click route=data/s3-query limit={} sqlPresent={} sqlLength={}",
        currentLimit,
        Strings.trimToNull(rawSql) != null,
        rawSql == null ? 0 : rawSql.length());

    String sql = Strings.trimToNull(rawSql);
    if (sql == null) {
      LOG.warn("[Stitch][S3Query][UI] execute-aborted reason=empty-sql");
      setQueryStatus("Enter SQL before executing.", true);
      return;
    }
    try {
      StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.QueryResult queryResult =
          provider.executeSql(sql, currentLimit, groupFilter.effectiveGroups());
      configureResultColumns(queryResult.columns(), queryResult.rows());
      results.setItems(queryResult.rows());
      results.setEmpty(queryResult.rows().isEmpty());
      LOG.info(
          "[Stitch][S3Query][UI] execute-complete rows={} columns={}",
          queryResult.rows().size(),
          queryResult.columns().size());
      setQueryStatus("Returned " + queryResult.rows().size() + " row(s).", false);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      LOG.error(
          "[Stitch][S3Query][UI] execute-failed message={}",
          Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), error.getClass().getName()),
          error);
      setQueryStatus(
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              Strings.trimToNull(error.getMessage()), "Unable to execute SQL query."),
          true);
      results.setItems(List.of());
      results.setEmpty(true);
    }
  }

  private void configureResultColumns(
      List<String> requestedColumns, List<Map<String, Object>> rows) {
    List<String> resolved = normalizeColumns(requestedColumns, rows);
    if (Objects.equals(configuredColumns, resolved)) {
      return;
    }
    StitchGrid<Map<String, Object>> grid = results.grid();
    grid.removeAllColumns();
    int index = 0;
    for (String column : resolved) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(column);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      final String accessor = key;
      grid.addColumn(
          StitchGridColumn.<Map<String, Object>>text(
                  key, row -> formatValue(row == null ? null : row.get(accessor)))
              .key("s3-query-col-" + index++)
              .kind(StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP)
              .enumLikeBadges(false)
              .sortable(false));
    }
    configuredColumns = resolved;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeColumns(
      List<String> requestedColumns, List<Map<String, Object>> rows) {
    if (requestedColumns != null && !requestedColumns.isEmpty()) {
      return List.copyOf(requestedColumns);
    }
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Map<String, Object> first = rows.get(0);
    if (first == null || first.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(first.keySet()));
  }

  private void setQueryStatus(String message, boolean error) {
    queryStatus.setText(Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(message), ""));
    queryStatus.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    if (error) {
      queryStatus.addClassName("stitch-s3-query-status--error");
    } else {
      queryStatus.removeClassName("stitch-s3-query-status--error");
    }
  }

  private Component treeNodeIcon(
      org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree.StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
    VaadinIcon iconType;
    if (node == null || !node.payloadNode()) {
      iconType = VaadinIcon.FOLDER_OPEN_O;
    } else {
      iconType = VaadinIcon.TABLE;
    }
    Icon icon = iconType.create();
    icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    return icon;
  }

  private static int normalizeLimit(Integer value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return DEFAULT_LIMIT;
    }
    int integer = (int) Math.round(value);
    if (integer < MIN_LIMIT) {
      return MIN_LIMIT;
    }
    if (integer > MAX_LIMIT) {
      return MAX_LIMIT;
    }
    return integer;
  }

  private static String buildAutoSql(StitchStorageS3QueryProvider.DatasetRef dataset, int limit) {
    int safeLimit = Math.max(MIN_LIMIT, limit);
    return "SELECT *\nFROM " + quoteIdentifier(dataset.namespace()) + "." + quoteIdentifier(dataset.name()) + "\nLIMIT " + safeLimit + ";";
  }

  private static String quoteIdentifier(String value) {
    return "\"" + Strings.trimToEmpty(value).replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  private static String formatValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (value instanceof byte[] bytes) {
      int max = Math.min(bytes.length, 12);
      StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder("0x");
      for (int i = 0; i < max; i++) {
        builder.append(String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%02x", bytes[i]));
      }
      if (bytes.length > max) {
        builder.append("...");
      }
      return builder.toString();
    }
    return String.valueOf(value);
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/feature/storage/StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.feature.storage;

public final class StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final String pageTitle;
  private final String pageSubtitle;
  private final int order;
  private final boolean enabled;

  private StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = require(builder.routePath, "routePath");
    this.pageTitle = require(builder.pageTitle, "pageTitle");
    this.pageSubtitle = optional(builder.pageSubtitle);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public String pageTitle() {
    return pageTitle;
  }

  public String pageSubtitle() {
    return pageSubtitle;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private String pageTitle;
    private String pageSubtitle;
    private int order;
    private boolean enabled = true;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = "S3 Query";
      this.routePath = "data/s3-query";
      this.pageTitle = "Data - S3 Query";
      this.pageSubtitle = "Query accessible S3-backed datasets using SQL.";
      this.order = 11;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageTitle(String value) {
      this.pageTitle = require(value, "pageTitle");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPageSubtitle(String value) {
      this.pageSubtitle = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig build() {
      return new StitchStorageS3QueryScreenConfig(this);
    }
  }
}


org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/grid/StitchGrid.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.AbstractGridSingleSelectionModel;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.ColumnTextAlign;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.GridVariant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchGrid<T> extends Grid<T> {
  private final Map<Grid.Column<T>, StitchGridColumn.Kind> kinds = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<Grid.Column<T>, Integer> insertionOrder = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private int sequence;

  public StitchGrid() {
    super();
    configureDefaults();
  }

  public StitchGrid(Class<T> beanType) {
    super(beanType, false);
    configureDefaults();
  }

  private void configureDefaults() {
    setWidthFull();
    setAllRowsVisible(true);
    setSelectionMode(SelectionMode.SINGLE);
    if (getSelectionModel() instanceof AbstractGridSingleSelectionModel<?> singleSelectionModel) {
      singleSelectionModel.setDeselectAllowed(true);
    }
    setColumnReorderingAllowed(true);
    addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT);
    addClassName("stitch-results-grid");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_GRID);
  }

  public StitchGrid<T> addColumns(Collection<StitchGridColumn<T>> columns) {
    if (columns != null) {
      for (StitchGridColumn<T> column : columns) {
        addColumn(column);
      }
    }
    return this;
  }

  public Grid.Column<T> addColumn(StitchGridColumn<T> definition) {
    StitchGridColumn<T> column = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(definition, "definition");
    Grid.Column<T> added = column.applyTo(this);
    registerColumn(added, column.kind());
    applyKindDefaults(added, column.kind());
    applyStandardOrder();
    return added;
  }

  void registerActionsColumn(Grid.Column<T> column) {
    if (column == null) {
      return;
    }
    registerColumn(column, StitchGridColumn.Kind.ACTIONS);
    applyKindDefaults(column, StitchGridColumn.Kind.ACTIONS);
    applyStandardOrder();
  }

  private void registerColumn(Grid.Column<T> column, StitchGridColumn.Kind kind) {
    kinds.put(column, kind == null ? StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP : kind);
    insertionOrder.put(column, sequence++);
  }

  private void applyKindDefaults(Grid.Column<T> column, StitchGridColumn.Kind kind) {
    if (column == null || kind == null) {
      return;
    }
    switch (kind) {
      case STATUS -> {
        column.setAutoWidth(false);
        column.setWidth("8.6rem");
        column.setFlexGrow(0);
        column.setResizable(true);
        column.setTextAlign(ColumnTextAlign.CENTER);
      }
      case ENABLED -> {
        column.setAutoWidth(false);
        column.setWidth("8.1rem");
        column.setFlexGrow(0);
        column.setResizable(false);
        column.setTextAlign(ColumnTextAlign.CENTER);
      }
      case NAME -> {
        if (column.getFlexGrow() <= 0) {
          column.setFlexGrow(1);
        }
        column.setPartNameGenerator(item -> "stitch-grid-name-cell");
      }
      case TIMESTAMP -> {
        column.setAutoWidth(true);
        column.setFlexGrow(0);
        column.setSortable(true);
      }
      case ACTIONS -> {
        column.setHeader("");
        column.setAutoWidth(false);
        if (column.getWidth() == null || column.getWidth().isBlank()) {
          column.setWidth("4.9rem");
        }
        column.setFlexGrow(0);
        column.setSortable(false);
        column.setResizable(false);
        column.setTextAlign(ColumnTextAlign.END);
        column.setPartNameGenerator(item -> "stitch-grid-actions-cell");
      }
      default -> {
      }
    }
  }

  private void applyStandardOrder() {
    List<Grid.Column<T>> current = new ArrayList<>(getColumns());
    if (current.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    boolean hasStatus =
        current.stream().anyMatch(column -> kindOf(column) == StitchGridColumn.Kind.STATUS);
    current.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt((Grid.Column<T> column) -> priority(kindOf(column), hasStatus))
            .thenComparingInt(column -> insertionOrder.getOrDefault(column, Integer.MAX_VALUE)));
    setColumnOrder(current);
  }

  private StitchGridColumn.Kind kindOf(Grid.Column<T> column) {
    return kinds.getOrDefault(column, StitchGridColumn.Kind.APP);
  }

  private static int priority(StitchGridColumn.Kind kind, boolean hasStatus) {
    return switch (kind) {
      case STATUS -> 10;
      case ENABLED -> hasStatus ? 40 : 10;
      case GROUP -> 20;
      case NAME -> 30;
      case APP -> 40;
      case TIMESTAMP -> 50;
      case ACTIONS -> 60;
    };
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/grid/StitchGridColumn.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.data.renderer.ComponentRenderer;
import com.vaadin.flow.data.renderer.Renderer;
import com.vaadin.flow.function.ValueProvider;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.ZonedDateTime;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.badge.StitchStatusBadge;

public class StitchGridColumn<T> {
  private static final DateTimeFormatter UTC_SECONDS =
      DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss 'UTC'").withZone(ZoneOffset.UTC);

  private final String header;
  private final ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider;
  private final Renderer<T> renderer;
  private String key;
  private boolean autoWidth = true;
  private int flexGrow = 1;
  private boolean sortable = true;
  private boolean resizable = true;
  private String width;
  private boolean frozen;
  private Kind kind = Kind.APP;
  private boolean enumLikeBadges = true;

  private StitchGridColumn(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider, Renderer<T> renderer) {
    this.header = normalizeHeader(header);
    this.valueProvider = valueProvider;
    this.renderer = renderer;
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> text(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return new StitchGridColumn<>(header, Objects.requireNonNull(valueProvider, "valueProvider"), null);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> renderer(String header, Renderer<T> renderer) {
    return new StitchGridColumn<>(header, null, Objects.requireNonNull(renderer, "renderer"));
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> component(
      String header, ValueProvider<T, ? extends Component> valueProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(valueProvider, "valueProvider");
    Renderer<T> componentRenderer =
        new ComponentRenderer<Component, T>(item -> valueProvider.apply(item));
    return new StitchGridColumn<>(header, null, componentRenderer);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> status(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return text(header == null ? "Status" : header, valueProvider).kind(Kind.STATUS);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> enabled(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return text(header == null ? "Enabled" : header, valueProvider).kind(Kind.ENABLED);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> group(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return text(header == null ? "Group" : header, valueProvider).kind(Kind.GROUP);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> name(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return text(header == null ? "Name" : header, valueProvider).kind(Kind.NAME);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> app(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    return text(header, valueProvider).kind(Kind.APP);
  }

  public static <T> StitchGridColumn<T> timestamp(String header, ValueProvider<T, ?> valueProvider) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(valueProvider, "valueProvider");
    return StitchGridColumn.<T>text(
            header == null ? "Timestamp" : header,
            (T item) -> formatTimestampValue(valueProvider.apply(item)))
        .kind(Kind.TIMESTAMP);
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> key(String value) {
    key = value == null ? null : value.trim();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> sortable(boolean value) {
    sortable = value;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> autoWidth(boolean value) {
    autoWidth = value;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> flexGrow(int value) {
    flexGrow = Math.max(0, value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> resizable(boolean value) {
    resizable = value;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> width(String value) {
    width = value == null ? null : value.trim();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> frozen(boolean value) {
    frozen = value;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> kind(Kind value) {
    kind = value == null ? Kind.APP : value;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchGridColumn<T> enumLikeBadges(boolean value) {
    enumLikeBadges = value;
    return this;
  }

  public Kind kind() {
    return kind;
  }

  Grid.Column<T> applyTo(Grid<T> grid) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(grid, "grid");
    Grid.Column<T> column;
    if (renderer != null) {
      column = grid.addColumn(renderer);
    } else {
      ValueProvider<T, ?> provider = Objects.requireNonNull(valueProvider, "valueProvider");
      column =
          grid.addColumn(
              new ComponentRenderer<Component, T>(
                  item -> renderValue(provider.apply(item), enumLikeBadges)));
      column.setComparator(item -> sortableText(provider.apply(item)));
    }
    column.setHeader(header);
    column.setAutoWidth(autoWidth);
    column.setFlexGrow(flexGrow);
    column.setSortable(sortable);
    column.setResizable(resizable);
    column.setFrozen(frozen);
    if (key != null && !key.isBlank()) {
      column.setKey(key);
    }
    if (width != null && !width.isBlank()) {
      column.setWidth(width);
    }
    return column;
  }

  private static Component renderValue(Object value, boolean enumLikeBadges) {
    String normalized = sortableText(value);
    if (enumLikeBadges && isEnumLikeValue(value, normalized)) {
      return StitchStatusBadge.forValue(normalized);
    }
    Span span = new Span(displayText(normalized));
    span.addClassName("stitch-grid-value");
    return span;
  }

  private static boolean isEnumLikeValue(Object value, String text) {
    if (value instanceof Enum<?>) {
      return true;
    }
    if (text == null || text.isBlank() || text.length() > 32 || text.contains("|")) {
      return false;
    }
    boolean hasLetter = false;
    for (int i = 0; i < text.length(); i++) {
      char ch = text.charAt(i);
      if (Character.isLetter(ch)) {
        hasLetter = true;
        if (Character.isLowerCase(ch)) {
          return false;
        }
        continue;
      }
      if (Character.isDigit(ch) || ch == '_' || ch == '-' || ch == ' ') {
        continue;
      }
      return false;
    }
    return hasLetter;
  }

  private static String sortableText(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (value instanceof Enum<?> enumValue) {
      return enumValue.name();
    }
    return value.toString().trim();
  }

  private static String displayText(String normalized) {
    return normalized == null || normalized.isBlank() ? "-" : normalized;
  }

  private static String formatTimestampValue(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    if (value instanceof Instant instant) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(instant);
    }
    if (value instanceof ZonedDateTime zonedDateTime) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(zonedDateTime.toInstant());
    }
    if (value instanceof OffsetDateTime offsetDateTime) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(offsetDateTime.toInstant());
    }
    if (value instanceof LocalDateTime localDateTime) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(localDateTime.toInstant(ZoneOffset.UTC));
    }
    if (value instanceof Date date) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(date.toInstant());
    }
    if (value instanceof Long epochMillis) {
      return UTC_SECONDS.format(Instant.ofEpochMilli(epochMillis));
    }
    return value.toString().trim();
  }

  private static String normalizeHeader(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "";
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      return "";
    }
    return trimmed.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public enum Kind {
    STATUS,
    ENABLED,
    GROUP,
    NAME,
    APP,
    TIMESTAMP,
    ACTIONS
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/grid/StitchRowActions.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.JustifyContentMode;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.data.renderer.ComponentRenderer;
import com.vaadin.flow.function.SerializableConsumer;
import com.vaadin.flow.function.SerializablePredicate;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionIcons;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchRowActions<T> {
  private final List<Action<T>> actions = new ArrayList<>();

  public StitchRowActions<T> addAction(String label, SerializableConsumer<T> onClick) {
    return addAction(Action.of(label, onClick));
  }

  public StitchRowActions<T> addAction(Action<T> action) {
    actions.add(Objects.requireNonNull(action, "action"));
    return this;
  }

  public Grid.Column<T> addColumn(Grid<T> grid) {
    return addColumn(grid, "");
  }

  public Grid.Column<T> addColumn(Grid<T> grid, String header) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(grid, "grid");
    Grid.Column<T> column = grid.addColumn(renderer());
    String normalizedHeader = header == null ? "" : header.trim();
    if (normalizedHeader.isBlank()) {
      Span accessibleHeader = new Span("Actions");
      accessibleHeader.addClassName("stitch-visually-hidden");
      column.setHeader(accessibleHeader);
      column.getElement().setProperty("ariaLabel", "Actions");
    } else {
      column.setHeader(normalizedHeader);
    }
    column.setAutoWidth(false);
    column.setWidth(columnWidth(actions.size()));
    column.setFlexGrow(0);
    column.setResizable(false);
    column.setSortable(false);
    if (grid instanceof StitchGrid<T> stitchGrid) {
      stitchGrid.registerActionsColumn(column);
    }
    return column;
  }

  public ComponentRenderer<HorizontalLayout, T> renderer() {
    return new ComponentRenderer<>(this::render);
  }

  private HorizontalLayout render(T item) {
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout();
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(false);
    row.setWidthFull();
    row.setJustifyContentMode(JustifyContentMode.END);
    row.getStyle().set("gap", "0.48rem");
    row.getStyle().set("display", "flex");
    row.getStyle().set("max-width", "100%");
    row.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    row.addClassName("stitch-row-actions");
    StitchComponents.withCode(row, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_ROW_ACTIONS);

    for (Action<T> action : actions) {
      Button button = createButton(action);
      button.addClassName("stitch-row-action-button");
      button.addClassName(resolveToneClass(action));
      button.getElement().setAttribute("title", action.tooltipText());
      button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", action.ariaLabel());
      button.setEnabled(action.enabledWhen().test(item));
      button.addClickListener(event -> action.onClick().accept(item));
      row.add(button);
    }
    return row;
  }

  private static <T> String resolveToneClass(Action<T> action) {
    String label = action == null ? "" : normalize(action.label());
    if (containsAny(label, "DETAIL", "DETAILS")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--info";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "DELETE", "REJECT", "ROLLBACK", "REMOVE")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--danger";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "RUN", "LIVE", "PLAY", "START")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--run";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "SAVE", "SUBMIT", "APPROVE")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--success";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "EDIT")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--edit";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "JSON", "PAYLOAD", "DOCUMENT", "RAW")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--json";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "ENTITLEMENT", "SHIELD", "SECURITY")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--link";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "RELATED", "LINK", "NAVIGATE", "OPEN RELATED")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--link";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "INSPECT", "INFO", "OPEN", "VIEW")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--info";
    }
    if (containsAny(label, "CANCEL", "CLOSE", "CLEAR")) {
      return "stitch-row-action--neutral";
    }
    return "stitch-row-action--info";
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  private static boolean containsAny(String value, String... patterns) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank() || patterns == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String pattern : patterns) {
      if (pattern != null && !pattern.isBlank() && value.contains(pattern)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static <T> Button createButton(Action<T> action) {
    Button button = new Button();
    button.setIcon(StitchActionIcons.forAction(action.label(), action.icon()));
    button.getThemeNames().remove("icon");
    button.getThemeNames().remove("tertiary-inline");
    button.getElement().setAttribute("type", "button");
    return button;
  }

  private static String columnWidth(int actionCount) {
    int normalized = Math.max(1, actionCount);
    double width = normalized * 2.25d + Math.max(0, normalized - 1) * 0.48d + 0.9d;
    return String.format(Locale.ROOT, "%.2frem", width);
  }

  public static final class Action<T> {
    private final String label;
    private final VaadinIcon icon;
    private final SerializableConsumer<T> onClick;
    private final SerializablePredicate<T> enabledWhen;
    private final ButtonVariant[] themeVariants;

    private Action(
        String label,
        VaadinIcon icon,
        SerializableConsumer<T> onClick,
        SerializablePredicate<T> enabledWhen,
        ButtonVariant[] themeVariants) {
      this.label = label;
      this.icon = icon;
      this.onClick = onClick;
      this.enabledWhen = enabledWhen;
      this.themeVariants = themeVariants;
    }

    public static <T> Action<T> of(String label, SerializableConsumer<T> onClick) {
      return new Action<>(
          normalizeLabel(label),
          null,
          Objects.requireNonNull(onClick, "onClick"),
          item -> true,
          new ButtonVariant[0]);
    }

    public static <T> Action<T> icon(VaadinIcon icon, String tooltip, SerializableConsumer<T> onClick) {
      return new Action<>(
          normalizeLabel(tooltip),
          Objects.requireNonNull(icon, "icon"),
          Objects.requireNonNull(onClick, "onClick"),
          item -> true,
          new ButtonVariant[0]);
    }

    public Action<T> enabledWhen(SerializablePredicate<T> predicate) {
      return new Action<>(
          label, icon, onClick, predicate == null ? item -> true : predicate, themeVariants);
    }

    public Action<T> withThemeVariants(ButtonVariant... variants) {
      ButtonVariant[] values = variants == null ? new ButtonVariant[0] : Arrays.copyOf(variants, variants.length);
      return new Action<>(label, icon, onClick, enabledWhen, values);
    }

    public String label() {
      return label;
    }

    public VaadinIcon icon() {
      return icon;
    }

    public SerializableConsumer<T> onClick() {
      return onClick;
    }

    public SerializablePredicate<T> enabledWhen() {
      return enabledWhen;
    }

    public ButtonVariant[] themeVariants() {
      return Arrays.copyOf(themeVariants, themeVariants.length);
    }

    public String tooltipText() {
      return label;
    }

    public String ariaLabel() {
      return label;
    }

    private static String normalizeLabel(String value) {
      String normalized = value == null ? "" : value.trim();
      return normalized.isEmpty() ? "Action" : normalized;
    }
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.help

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/help/StitchReferenceView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.help;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.dependency.CssImport;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.NotFoundException;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.PageTitle;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.Route;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout.StitchShellLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

@Route(value = StitchReferenceView.ROUTE, layout = StitchShellLayout.class)
@PageTitle("Stitch Reference")
@CssImport("./themes/stitch/reference.css")
public class StitchReferenceView extends VerticalLayout {
  public static final String ROUTE = "stitch/reference";

  public StitchReferenceView(StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext) {
    if (runtimeContext == null || !runtimeContext.settings().help().referenceEnabled()) {
      throw new NotFoundException();
    }
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setSizeFull();
    addClassName("stitch-reference-view");

    StitchPage page =
        new StitchPage(
            "Stitch Reference",
            "Visual screen map of the current layout with component names and stable codes.");

    StitchSection map = new StitchSection("Main Screen Map");
    map.addToBody(buildScreenMap());

    StitchSection codes = new StitchSection("Component Codes");
    Grid<CodeRow> grid = new Grid<>(CodeRow.class, false);
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.addColumn(CodeRow::code).setHeader("CODE").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(0);
    grid.addColumn(CodeRow::region).setHeader("REGION").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(1);
    grid.addColumn(CodeRow::extensionPoint).setHeader("EXTENSION POINT").setAutoWidth(true).setFlexGrow(2);
    grid.setItems(referenceRows());
    codes.addToBody(grid);

    page.addToBody(map, codes);
    add(page);
    setFlexGrow(1, page);
  }

  private static Component buildScreenMap() {
    Div map = new Div();
    map.addClassName("stitch-reference-map");

    Div shellHeader =
        panel(
            "Top Shell Header",
            StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_HEADER,
            row(
                node("Brand (logo + title)", null, "stitch-reference-col-2"),
                node("Navigation Menu", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_NAVIGATION, "stitch-reference-col-3"),
                node("User Area / SSO Spoof", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_USER_AREA, "stitch-reference-col-2")));

    Div pageHeader =
        panel(
            "Page Header",
            StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE,
            panel(
                "Header",
                StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_HEADER,
            row(
                stack(
                    node("Page Title", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_TITLE),
                    node("Page Subtitle", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_SUBTITLE)),
                node("Page Actions", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_ACTIONS, "stitch-reference-col-2"))));

    Div resultsBlock =
        panel(
            "Results Block",
            StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_VIEW,
            panel(
                "Results Toolbar",
                StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_TOOLBAR,
                row(
                    node("Toolbar Start", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_TOOLBAR_START),
                    node("Toolbar Filters/Search", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_TOOLBAR_FILTERS),
                    node("Toolbar End", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_TOOLBAR_END))),
            panel(
                "Results Area",
                StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_AREA,
                row(
                    node("Results Grid", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_GRID),
                    node("Empty State", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_EMPTY_STATE),
                    node("Row Actions", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_ROW_ACTIONS),
                    node("Status Badge", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_STATUS_BADGE))),
            panel(
                "Results Footer",
                StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_FOOTER,
                row(
                    node("Footer Start", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_FOOTER_START),
                    node("Pagination", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGINATION),
                    node("Page Info", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGE_INFO),
                    node("Page Size", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_PAGE_SIZE),
                    node("Results Count", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_COUNT))));

    Div section =
        panel(
            "Section",
            null,
            row(
                node("Section Header", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_HEADER, "stitch-reference-col-3"),
                node("Section Actions", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_ACTIONS, "stitch-reference-col-2")),
            panel(
                "Section Body",
                StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SECTION_BODY,
                node("Tabs", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TABS),
                node("Tab Panel", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TAB_PANEL),
                resultsBlock));

    Div pageBody = panel("Page Body", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_BODY, section);
    Div shellContent = panel("Shell Content", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_CONTENT, pageHeader, pageBody);

    Div dialog =
        panel(
            "Dialog Overlay (Optional)",
            null,
            node("Dialog Header", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_HEADER),
            node("Dialog Body", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_BODY),
            row(
                node("Dialog Footer", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_FOOTER, "stitch-reference-col-2"),
                node("Primary Action", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_PRIMARY_ACTION),
                node("Secondary Action", StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_DIALOG_SECONDARY_ACTION)));

    map.add(shellHeader, shellContent, dialog);
    return map;
  }

  private static Div panel(String title, String code, Component... children) {
    Div panel = new Div();
    panel.addClassName("stitch-reference-panel");

    Div header = new Div();
    header.addClassName("stitch-reference-panel-head");

    Span name = new Span(title == null ? "" : title);
    name.addClassName("stitch-reference-panel-title");
    header.add(name);

    if (code != null && !code.isBlank()) {
      header.add(codeChip(code));
    }

    Div body = new Div();
    body.addClassName("stitch-reference-panel-body");
    if (children != null) {
      body.add(children);
    }

    panel.add(header, body);
    return panel;
  }

  private static Div row(Component... children) {
    Div row = new Div();
    row.addClassName("stitch-reference-row");
    if (children != null) {
      row.add(children);
    }
    return row;
  }

  private static Div stack(Component... children) {
    Div stack = new Div();
    stack.addClassName("stitch-reference-stack");
    if (children != null) {
      stack.add(children);
    }
    return stack;
  }

  private static Div node(String label, String code, String... extraClasses) {
    Div node = new Div();
    node.addClassName("stitch-reference-node");
    if (extraClasses != null) {
      node.addClassNames(extraClasses);
    }
    Span name = new Span(label == null ? "" : label);
    name.addClassName("stitch-reference-node-label");
    node.add(name);
    if (code != null && !code.isBlank()) {
      node.add(codeChip(code));
    }
    return node;
  }

  private static Span codeChip(String code) {
    Span chip = new Span(code == null ? "" : code);
    chip.addClassName("stitch-reference-code");
    return chip;
  }

  private static List<CodeRow> referenceRows() {
    return List.of(
        new CodeRow(StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_HEADER, "Shell Header", "Branding, title, top chrome"),

}



org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/layout/StitchShellLayout.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.layout;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.applayout.AppLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.contextmenu.MenuItem;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.contextmenu.SubMenu;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Image;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.icon.VaadinIcon;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.menubar.MenuBar;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.AfterNavigationEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.AfterNavigationObserver;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.RouteConfiguration;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.help.StitchReferenceView;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchShellUserArea;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuItem;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu.StitchMenuProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeHeaderStatus;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime.StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchShellLayout extends AppLayout implements AfterNavigationObserver {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext context;
  private final List<StitchMenuItem> topItems;
  private final boolean debugToggleEnabled;
  private boolean debugAnnotationsVisible;
  private Button debugToggleButton;

  public StitchShellLayout(
      StitchRuntimeContext context,
      Optional<StitchMenuProvider> provider,
      Optional<StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry> realtimeRegistry) {
    this.context = Objects.requireNonNull(context, "context");
    this.debugToggleEnabled = context.settings().help().referenceEnabled();
    this.debugAnnotationsVisible = false;
    List<StitchMenuItem> provided =
        provider == null || provider.isEmpty() ? List.of() : safe(provider.get().items());
    this.topItems = sortMenus(withHelpMenu(provided, context.settings().help()), true);

    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_CONTENT);

    Span brandTitle = new Span(context.appTitle());
    HorizontalLayout brand = new HorizontalLayout();
    brand.setPadding(false);
    brand.setSpacing(true);
    brand.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    brand.addClassName("stitch-shell-brand");
    String logoPath = context.settings().shell().brandLogoPath();
    if (logoPath != null && !logoPath.isBlank()) {
      String logoAlt = context.settings().shell().brandLogoAlt();
      Image logo = new Image(logoPath, logoAlt == null || logoAlt.isBlank() ? context.appTitle() : logoAlt);
      logo.addClassName("stitch-brand-logo");
      brand.add(logo);
    }
    brand.add(brandTitle);

    MenuBar nav = buildNavigation();
    nav.addClassName("stitch-shell-navigation");
    nav.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Primary navigation");
    StitchComponents.withCode(nav, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_NAVIGATION);

    List<Component> userAreaItems = new ArrayList<>();
    userAreaItems.add(StitchShellUserArea.create(context));
    realtimeRegistry.ifPresent(registry -> userAreaItems.add(new StitchRealtimeHeaderStatus(registry)));
    if (debugToggleEnabled) {
      userAreaItems.add(buildDebugToggleButton());
    }
    HorizontalLayout userArea = new HorizontalLayout(userAreaItems.toArray(Component[]::new));
    userArea.setPadding(false);
    userArea.setSpacing(true);
    userArea.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    userArea.addClassName("stitch-shell-user-area");
    StitchComponents.withCode(userArea, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_USER_AREA);

    Div spacer = new Div();
    HorizontalLayout header = new HorizontalLayout(brand, nav, spacer, userArea);
    header.setPadding(false);
    header.setSpacing(true);
    header.setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    header.setWidthFull();
    header.expand(spacer);
    header.addClassName("stitch-shell-header");
    header.getElement().setAttribute("role", "banner");
    StitchComponents.withCode(header, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_HEADER);

    addToNavbar(header);
    addAttachListener(event -> applyDebugAnnotations());
  }

  @Override
  public void afterNavigation(AfterNavigationEvent event) {
    String appTitle = Strings.trimToNull(context.appTitle());
    String fixedTitle = appTitle == null ? "Stitch Application" : appTitle;
    getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui ->
                ui.beforeClientResponse(
                    this,
                    context -> {
                      ui.getPage().setTitle(fixedTitle);
                    }));
  }

  private MenuBar buildNavigation() {
    MenuBar menu = new MenuBar();
    menu.setOpenOnHover(true);
    for (StitchMenuItem top : topItems) {
      MenuItem topMenu = menu.addItem(top.label());
      if (top.hasChildren()) {
        for (StitchMenuItem child : sortMenus(top.children(), false)) {
          addChild(topMenu.getSubMenu(), child);
        }
      } else {
        topMenu.addClickListener(event -> navigate(top));
      }
    }
    return menu;
  }

  private void addChild(SubMenu parent, StitchMenuItem item) {
    if (item == null) {
      return;
    }
    MenuItem child =
        parent.addItem(
            item.label(),
            event -> {
              if (!item.hasChildren()) {
                navigate(item);
              }
            });
    if (!item.hasChildren()) {
      return;
    }
    for (StitchMenuItem nested : sortMenus(item.children(), false)) {
      addChild(child.getSubMenu(), nested);
    }
  }

  private void navigate(StitchMenuItem item) {
    if (item == null) {
      return;
    }
    getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui -> {
              if (item.routeTarget() != null) {
                ui.navigate(item.routeTarget());
                return;
              }
              String path = resolveRoutePath(item);
              if (path != null) {
                ui.navigate(path);
              }
            });
  }

  private static List<StitchMenuItem> withHelpMenu(List<StitchMenuItem> items, StitchSettings.Help help) {
    if (help == null || !help.menuEnabled()) {
      return List.copyOf(safe(items));
    }
    List<StitchMenuItem> merged = new ArrayList<>(safe(items));
    StitchMenuItem docsEntry = extractDocsEntryForHelp(merged);
    StitchMenuItem referenceEntry =
        help.referenceEnabled() && isRouteRegistered(StitchReferenceView.class)
            ? StitchMenuItem.builder("stitch-reference")
                .withLabel("Stitch Reference")
                .withRoutePath(StitchReferenceView.ROUTE)
                .withOrder(10)
                .build()
            : null;

    int helpIndex = findHelpMenuIndex(merged);
    if (helpIndex < 0) {
      if (docsEntry == null && referenceEntry == null) {
        return List.copyOf(merged);
      }
      List<StitchMenuItem> children = new ArrayList<>();
      if (docsEntry != null) {
        children.add(docsEntry);
      }
      if (referenceEntry != null) {
        children.add(referenceEntry);
      }
      merged.add(
          StitchMenuItem.builder("help")
              .withLabel("Help")
              .withOrder(9999)
              .withChildren(sortMenus(children, false))
              .build());
      return List.copyOf(merged);
    }

    StitchMenuItem helpMenu = merged.get(helpIndex);
    List<StitchMenuItem> children = new ArrayList<>(safe(helpMenu.children()));
    if (docsEntry != null) {
      children.removeIf(StitchShellLayout::isDocsMenu);
      children.add(docsEntry);
    }
    if (referenceEntry != null) {
      children.removeIf(
          item -> item != null && "stitch-reference".equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(item.id(), "")));
      children.add(referenceEntry);
    }
    StitchMenuItem.Builder rebuilt =
        StitchMenuItem.builder(helpMenu.id())
            .withLabel(helpMenu.label())
            .withOrder(helpMenu.order())
            .withChildren(sortMenus(children, false));
    if (helpMenu.routePath() != null) {
      rebuilt.withRoutePath(helpMenu.routePath());
    }
    if (helpMenu.routeTarget() != null) {
      rebuilt.withRouteTarget(helpMenu.routeTarget());
    }
    if (helpMenu.iconKey() != null) {
      rebuilt.withIconKey(helpMenu.iconKey());
    }
    merged.set(helpIndex, rebuilt.build());
    return List.copyOf(merged);
  }

  private static int findHelpMenuIndex(List<StitchMenuItem> items) {
    for (int i = 0; i < items.size(); i++) {
      StitchMenuItem item = items.get(i);
      if (item == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if ("help".equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(item.id(), ""))
          || "help".equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.firstNonBlank(item.label(), ""))) {
        return i;
      }
    }
    return -1;
  }

  private static StitchMenuItem extractDocsEntryForHelp(List<StitchMenuItem> items) {
    for (int i = 0; i < items.size(); i++) {
      StitchMenuItem item = items.get(i);
      if (!isDocsMenu(item)) {
        continue;
      }
      items.remove(i);
      return toHelpDocsEntry(item);
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean isDocsMenu(StitchMenuItem item) {
    if (item == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String id = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(item.id()), "");
    String label = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(item.label()), "");
    return id.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("docs") || "docs".equalsIgnoreCase(label);
  }

  private static StitchMenuItem toHelpDocsEntry(StitchMenuItem docsMenu) {
    if (docsMenu == null) {
      return null;
    }
    StitchMenuItem routeSource = firstRoutableItem(docsMenu);
    StitchMenuItem.Builder docsEntry =
        StitchMenuItem.builder("help-docs").withLabel("Docs").withOrder(5);
    if (routeSource != null) {
      if (routeSource.routePath() != null) {
        docsEntry.withRoutePath(routeSource.routePath());
      } else if (routeSource.routeTarget() != null) {
        docsEntry.withRouteTarget(routeSource.routeTarget());
      }
      return docsEntry.build();
    }
    if (docsMenu.hasChildren()) {
      docsEntry.withChildren(sortMenus(docsMenu.children(), false));
      return docsEntry.build();
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static StitchMenuItem firstRoutableItem(StitchMenuItem item) {
    if (item == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (item.routePath() != null || item.routeTarget() != null) {
      return item;
    }
    for (StitchMenuItem child : sortMenus(item.children(), false)) {
      StitchMenuItem resolved = firstRoutableItem(child);
      if (resolved != null) {
        return resolved;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean isRouteRegistered(Class<? extends Component> target) {
    try {
      RouteConfiguration.forApplicationScope().getUrl(target);
      return true;
    } catch (Exception error) {
      return false;
    }
  }

  private Button buildDebugToggleButton() {
    Button toggle = new Button(VaadinIcon.CODE.create(), event -> toggleDebugAnnotations());
    toggle.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    toggle.addClassName("stitch-shell-debug-toggle");
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Toggle component annotations");
    toggle.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Toggle component annotations");
    StitchComponents.withCode(toggle, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_DEBUG_TOGGLE);
    this.debugToggleButton = toggle;
    updateDebugToggleState();
    return toggle;
  }

  private void toggleDebugAnnotations() {
    debugAnnotationsVisible = !debugAnnotationsVisible;
    updateDebugToggleState();
    applyDebugAnnotations();
  }

  private void updateDebugToggleState() {
    if (debugToggleButton == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (debugAnnotationsVisible) {
      debugToggleButton.addClassName("stitch-active");
    } else {
      debugToggleButton.removeClassName("stitch-active");
    }
  }

  private void applyDebugAnnotations() {
    if (!debugToggleEnabled) {
      return;
    }
    getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui ->
                ui.getPage()
                    .executeJs(
                        """
                        (() => {
                          const enabled = Boolean($0);
                          const root = document.documentElement;
                          const mouseKey = '__stitchDebugMouseMoveHandler';
                          const clickKey = '__stitchDebugCopyClickHandler';
                          const toastKey = '__stitchDebugCopyToast';
                          const toastTimerKey = '__stitchDebugCopyToastTimer';
                          const annotationSelector = '.stitch-debug-labeled[data-stitch-debug-tooltip]';

                          if (!window[mouseKey]) {
                            window[mouseKey] = (event) => {
                              root.style.setProperty('--stitch-debug-mouse-x', `${event.clientX}px`);
                              root.style.setProperty('--stitch-debug-mouse-y', `${event.clientY}px`);
                            };
                          }

                          const resolveAnnotatedElement = (event) => {
                            const path = typeof event.composedPath === 'function' ? event.composedPath() : [];
                            for (const node of path) {
                              if (!(node instanceof Element)) {
                                continue;
                              }
                              if (node.matches && node.matches('.stitch-shell-debug-toggle')) {
                                return null;
                              }
                              if (node.matches && node.matches(annotationSelector)) {
                                return node;
                              }
                            }
                            if (!(event.target instanceof Element)) {
                              return null;
                            }
                            if (event.target.closest('.stitch-shell-debug-toggle')) {
                              return null;
                            }
                            return event.target.closest(annotationSelector);
                          };

                          const showToast = (message, success, x, y) => {
                            let toast = window[toastKey];
                            if (!(toast instanceof HTMLElement)) {
                              toast = document.createElement('div');
                              toast.style.position = 'fixed';
                              toast.style.zIndex = '2147483647';
                              toast.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
                              toast.style.padding = '0.18rem 0.46rem';
                              toast.style.borderRadius = '5px';
                              toast.style.border = '1px solid';
                              toast.style.fontSize = '0.7rem';
                              toast.style.fontWeight = '600';
                              toast.style.lineHeight = '1.2';
                              toast.style.maxWidth = 'calc(100vw - 1rem)';
                              toast.style.whiteSpace = 'nowrap';
                              toast.style.overflow = 'hidden';
                              toast.style.textOverflow = 'ellipsis';
                              toast.style.opacity = '0';
                              toast.style.transition = 'opacity 120ms ease';
                              document.body.appendChild(toast);
                              window[toastKey] = toast;
                            }
                            if (window[toastTimerKey]) {
                              clearTimeout(window[toastTimerKey]);
                            }
                            toast.textContent = message;
                            toast.style.background = success ? 'rgba(13, 17, 23, 0.96)' : 'rgba(87, 0, 0, 0.96)';
                            toast.style.borderColor =
                                success ? 'rgba(88, 166, 255, 0.42)' : 'rgba(248, 81, 73, 0.55)';
                            toast.style.color = success ? '#8ab4ff' : '#ffd7d5';
                            toast.style.left = `${Math.max(8, x + 14)}px`;
                            toast.style.top = `${Math.max(8, y + 14)}px`;
                            requestAnimationFrame(() => {
                              toast.style.opacity = '1';
                            });
                            window[toastTimerKey] = window.setTimeout(() => {
                              toast.style.opacity = '0';
                            }, 950);
                          };

                          const copyToClipboard = async (text) => {
                            if (!text) {
                              return false;
                            }
                            try {
                              if (navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext) {
                                await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
                                return true;
                              }
                            } catch (ignore) {
                              // fall through to textarea fallback
                            }
                            try {
                              const textarea = document.createElement('textarea');
                              textarea.value = text;
                              textarea.setAttribute('readonly', '');
                              textarea.style.position = 'fixed';
                              textarea.style.top = '0';
                              textarea.style.left = '-9999px';
                              textarea.style.opacity = '0';
                              document.body.appendChild(textarea);
                              textarea.focus();
                              textarea.select();
                              const ok = document.execCommand('copy');
                              document.body.removeChild(textarea);
                              return Boolean(ok);
                            } catch (ignore) {
                              return false;
                            }
                          };

                          if (!window[clickKey]) {
                            window[clickKey] = async (event) => {
                              if (!root.classList.contains('stitch-debug-annotations-on')) {
                                return;
                              }
                              const element = resolveAnnotatedElement(event);
                              if (!element) {
                                return;
                              }
                              const value =
                                  (element.getAttribute('data-stitch-debug-tooltip') ||
                                      element.getAttribute('data-stitch-code') ||
                                      '')
                                      .trim();
                              if (!value) {
                                return;
                              }
                              event.preventDefault();
                              event.stopPropagation();
                              event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                              const copied = await copyToClipboard(value);
                              showToast(
                                  copied ? `Copied: ${value}` : `Copy failed: ${value}`,
                                  copied,
                                  event.clientX || 0,
                                  event.clientY || 0);
                            };
                          }

                          const mouseHandler = window[mouseKey];
                          const clickHandler = window[clickKey];
                          document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseHandler);
                          document.removeEventListener('click', clickHandler, true);
                          if (enabled) {
                            document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseHandler, { passive: true });
                            document.addEventListener('click', clickHandler, true);
                          } else {
                            root.style.removeProperty('--stitch-debug-mouse-x');
                            root.style.removeProperty('--stitch-debug-mouse-y');
                            const toast = window[toastKey];
                            if (toast instanceof HTMLElement) {
                              toast.remove();
                            }
                            window[toastKey] = null;
                            if (window[toastTimerKey]) {
                              clearTimeout(window[toastTimerKey]);
                            }
                            window[toastTimerKey] = null;
                          }
                          root.classList.toggle('stitch-debug-annotations-on', enabled);
                        })();
                        """,
                        debugAnnotationsVisible));
  }

  private static List<StitchMenuItem> sortMenus(List<StitchMenuItem> values, boolean topLevel) {
    List<StitchMenuItem> sorted = new ArrayList<>(safe(values));
    sorted.sort(
        Comparator.comparingInt(StitchMenuItem::order)
            .thenComparing(item -> item.label().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    if (!topLevel) {
      return List.copyOf(sorted);
    }
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private String resolveRoutePath(StitchMenuItem item) {
    if (item == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String direct = normalizePath(item.routePath());
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    Class<? extends Component> target = item.routeTarget();
    if (target == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return normalizePath(RouteConfiguration.forApplicationScope().getUrl(target));
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static String normalizePath(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    while (normalized.startsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(1);
    }
    while (normalized.endsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static List<StitchMenuItem> safe(List<StitchMenuItem> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return values.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/menu/StitchMenuContributionRegistry.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;

public final class StitchMenuContributionRegistry {
  private final Map<StitchMenuEntryId, StitchMenuEntry> entriesById;

  public StitchMenuContributionRegistry(List<? extends StitchMenuEntry> entries) {
    LinkedHashMap<StitchMenuEntryId, StitchMenuEntry> resolved = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    if (entries != null) {
      for (StitchMenuEntry entry : entries) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        StitchMenuEntry existing = resolved.putIfAbsent(entry.id(), entry);
        if (existing != null) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Duplicate menu entry id: " + entry.id().value());
        }
      }
    }
    this.entriesById = Map.copyOf(resolved);
  }

  public static StitchMenuContributionRegistry empty() {
    return new StitchMenuContributionRegistry(List.of());
  }

  public List<StitchMenuEntry> entries() {
    return List.copyOf(entriesById.values());
  }

  public Optional<StitchMenuEntry> entry(String id) {
    if (id == null || id.isBlank()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(entriesById.get(StitchMenuEntryId.of(id)));
  }

  public StitchMenuEntry requireEntry(String id) {
    return entry(id)
        .orElseThrow(
            () ->
                new IllegalStateException(
                    "Menu entry not found for id: "
                        + Objects.requireNonNullElse(id, "")
                            .trim()
                            .toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
  }

  public List<StitchMenuItem> resolveEntries(List<String> ids) {
    if (ids == null || ids.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchMenuItem> resolved = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String id : ids) {
      StitchMenuEntry entry = requireEntry(id);
      StitchMenuItem.Builder builder =
          StitchMenuItem.builder(entry.id().value())
              .withLabel(entry.label())
              .withOrder(entry.order());
      if (entry.routePath() != null) {
        builder.withRoutePath(entry.routePath());
      }
      if (entry.routeTarget() != null) {
        builder.withRouteTarget(entry.routeTarget());
      }
      if (entry.iconKey() != null) {
        builder.withIconKey(entry.iconKey());
      }
      resolved.add(builder.build());
    }
    return List.copyOf(resolved);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/menu/StitchMenuEntry.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;

public final class StitchMenuEntry {
  private final StitchMenuEntryId id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final Class<? extends Component> routeTarget;
  private final String iconKey;
  private final int order;

  private StitchMenuEntry(Builder builder) {
    this.id = StitchMenuEntryId.of(builder.id);
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = optional(builder.routePath);
    this.routeTarget = builder.routeTarget;
    this.iconKey = optional(builder.iconKey);
    this.order = builder.order;
    if (routePath == null && routeTarget == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Menu entry must define routePath or routeTarget");
    }
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public StitchMenuEntryId id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public Class<? extends Component> routeTarget() {
    return routeTarget;
  }

  public String iconKey() {
    return iconKey;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private Class<? extends Component> routeTarget;
    private String iconKey;
    private int order;

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = require(id, "id");
      this.label = id;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = require(value, "label");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = require(value, "routePath");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRouteTarget(Class<? extends Component> value) {
      this.routeTarget = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withIconKey(String value) {
      this.iconKey = optional(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchMenuEntry build() {
      return new StitchMenuEntry(this);
    }
  }
}
