package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class StitchMenuEntryId {
  private final String value;

  private StitchMenuEntryId(String value) {
    this.value = normalize(value);
  }

  public static StitchMenuEntryId of(String value) {
    return new StitchMenuEntryId(value);
  }

  public String value() {
    return value;
  }

  @Override
  public String toString() {
    return value;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean equals(Object value) {
    if (this == value) {
      return true;
    }
    if (!(value instanceof StitchMenuEntryId other)) {
      return false;
    }
    return this.value.equals(other.value);
  }

  @Override
  public int hashCode() {
    return Objects.hash(value);
  }

  private static String normalize(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("id is required");
    }
    return value.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/menu/StitchMenuItem.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class StitchMenuItem {
  private final String id;
  private final String label;
  private final String routePath;
  private final Class<? extends Component> routeTarget;
  private final String iconKey;
  private final int order;
  private final List<StitchMenuItem> children;

  private StitchMenuItem(Builder builder) {
    this.id = require(builder.id, "id");
    this.label = require(builder.label, "label");
    this.routePath = optional(builder.routePath);
    this.routeTarget = builder.routeTarget;
    this.iconKey = optional(builder.iconKey);
    this.order = builder.order;
    this.children = List.copyOf(builder.children);
    if (this.routePath == null && this.routeTarget == null && this.children.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Menu item must define routePath, routeTarget, or children");
    }
  }

  public static Builder builder(String id) {
    return new Builder(id);
  }

  public String id() {
    return id;
  }

  public String label() {
    return label;
  }

  public String routePath() {
    return routePath;
  }

  public Class<? extends Component> routeTarget() {
    return routeTarget;
  }

  public String iconKey() {
    return iconKey;
  }

  public int order() {
    return order;
  }

  public List<StitchMenuItem> children() {
    return children;
  }

  public boolean hasChildren() {
    return !children.isEmpty();
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final String id;
    private String label;
    private String routePath;
    private Class<? extends Component> routeTarget;
    private String iconKey;
    private int order;
    private final List<StitchMenuItem> children = new ArrayList<>();

    private Builder(String id) {
      this.id = id;
      this.label = id;
    }

    public Builder withLabel(String value) {
      this.label = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutePath(String value) {
      this.routePath = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRouteTarget(Class<? extends Component> value) {
      this.routeTarget = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withIconKey(String value) {
      this.iconKey = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOrder(int value) {
      this.order = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withChildren(List<StitchMenuItem> values) {
      this.children.clear();
      if (values != null) {
        this.children.addAll(values.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList());
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addChild(StitchMenuItem value) {
      if (value != null) {
        this.children.add(value);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public StitchMenuItem build() {
      return new StitchMenuItem(this);
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/menu/StitchMenuNodeBuilder.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

abstract class StitchMenuNodeBuilder<T extends StitchMenuNodeBuilder<T>> {
  private final String id;
  private String label;
  private Integer order;
  private String iconKey;
  private String entryRef;
  private final List<String> entryRefs = new ArrayList<>();
  private final List<StitchSubmenuBuilder> submenus = new ArrayList<>();

  protected StitchMenuNodeBuilder(String id) {
    this.id = require(id, "id");
  }

  protected abstract T self();

  public T withLabel(String value) {
    this.label = require(value, "label");
    return self();
  }

  public T withOrder(int value) {
    this.order = value;
    return self();
  }

  public T withIconKey(String value) {
    this.iconKey = optional(value);
    return self();
  }

  public T withEntry(String entryId) {
    this.entryRef = normalizeEntryId(entryId);
    return self();
  }

  public T add(String entryId) {
    this.entryRefs.add(normalizeEntryId(entryId));
    return self();
  }

  public T submenu(String id, Consumer<StitchSubmenuBuilder> customizer) {
    StitchSubmenuBuilder builder = new StitchSubmenuBuilder(id);
    if (customizer != null) {
      customizer.accept(builder);
    }
    submenus.add(builder);
    return self();
  }

  final void collectEntryRefs(Set<String> output) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(output, "output");
    if (entryRef != null) {
      output.add(entryRef);
    }
    output.addAll(entryRefs);
    for (StitchSubmenuBuilder submenu : submenus) {
      submenu.collectEntryRefs(output);
    }
  }

  final StitchMenuItem build(StitchMenuContributionRegistry contributions) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(contributions, "contributions");
    if (entryRef != null) {
      if (!entryRefs.isEmpty() || !submenus.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Menu node '" + id + "' cannot define withEntry(...) and child entries/submenus");
      }
      return entryBackedNode(contributions);
    }

    List<StitchMenuItem> children = new ArrayList<>();
    children.addAll(contributions.resolveEntries(entryRefs));
    for (StitchSubmenuBuilder submenu : submenus) {
      children.add(submenu.build(contributions));
    }
    if (children.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Menu node '" + id + "' must define withEntry(...) or at least one child entry/submenu");
    }

    StitchMenuItem.Builder builder =
        StitchMenuItem.builder(id)
            .withLabel(resolveLabel())
            .withOrder(resolveOrder())
            .withChildren(children);
    if (iconKey != null) {
      builder.withIconKey(iconKey);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  private StitchMenuItem entryBackedNode(StitchMenuContributionRegistry contributions) {
    StitchMenuEntry entry = contributions.requireEntry(entryRef);
    StitchMenuItem.Builder builder =
        StitchMenuItem.builder(id)
            .withLabel(label == null ? entry.label() : label)
            .withOrder(order == null ? entry.order() : order);
    if (entry.routePath() != null) {
      builder.withRoutePath(entry.routePath());
    }
    if (entry.routeTarget() != null) {
      builder.withRouteTarget(entry.routeTarget());
    }
    String resolvedIcon = iconKey == null ? entry.iconKey() : iconKey;
    if (resolvedIcon != null) {
      builder.withIconKey(resolvedIcon);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  private String resolveLabel() {
    if (label != null) {
      return label;
    }
    if (!id.contains(".")) {
      return id;
    }
    String[] segments = id.split("\\.");
    String leaf = segments[segments.length - 1];
    if (leaf.isBlank()) {
      return id;
    }
    String normalized = leaf.replace('-', ' ');
    return Character.toUpperCase(normalized.charAt(0)) + normalized.substring(1);
  }

  private int resolveOrder() {
    return order == null ? 0 : order;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String normalizeEntryId(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("entryId is required");
    }
    return value.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/menu/StitchMenusBuilder.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.menu;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

public final class StitchMenusBuilder {
  private final List<StitchMenuBuilder> menus = new ArrayList<>();

  public StitchMenusBuilder menu(String id, Consumer<StitchMenuBuilder> customizer) {
    StitchMenuBuilder builder = new StitchMenuBuilder(id);
    if (customizer != null) {
      customizer.accept(builder);
    }
    menus.add(builder);
    return this;
  }

  public List<StitchMenuItem> build(StitchMenuContributionRegistry contributions) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(contributions, "contributions");
    if (menus.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<StitchMenuItem> built = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StitchMenuBuilder menu : menus) {
      built.add(menu.build(contributions));
    }
    return List.copyOf(built);
  }

  public Set<String> referencedEntryIds() {
    if (menus.isEmpty()) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> ids = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (StitchMenuBuilder menu : menus) {
      menu.collectEntryRefs(ids);
    }
    return Set.copyOf(ids);
  }

  public boolean isEmpty() {
    return menus.isEmpty();
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchEventLogShell.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

/** Shared append-only realtime event log shell with bounded retention and clear/reset support. */
public final class StitchEventLogShell<E> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar = new StitchRealtimeStatusBar();
  private final StitchSubscriptionControls controls = new StitchSubscriptionControls();
  private final StitchResultsView<E> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final ArrayDeque<E> events = new ArrayDeque<>();

  private int maxEvents = 500;

  public StitchEventLogShell() {
    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime event log shell");

    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(false);
    results.setResultCountVisible(true);
    results.setEmptyState("No events", "Start a subscription to receive events.");
    results.grid().setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.NONE);
    results.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime event log");

    controls.onClear(this::clearEvents);
    controls.clearEnabled(false);

    add(statusBar, controls, results);
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar() {
    return statusBar;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls controls() {
    return controls;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<E> resultsView() {
    return results;
  }

  public StitchEventLogShell<E> setMaxEvents(int value) {
    maxEvents = Math.max(10, value);
    trimToMax();
    refreshRows();
    return this;
  }

  public int maxEvents() {
    return maxEvents;
  }

  public void append(E event) {
    if (event == null) {
      return;
    }
    events.addFirst(event);
    trimToMax();
    refreshRows();
  }

  public void appendAll(Collection<E> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (E value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        events.addFirst(value);
      }
    }
    trimToMax();
    refreshRows();
  }

  public void clearEvents() {
    events.clear();
    refreshRows();
  }

  public List<E> events() {
    return List.copyOf(events);
  }

  public AutoCloseable bindController(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<E> controller) {
    return bindController(controller, null);
  }

  public AutoCloseable bindController(
      StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<E> controller,
      Consumer<List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<E>>> updatesObserver) {
    if (controller == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    Consumer<List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<E>>> observer =
        updatesObserver == null ? updates -> {} : updatesObserver;
    Registration statusRegistration = statusBar.bind(controller);
    Registration controlsRegistration = controls.bind(controller);
    AutoCloseable updatesHandle =
        controller.addListener(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<>() {
              @Override
              public void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<E>> updates) {
                if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
                  return;
                }
                runUi(
                    () -> {
                      List<E> append = new ArrayList<>();
                      for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<E> update : updates) {
                        if (update == null) {
                          continue;
                        }
                        if (update.kind() == StitchRealtimeUpdate.Kind.SNAPSHOT) {
                          events.clear();
                        }
                        if (update.kind() != StitchRealtimeUpdate.Kind.HEARTBEAT
                            && update.payload() != null) {
                          append.add(update.payload());
                        }
                      }
                      if (!append.isEmpty()) {
                        appendAll(append);
                      } else {
                        refreshRows();
                      }
                      observer.accept(updates);
                      statusBar.setLastUpdate(controller.lastUpdateAt());
                      statusBar.setDispatchMetrics(controller.dispatchMetrics());
                    });
              }
            });
    return () -> {
      StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(updatesHandle);
      statusRegistration.remove();
      controlsRegistration.remove();
    };
  }

  private void trimToMax() {
    while (events.size() > maxEvents) {
      events.removeLast();
    }
  }

  private void refreshRows() {
    List<E> snapshot = List.copyOf(events);
    results.setItems(snapshot);
    results.setEmpty(snapshot.isEmpty());
    controls.clearEnabled(!snapshot.isEmpty());
    statusBar.setMessage("Events retained: " + snapshot.size() + " / " + maxEvents);
    statusBar.setLastUpdate(Instant.now());
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(action::run);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchLiveTableChangeTracker.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.HashSet;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;

/**
 * Shared row/cell change-state tracker supporting temporary flash windows and persistent highlight
 * marks.
 */
public final class StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<RowId> {
  private final Set<RowId> transientRows = new HashSet<>();
  private final Set<RowId> persistentRows = new HashSet<>();
  private final Map<RowId, Set<String>> transientCells = new HashMap<>();
  private final Map<RowId, Set<String>> persistentCells = new HashMap<>();
  private final Map<RowId, Long> transientRowChangedAt = new HashMap<>();
  private final Map<RowId, Map<String, Long>> transientCellChangedAt = new HashMap<>();

  private StitchLiveTableHighlightMode mode = StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY;
  private Duration flashWindow = Duration.ofSeconds(2);

  public synchronized StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<RowId> setHighlightMode(
      StitchLiveTableHighlightMode value) {
    this.mode = value == null ? StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.NONE : value;
    return this;
  }

  public synchronized StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<RowId> setFlashWindow(Duration value) {
    if (value != null && !value.isNegative() && !value.isZero()) {
      this.flashWindow = value;
    }
    return this;
  }

  public synchronized StitchLiveTableHighlightMode highlightMode() {
    return mode;
  }

  public synchronized Duration flashWindow() {
    return flashWindow;
  }

  public synchronized void markRowChanged(RowId rowId) {
    if (rowId == null || mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.NONE) {
      return;
    }
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    if (usesTemporary()) {
      transientRows.add(rowId);
      transientRowChangedAt.put(rowId, now);
    }
    if (usesPersistent()) {
      persistentRows.add(rowId);
    }
  }

  public synchronized void markCellChanged(RowId rowId, String cellKey) {
    if (rowId == null || mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.NONE) {
      return;
    }
    String normalizedCell = normalizeCell(cellKey);
    if (normalizedCell == null) {
      return;
    }
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    if (usesTemporary()) {
      transientCells.computeIfAbsent(rowId, ignored -> new HashSet<>()).add(normalizedCell);
      transientCellChangedAt
          .computeIfAbsent(rowId, ignored -> new HashMap<>())
          .put(normalizedCell, now);
    }
    if (usesPersistent()) {
      persistentCells.computeIfAbsent(rowId, ignored -> new HashSet<>()).add(normalizedCell);
    }
  }

  public synchronized Set<RowId> changedRows() {
    pruneExpired();
    Set<RowId> changed = new HashSet<>(persistentRows);
    changed.addAll(transientRows);
    return Set.copyOf(changed);
  }

  public synchronized int changedRowCount() {
    return changedRows().size();
  }

  public synchronized Set<String> changedCells(RowId rowId) {
    pruneExpired();
    if (rowId == null) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    Set<String> changed = new HashSet<>();
    Set<String> persistent = persistentCells.get(rowId);
    if (persistent != null) {
      changed.addAll(persistent);
    }
    Set<String> temporary = transientCells.get(rowId);
    if (temporary != null) {
      changed.addAll(temporary);
    }
    return Set.copyOf(changed);
  }

  public synchronized int changedCellCount() {
    pruneExpired();
    int changed = 0;
    Set<RowId> rows = new HashSet<>(persistentRows);
    rows.addAll(transientRows);
    for (RowId rowId : rows) {
      changed += changedCells(rowId).size();
    }
    return changed;
  }

  public synchronized boolean isRowChanged(RowId rowId) {
    if (rowId == null) {
      return false;
    }
    pruneExpired();
    return transientRows.contains(rowId) || persistentRows.contains(rowId);
  }

  public synchronized boolean isCellChanged(RowId rowId, String cellKey) {
    if (rowId == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String normalizedCell = normalizeCell(cellKey);
    if (normalizedCell == null) {
      return false;
    }
    pruneExpired();
    Set<String> temporary = transientCells.get(rowId);
    if (temporary != null && temporary.contains(normalizedCell)) {
      return true;
    }
    Set<String> persistent = persistentCells.get(rowId);
    return persistent != null && persistent.contains(normalizedCell);
  }

  public synchronized void clearPersistentHighlights() {
    persistentRows.clear();
    persistentCells.clear();
  }

  public synchronized void clearTransientHighlights() {
    transientRows.clear();
    transientCells.clear();
    transientRowChangedAt.clear();
    transientCellChangedAt.clear();
  }

  public synchronized void clearRow(RowId rowId) {
    if (rowId == null) {
      return;
    }
    transientRows.remove(rowId);
    persistentRows.remove(rowId);
    transientCells.remove(rowId);
    persistentCells.remove(rowId);
    transientRowChangedAt.remove(rowId);
    transientCellChangedAt.remove(rowId);
  }

  public synchronized void clearAll() {
    clearTransientHighlights();
    clearPersistentHighlights();
  }

  public synchronized void pruneExpired() {
    if (!usesTemporary()) {
      return;
    }
    long now = System.currentTimeMillis();
    long ttlMillis = Math.max(1L, flashWindow.toMillis());

    transientRowChangedAt.entrySet().removeIf(entry -> expireRow(entry, now, ttlMillis));

    transientCellChangedAt
        .entrySet()
        .removeIf(
            entry -> {
              RowId rowId = entry.getKey();
              Map<String, Long> timings = entry.getValue();
              if (timings == null || timings.isEmpty()) {
                transientCells.remove(rowId);
                return true;
              }
              timings.entrySet()
                  .removeIf(
                      cellEntry ->
                          now - Objects.requireNonNullElse(cellEntry.getValue(), 0L) > ttlMillis);
              Set<String> cells = transientCells.get(rowId);
              if (cells != null) {
                cells.removeIf(cell -> !timings.containsKey(cell));
                if (cells.isEmpty()) {
                  transientCells.remove(rowId);
                }
              }
              return timings.isEmpty();
            });
  }

  private boolean expireRow(Map.Entry<RowId, Long> entry, long now, long ttlMillis) {
    if (entry == null) {
      return true;
    }
    long changedAt = Objects.requireNonNullElse(entry.getValue(), 0L);
    if (now - changedAt <= ttlMillis) {
      return false;
    }
    RowId rowId = entry.getKey();
    transientRows.remove(rowId);
    transientCells.remove(rowId);
    transientCellChangedAt.remove(rowId);
    return true;
  }

  private boolean usesTemporary() {
    return mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY
        || mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT;
  }

  private boolean usesPersistent() {
    return mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.PERSISTENT
        || mode == StitchLiveTableHighlightMode.TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT;
  }

  private static String normalizeCell(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchLiveTableDelta.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

/** Snapshot/delta envelope for reusable live table shells. */
public record StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>(
    Type type,
    List<Row> rows,
    List<RowId> removedRowIds,
    Map<RowId, List<String>> changedCells) {

  public enum Type {
    SNAPSHOT,
    UPSERT,
    REMOVE
  }

  public StitchLiveTableDelta {
    type = type == null ? Type.UPSERT : type;
    rows = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
    removedRowIds = removedRowIds == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(removedRowIds);
    changedCells = changedCells == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(changedCells);
  }

  public static <Row, RowId> StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId> snapshot(Collection<Row> rows) {
    return new StitchLiveTableDelta<>(Type.SNAPSHOT, rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows), List.of(), Map.of());
  }

  public static <Row, RowId> StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId> upsert(Collection<Row> rows) {
    return new StitchLiveTableDelta<>(Type.UPSERT, rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows), List.of(), Map.of());
  }

  public static <Row, RowId> StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId> remove(Collection<RowId> ids) {
    return new StitchLiveTableDelta<>(Type.REMOVE, List.of(), ids == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(ids), Map.of());
  }
}

  PERSISTENT,
  TEMPORARY_AND_PERSISTENT
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchLiveTableShell.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchResultsView;

/**
 * Reusable live table substrate with snapshot/delta hooks, update policy integration, and
 * row/cell change tracking.
 */
public final class StitchLiveTableShell<Row, RowId> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar = new StitchRealtimeStatusBar();
  private final StitchSubscriptionControls controls = new StitchSubscriptionControls();
  private final StitchResultsView<Row> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final Div content = new Div();
  private final StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<RowId> changeTracker = new StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<>();
  private final Map<RowId, Row> rowsById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private List<Row> currentRows = List.of();

  private Function<Row, RowId> rowIdResolver = row -> null;
  private boolean rowIdResolverConfigured;

  public StitchLiveTableShell() {
    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime live table shell");

    content.setWidthFull();
    content.setHeight(null);
    content.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    content.add(results);
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.grid().getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Live table");
    results.setPaginationEnabled(false);
    results.setResultCountVisible(true);
    results.emptyState().setTitle("No live rows");
    results.emptyState().setMessage("Start a subscription to receive rows.");

    add(statusBar, controls, content);

    controls.onClear(this::clearHighlights);
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar() {
    return statusBar;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls controls() {
    return controls;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<Row> resultsView() {
    return results;
  }

  public StitchLiveTableChangeTracker<RowId> changeTracker() {
    return changeTracker;
  }

  public StitchLiveTableShell<Row, RowId> withRowIdResolver(Function<Row, RowId> resolver) {
    this.rowIdResolver = Objects.requireNonNullElse(resolver, row -> null);
    this.rowIdResolverConfigured = resolver != null;
    return this;
  }

  public StitchLiveTableShell<Row, RowId> setHighlightMode(StitchLiveTableHighlightMode mode) {
    changeTracker.setHighlightMode(mode);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchLiveTableShell<Row, RowId> setFlashWindow(Duration value) {
    changeTracker.setFlashWindow(value);
    return this;
  }

  public void applySnapshot(Collection<Row> rows) {
    rowsById.clear();
    changeTracker.clearAll();
    List<Row> next = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
    if (!next.isEmpty()) {
      for (Row row : next) {
        RowId rowId = rowIdResolver.apply(row);
        if (rowId != null) {
          rowsById.put(rowId, row);
        }
      }
    }
    refreshRows(hasResolver() ? rowsById.values() : next);
  }

  public void applyUpserts(Collection<Row> rows) {
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    List<Row> incoming = List.copyOf(rows);
    boolean hasResolver = hasResolver();
    if (!hasResolver) {
      refreshRows(incoming);
      return;
    }
    for (Row row : incoming) {
      RowId rowId = rowIdResolver.apply(row);
      if (rowId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Row previous = rowsById.put(rowId, row);
      if (!Objects.equals(previous, row)) {
        changeTracker.markRowChanged(rowId);
      }
    }
    refreshRows(rowsById.values());
  }

  public void applyRemovalsById(Collection<RowId> rowIds) {
    if (rowIds == null || rowIds.isEmpty() || !hasResolver()) {
      return;
    }
    for (RowId rowId : rowIds) {
      if (rowId == null) {
        continue;
      }
      rowsById.remove(rowId);
      changeTracker.clearRow(rowId);
    }
    refreshRows(rowsById.values());
  }

  public void applyDelta(StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId> delta) {
    if (delta == null) {
      return;
    }
    switch (delta.type()) {
      case SNAPSHOT -> applySnapshot(delta.rows());
      case UPSERT -> applyUpserts(delta.rows());
      case REMOVE -> applyRemovalsById(delta.removedRowIds());
    }
    if (!delta.changedCells().isEmpty()) {
      for (Map.Entry<RowId, List<String>> entry : delta.changedCells().entrySet()) {
        RowId rowId = entry.getKey();
        List<String> cells = entry.getValue();
        if (rowId == null || cells == null || cells.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        for (String cell : cells) {
          changeTracker.markCellChanged(rowId, cell);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  public AutoCloseable bindController(
      StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>> controller) {
    return bindController(controller, null);
  }

  public AutoCloseable bindController(
      StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>> controller,
      Consumer<List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>>>> updatesObserver) {
    if (controller == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    Consumer<List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>>>> observer =
        updatesObserver == null ? updates -> {} : updatesObserver;
    Registration statusRegistration = statusBar.bind(controller);
    Registration controlsRegistration = controls.bind(controller);
    AutoCloseable updatesHandle =
        controller.addListener(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<>() {
              @Override
              public void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>>> updates) {
                if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
                  return;
                }
                runUi(
                    () -> {
                      for (StitchRealtimeUpdate<StitchLiveTableDelta<Row, RowId>> update : updates) {
                        if (update == null) {
                          continue;
                        }
                        applyDelta(update.payload());
                      }
                      observer.accept(updates);
                      statusBar.setLastUpdate(controller.lastUpdateAt());
                      statusBar.setDispatchMetrics(controller.dispatchMetrics());
                    });
              }
            });
    return () -> {
      StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(updatesHandle);
      statusRegistration.remove();
      controlsRegistration.remove();
    };
  }

  public void markCellChanged(RowId rowId, String cellKey) {
    changeTracker.markCellChanged(rowId, cellKey);
  }

  public Set<RowId> changedRows() {
    return changeTracker.changedRows();
  }

  public Set<String> changedCells(RowId rowId) {
    return changeTracker.changedCells(rowId);
  }

  public void pruneTransientHighlights() {
    changeTracker.pruneExpired();
  }

  public void clearHighlights() {
    changeTracker.clearAll();
  }

  public int changedRowsCount() {
    return changeTracker.changedRowCount();
  }

  public int changedCellsCount() {
    return changeTracker.changedCellCount();
  }

  public void refreshGrid() {
    results.grid().getDataProvider().refreshAll();
  }

  public List<Row> rows() {
    return currentRows;
  }

  private boolean hasResolver() {
    return rowIdResolverConfigured;
  }

  private void refreshRows(Collection<Row> rows) {
    List<Row> next = rows == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(rows);
    currentRows = next;
    results.setItems(next);
    statusBar.setLastUpdate(Instant.now());
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(() -> action.run());
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeConflationMode.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

/** Coalescing strategy applied before UI dispatch for high-volume realtime updates. */
public enum StitchRealtimeConflationMode {
  /** Keep all queued updates up to queue limits. */
  NONE,
  /** Keep only the newest update in queue. */
  LATEST_ONLY,
  /** Use debounce-style coalescing by delaying flush until interval quiets. */
  DEBOUNCE
}

  CONNECTED,
  STALE,

  STOPPED
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeHeaderStatus.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.grid.Grid;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchDialog;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

/** Global shell-header realtime status indicator with click-through subscription summary. */
public final class StitchRealtimeHeaderStatus extends Button {
  private static final DateTimeFormatter TS_FORMAT =
      DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss").withZone(ZoneOffset.UTC);

  private final StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry registry;
  private final Span indicatorDot = new Span();
  private final Runnable refreshAction = this::refresh;

  private StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.Snapshot lastSnapshot =
      new StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.Snapshot(
          StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.AggregateState.NONE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, List.of());

  private AutoCloseable registryHandle = () -> {};
  private Registration attachHandle;
  private Registration detachHandle;

  public StitchRealtimeHeaderStatus(StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry registry) {
    this.registry = Objects.requireNonNull(registry, "registry");
    addClassName("stitch-shell-realtime-status");
    indicatorDot.addClassName("stitch-shell-realtime-dot");
    indicatorDot.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
    setIcon(indicatorDot);
    setText("");
    getElement().setAttribute("role", "button");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-haspopup", "dialog");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Global realtime subscription status");
    getElement().setAttribute("title", "Realtime: no subscriptions");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_SHELL_REALTIME_STATUS);
    addClickListener(event -> openSummaryDialog());

    attachHandle =
        addAttachListener(
            event -> {
              StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(registryHandle);
              registryHandle =
                  registry.addListener(
                      event.getUI(),
                      snapshot -> runUi(() -> applySnapshot(snapshot), event.getUI()));
              refresh();
            });
    detachHandle =
        addDetachListener(
            event -> {
              StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(registryHandle);
              registryHandle = () -> {};
            });
    applySnapshot(lastSnapshot);
  }

  public void refresh() {
    applySnapshot(registry.snapshot(getUI().orElse(null)));
  }

  private void applySnapshot(StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.Snapshot snapshot) {
    lastSnapshot = snapshot == null ? lastSnapshot : snapshot;
    int totalSubscriptions = Math.max(0, lastSnapshot.activeCount());
    boolean healthy =
        totalSubscriptions > 0
            && lastSnapshot.connectedCount() > 0
            && lastSnapshot.staleCount() == 0
            && lastSnapshot.errorCount() == 0
            && lastSnapshot.disconnectedCount() == 0;
    String stateClass;
    String title;
    if (totalSubscriptions == 0) {
      stateClass = "stitch-rt-none";
      title = "Realtime: no subscriptions";
    } else if (healthy) {
      stateClass = "stitch-rt-healthy";
      title = "Realtime: connected";
    } else {
      stateClass = "stitch-rt-unhealthy";
      title = "Realtime: disconnected";
    }
    removeClassNames("stitch-rt-none", "stitch-rt-healthy", "stitch-rt-unhealthy");
    addClassName(stateClass);
    getElement().setAttribute("title", title);
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", title);
  }

  private void openSummaryDialog() {
    StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.Snapshot snapshot = registry.snapshot(getUI().orElse(null));
    StitchDialog dialog = new StitchDialog("Realtime Subscriptions");
    dialog.setWidth("980px");
    dialog.setMaxWidth("96vw");
    dialog.setTop("8vh");
    dialog.addSecondaryAction("CLOSE", dialog::close);
    dialog.withJsonPayloadSupplier(() -> snapshot);

    VerticalLayout summary = new VerticalLayout();
    summary.setPadding(false);
    summary.setSpacing(false);
    summary.getStyle().set("gap", "0.35rem");
    summary.add(
        summaryLine("Aggregate", snapshot.aggregateState().name()),
        summaryLine("Active", String.valueOf(snapshot.activeCount())),
        summaryLine("Connected", String.valueOf(snapshot.connectedCount())),
        summaryLine("Connecting", String.valueOf(snapshot.connectingCount())),
        summaryLine("Stale", String.valueOf(snapshot.staleCount())),
        summaryLine("Error", String.valueOf(snapshot.errorCount())),
        summaryLine("Disconnected", String.valueOf(snapshot.disconnectedCount())),
        summaryLine("Stopped", String.valueOf(snapshot.stoppedCount())));
    summary.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime aggregate status summary");

    Grid<StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.SubscriptionSummary> grid =
        new Grid<StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.SubscriptionSummary>();
    grid.setWidthFull();
    grid.setHeight("360px");
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime active subscription summary");
    grid.addColumn(value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.sourceLabel(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Source")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.contextLabel(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Context")
        .setFlexGrow(1)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(value -> value.state().name()).setHeader("State").setAutoWidth(true).setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(value -> value.scope().name()).setHeader("Scope").setAutoWidth(true).setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(value -> formatInstant(value.lastUpdateAt()))
        .setHeader("Last Update")
        .setAutoWidth(true)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.addColumn(value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.lastError(), "-"))
        .setHeader("Last Error")
        .setFlexGrow(1)
        .setResizable(true);
    grid.setItems(snapshot.subscriptions());

    dialog.addToBody(summary, grid);
    dialog.open();
  }

  private static HorizontalLayout summaryLine(String label, String value) {
    Span left = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(label, ""));
    left.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");
    Span right = new Span(Strings.firstNonBlank(value, "-"));
    HorizontalLayout row = new HorizontalLayout(left, right);
    row.setPadding(false);
    row.setSpacing(true);
    row.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    return row;
  }

  private static String formatInstant(Instant value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return "-";
    }
    return TS_FORMAT.format(value) + " UTC";
  }

  private static void runUi(Runnable action, UI ui) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI activeUi = ui == null ? null : ui;
    if (activeUi == null || !activeUi.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    activeUi.access(() -> action.run());
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeSource.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

/** Transport/source adapter contract normalized for Stitch realtime controllers. */
@FunctionalInterface
public interface StitchRealtimeSource<T> {

  Subscription subscribe(Listener<T> listener) throws Exception;

  @FunctionalInterface
  interface Subscription extends AutoCloseable {
    @Override
    void close() throws Exception;
  }

  interface Listener<T> {
    default void onSubscribed() {}

    default void onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> update) {}

    default void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {}

    default void onUnsubscribed() {}
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeStatusBar.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;

/** Reusable accessible realtime status strip for watcher/table/stream surfaces. */
public final class StitchRealtimeStatusBar extends HorizontalLayout {
  private static final DateTimeFormatter TS_FORMAT =
      DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss").withZone(ZoneOffset.UTC);

  private final Span state = new Span("DISCONNECTED");
  private final Span scope = new Span("Scope: PRIVATE");
  private final Span lastUpdate = new Span("Last update: -");
  private final Span queue = new Span("Pending: 0");
  private final Span dropped = new Span("Dropped: 0");
  private final Span message = new Span();

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    getElement().setAttribute("role", "status");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime connection status");

    state.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");
    message.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");
    add(state, scope, lastUpdate, queue, dropped, message);
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar setState(StitchRealtimeConnectionState value) {
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState resolved =
        value == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : value;
    runUi(() -> state.setText(resolved.name()));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar setScope(StitchSubscriptionScope value) {
    StitchSubscriptionScope resolved =
        value == null ? StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE : value;
    runUi(() -> scope.setText("Scope: " + resolved.name()));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar setLastUpdate(Instant value) {
    runUi(
        () ->
            lastUpdate.setText(
                value == null ? "Last update: -" : "Last update: " + TS_FORMAT.format(value) + " UTC"));
    return this;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar setDispatchMetrics(StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics) {
    StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics resolved =
        metrics == null ? new StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics(0, 0, 0, null) : metrics;
    runUi(
        () -> {
          queue.setText("Pending: " + Math.max(0, resolved.pendingUpdates()));
          dropped.setText("Dropped: " + Math.max(0L, resolved.droppedUpdates()));
        });
    return this;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar setMessage(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    runUi(() -> message.setText(normalized == null ? "" : normalized));
    return this;
  }

  public Registration bind(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> controller) {
    if (controller == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    setScope(controller.scope());
    setState(controller.state());
    setLastUpdate(controller.lastUpdateAt());
    setDispatchMetrics(controller.dispatchMetrics());
    if (controller.lastError() != null) {
      setMessage(controller.lastError().getMessage());
    } else {
      setMessage("");
    }
    try {
      AutoCloseable handle =
          controller.addObserver(
              new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Observer() {
                @Override
                public void onStateChanged(
                    StitchRealtimeConnectionState state, StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {
                  setScope(scope);
                  setState(state);
                }

                @Override
                public void onMetrics(
                    StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics, Instant lastUpdateAt) {
                  setDispatchMetrics(metrics);
                  setLastUpdate(lastUpdateAt);
                }

                @Override
                public void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
                  setMessage(error == null ? "" : error.getMessage());
                  setState(terminal ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR : StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE);
                }
              });
      return () -> StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(handle);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return () -> {};
    }
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(() -> action.run());
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.concurrent.CopyOnWriteArrayList;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;

/** Shared realtime subscription registry for global session-level status aggregation. */
public final class StitchRealtimeStatusRegistry {
  public enum AggregateState {
    NONE,
    HEALTHY,
    UNHEALTHY
  }

  private final Map<String, Entry> entries = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final CopyOnWriteArrayList<ListenerRegistration> listeners = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();

  public AutoCloseable register(
      String sourceLabel,
      String contextLabel,
      StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> controller,
      UI ui) {
    StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> requiredController =
        Objects.requireNonNull(controller, "controller");
    String entryId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
    Entry entry =
        new Entry(
            entryId,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sourceLabel), "Realtime"),
            Strings.trimToNull(contextLabel),
            resolveUiId(ui),
            requiredController.scope(),
            requiredController.state(),
            requiredController.lastUpdateAt(),
            message(requiredController.lastError()),
            requiredController.dispatchMetrics());

    AutoCloseable observerHandle =
        requiredController.addObserver(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Observer() {
              @Override
              public void onStateChanged(
                  StitchRealtimeConnectionState state, StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {
                update(
                    entryId,
                    value ->
                        value.withStateAndScope(
                            state == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : state,
                            scope == null ? StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE : scope));
              }

              @Override
              public void onMetrics(
                  StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics, Instant lastUpdateAt) {
                update(entryId, value -> value.withMetrics(lastUpdateAt, metrics));
              }

              @Override
              public void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
                update(
                    entryId,
                    value ->
                        value.withError(
                            message(error),
                            terminal
                                ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR
                                : StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE));
              }
            });

    synchronized (this) {
      entries.put(entryId, entry);
    }
    notifyListeners();
    return () -> {
      StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(observerHandle);
      synchronized (this) {
        entries.remove(entryId);
      }
      notifyListeners();
    };
  }

  public AutoCloseable addListener(UI ui, Consumer<Snapshot> consumer) {
    Consumer<Snapshot> requiredConsumer = Objects.requireNonNull(consumer, "consumer");
    ListenerRegistration registration = new ListenerRegistration(resolveUiId(ui), requiredConsumer);
    listeners.add(registration);
    requiredConsumer.accept(snapshot(ui));
    return () -> listeners.remove(registration);
  }

  public Snapshot snapshot(UI ui) {
    return snapshot(resolveUiId(ui));
  }

  private Snapshot snapshot(int uiId) {
    List<Entry> scoped;
    synchronized (this) {
      scoped =
          entries.values().stream()
              .filter(value -> uiId < 0 || value.uiId() == uiId)
              .sorted(
                  Comparator.comparing(Entry::sourceLabel, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
                      .thenComparing(
                          value -> Strings.firstNonBlank(value.contextLabel(), ""),
                          String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
              .toList();
    }

    List<Entry> active =
        scoped.stream()
            .filter(value -> value.state() != StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED)
            .toList();
    int connected = count(active, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED);
    int connecting = count(active, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING);
    int stale = count(active, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE);
    int error = count(active, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR);
    int disconnected = count(active, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED);
    int stopped = count(scoped, StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED);

    AggregateState aggregate;
    if (active.isEmpty()) {
      aggregate = AggregateState.NONE;
    } else if (stale > 0 || error > 0 || disconnected > 0) {
      aggregate = AggregateState.UNHEALTHY;
    } else {
      aggregate = AggregateState.HEALTHY;
    }

    List<SubscriptionSummary> subscriptions =
        scoped.stream()
            .map(
                value ->
                    new SubscriptionSummary(
                        value.id(),
                        value.sourceLabel(),
                        value.contextLabel(),
                        value.scope(),
                        value.state(),
                        value.lastUpdateAt(),
                        value.lastError(),
                        value.metrics()))
            .toList();
    return new Snapshot(
        aggregate,
        active.size(),
        connected,
        connecting,
        stale,
        error,
        disconnected,
        stopped,
        subscriptions);
  }

  private static int count(List<Entry> entries, StitchRealtimeConnectionState state) {
    return (int) entries.stream().filter(value -> value.state() == state).count();
  }

  private void update(String entryId, java.util.function.UnaryOperator<Entry> mutator) {
    synchronized (this) {
      Entry existing = entries.get(entryId);
      if (existing == null) {
        return;
      }
      entries.put(entryId, mutator.apply(existing));
    }
    notifyListeners();
  }

  private void notifyListeners() {
    if (listeners.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    List<ListenerRegistration> snapshotListeners = new ArrayList<>(listeners);
    for (ListenerRegistration listener : snapshotListeners) {
      try {
        listener.consumer().accept(snapshot(listener.uiId()));
      } catch (Exception ignored) {
      }
    }
  }

  private static int resolveUiId(UI ui) {
    return ui == null ? -1 : ui.getUIId();
  }

  private static String message(Throwable error) {
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(error == null ? null : error.getMessage());
    if (value != null) {
      return value;
    }
    return error == null ? null : error.getClass().getSimpleName();
  }

  private record Entry(
      String id,
      String sourceLabel,
      String contextLabel,
      int uiId,
      StitchSubscriptionScope scope,
      StitchRealtimeConnectionState state,
      Instant lastUpdateAt,
      String lastError,
      StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics) {
    private Entry {
      sourceLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sourceLabel), "Realtime");
      contextLabel = Strings.trimToNull(contextLabel);
      scope = scope == null ? StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE : scope;
      state = state == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : state;
      metrics = metrics == null ? new StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics(0, 0, 0, null) : metrics;
      lastError = Strings.trimToNull(lastError);
    }

    private Entry withStateAndScope(
        StitchRealtimeConnectionState nextState, StitchSubscriptionScope nextScope) {
      return new Entry(
          id,
          sourceLabel,
          contextLabel,
          uiId,
          nextScope,
          nextState,
          lastUpdateAt,
          lastError,
          metrics);
    }

    private Entry withMetrics(Instant nextLastUpdateAt, StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics nextMetrics) {
      return new Entry(
          id,
          sourceLabel,
          contextLabel,
          uiId,
          scope,
          state,
          nextLastUpdateAt,
          lastError,
          nextMetrics);
    }

    private Entry withError(String error, StitchRealtimeConnectionState nextState) {
      return new Entry(
          id, sourceLabel, contextLabel, uiId, scope, nextState, lastUpdateAt, error, metrics);
    }
  }

  private record ListenerRegistration(int uiId, Consumer<Snapshot> consumer) {}

  public record Snapshot(
      AggregateState aggregateState,
      int activeCount,
      int connectedCount,
      int connectingCount,
      int staleCount,
      int errorCount,
      int disconnectedCount,
      int stoppedCount,
      List<SubscriptionSummary> subscriptions) {
    public Snapshot {
      aggregateState = aggregateState == null ? AggregateState.NONE : aggregateState;
      subscriptions = subscriptions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(subscriptions);
    }
  }

  public record SubscriptionSummary(
      String id,
      String sourceLabel,
      String contextLabel,
      StitchSubscriptionScope scope,
      StitchRealtimeConnectionState state,
      Instant lastUpdateAt,
      String lastError,
      StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics) {
    public SubscriptionSummary {
      sourceLabel = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(sourceLabel), "Realtime");
      contextLabel = Strings.trimToNull(contextLabel);
      scope = scope == null ? StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE : scope;
      state = state == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : state;
      lastError = Strings.trimToNull(lastError);
      metrics = metrics == null ? new StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics(0, 0, 0, null) : metrics;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.CopyOnWriteArrayList;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicReference;

/**
 * Shared lifecycle controller for one realtime subscription with restart, stale detection, and UI
 * dispatch integration.
 */
public final class StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<T> implements AutoCloseable {
  private final StitchRealtimeSource<T> source;
  private final StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy;
  private final StitchSubscriptionScope scope;
  private final StitchUiUpdateDispatcher<StitchRealtimeUpdate<T>> dispatcher;
  private final CopyOnWriteArrayList<Listener<T>> listeners = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();
  private final CopyOnWriteArrayList<Observer> observers = new CopyOnWriteArrayList<>();
  private final AtomicReference<StitchRealtimeConnectionState> state =
      new AtomicReference<>(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED);
  private final ScheduledExecutorService staleChecker =
      Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(
          task -> {
            Thread thread = new Thread(task, "stitch-realtime-stale-checker");
            thread.setDaemon(true);
            return thread;
          });
  private final AtomicBoolean disposed = new AtomicBoolean(false);

  private volatile StitchRealtimeSource.Subscription subscription;
  private volatile Instant lastUpdateAt;
  private volatile Throwable lastError;

  public StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController(
      StitchRealtimeSource<T> source,
      StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy,
      StitchSubscriptionScope scope,
      UI ui) {
    this.source = Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    this.policy = Objects.requireNonNullElse(policy, StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.defaults());
    this.scope = Objects.requireNonNullElse(scope, StitchSubscriptionScope.PRIVATE);
    this.dispatcher =
        new StitchUiUpdateDispatcher<>(
            this.policy,
            updates -> notifyUpdates(List.copyOf(updates)),
            ui);
    staleChecker.scheduleWithFixedDelay(this::checkStale, 1, 1, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy() {
    return policy;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionScope scope() {
    return scope;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeConnectionState state() {
    return state.get();
  }

  public Throwable lastError() {
    return lastError;
  }

  public Instant lastUpdateAt() {
    return lastUpdateAt;
  }

  public StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics dispatchMetrics() {
    return dispatcher.metrics();
  }

  public void setUi(UI ui) {
    dispatcher.setUi(ui);
  }

  public AutoCloseable addListener(Listener<T> listener) {
    Listener<T> resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    listeners.add(resolved);
    resolved.onStateChanged(state.get(), scope);
    return () -> listeners.remove(resolved);
  }

  public AutoCloseable addObserver(Observer observer) {
    Observer resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(observer, "observer");
    observers.add(resolved);
    resolved.onStateChanged(state.get(), scope);
    resolved.onMetrics(dispatcher.metrics(), lastUpdateAt);
    return () -> observers.remove(resolved);
  }

  public synchronized void start() {
    if (disposed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    if (subscription != null) {
      return;
    }
    transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING);
    try {
      subscription =
          source.subscribe(
              new StitchRealtimeSource.Listener<>() {
                @Override
                public void onSubscribed() {
                  transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED);
                }

                @Override
                public void onUpdate(StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> update) {
                  if (update == null || disposed.get()) {
                    return;
                  }
                  lastUpdateAt = update.receivedAt();
                  if (state.get() == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE) {
                    transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED);
                  }
                  dispatcher.enqueue(update);
                }

                @Override
                public void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
                  if (disposed.get()) {
                    return;
                  }
                  lastError = error;
                  notifyError(error, terminal);
                  transition(
                      terminal
                          ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR
                          : StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE);
                  if (terminal) {
                    safeCloseSubscription();
                  }
                }

                @Override
                public void onUnsubscribed() {
                  if (disposed.get()) {
                    return;
                  }
                  transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED);
                }
              });
      lastUpdateAt = Instant.now();
      transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED);
    } catch (Exception error) {
      lastError = error;
      notifyError(error, true);
      safeCloseSubscription();
      transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR);
    }
  }

  public synchronized void stop() {
    if (disposed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    safeCloseSubscription();
    transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED);
  }

  public synchronized void restart() {
    if (disposed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    safeCloseSubscription();
    transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED);
    start();
  }

  @Override
  public synchronized void close() {
    if (!disposed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    safeCloseSubscription();
    dispatcher.close();
    staleChecker.shutdownNow();
    transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED);
    listeners.clear();
    observers.clear();
  }

  private void transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState next) {
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState resolved =
        next == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : next;
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState previous = state.getAndSet(resolved);
    if (previous == resolved) {
      return;
    }
    for (Listener<T> listener : listeners) {
      listener.onStateChanged(resolved, scope);
    }
    for (Observer observer : observers) {
      observer.onStateChanged(resolved, scope);
      observer.onMetrics(dispatcher.metrics(), lastUpdateAt);
    }
  }

  private void notifyUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<T>> updates) {
    if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (Listener<T> listener : listeners) {
      listener.onUpdates(updates);
    }
    for (Observer observer : observers) {
      observer.onMetrics(dispatcher.metrics(), lastUpdateAt);
    }
  }

  private void notifyError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {
    for (Listener<T> listener : listeners) {
      listener.onError(error, terminal);
    }
    for (Observer observer : observers) {
      observer.onError(error, terminal);
      observer.onMetrics(dispatcher.metrics(), lastUpdateAt);
    }
  }

  private void checkStale() {
    if (disposed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    if (state.get() != StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED) {
      return;
    }
    Instant updateTime = lastUpdateAt;
    if (updateTime == null) {
      return;
    }
    long staleAfter = Math.max(1L, policy.staleTimeoutMillis());
    if (Instant.now().toEpochMilli() - updateTime.toEpochMilli() > staleAfter) {
      transition(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE);
    }
  }

  private void safeCloseSubscription() {
    StitchRealtimeSource.Subscription active = subscription;
    subscription = null;
    if (active == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      active.close();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }
  }

  public interface Listener<T> {
    default void onStateChanged(
        StitchRealtimeConnectionState state, StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {}

    default void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<T>> updates) {}

    default void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {}
  }

  public interface Observer {
    default void onStateChanged(
        StitchRealtimeConnectionState state, StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {}

    default void onMetrics(StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.Metrics metrics, Instant lastUpdateAt) {}

    default void onError(Throwable error, boolean terminal) {}
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeUpdate.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Objects;

/** Shared realtime update envelope supporting snapshot and delta payloads. */
public record StitchRealtimeUpdate<T>(Kind kind, T payload, Instant receivedAt) {
  public enum Kind {
    SNAPSHOT,
    DELTA,
    HEARTBEAT
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdate {
    kind = kind == null ? Kind.DELTA : kind;
    receivedAt = Objects.requireNonNullElseGet(receivedAt, Instant::now);
  }

  public static <T> StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> snapshot(T payload) {
    return new StitchRealtimeUpdate<>(Kind.SNAPSHOT, payload, Instant.now());
  }

  public static <T> StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> delta(T payload) {
    return new StitchRealtimeUpdate<>(Kind.DELTA, payload, Instant.now());
  }

  public static <T> StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> heartbeat(T payload) {
    return new StitchRealtimeUpdate<>(Kind.HEARTBEAT, payload, Instant.now());
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import java.util.Objects;

/**
 * Shared per-subscription update policy covering conflation, dispatch cadence, queue bounds, and
 * stale detection.
 */
public final class StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy {
  private final StitchRealtimeConflationMode conflationMode;
  private final int dispatchIntervalMillis;
  private final int maxBatchSize;
  private final int maxQueueSize;
  private final int staleTimeoutMillis;

  private StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy(Builder builder) {
    this.conflationMode =
        Objects.requireNonNullElse(builder.conflationMode, StitchRealtimeConflationMode.NONE);
    this.dispatchIntervalMillis = positive(builder.dispatchIntervalMillis, 100);
    this.maxBatchSize = positive(builder.maxBatchSize, 128);
    this.maxQueueSize = positive(builder.maxQueueSize, 2_000);
    this.staleTimeoutMillis = positive(builder.staleTimeoutMillis, 15_000);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy defaults() {
    return builder().build();
  }

  public StitchRealtimeConflationMode conflationMode() {
    return conflationMode;
  }

  public int dispatchIntervalMillis() {
    return dispatchIntervalMillis;
  }

  public int maxBatchSize() {
    return maxBatchSize;
  }

  public int maxQueueSize() {
    return maxQueueSize;
  }

  public int staleTimeoutMillis() {
    return staleTimeoutMillis;
  }

  private static int positive(Integer value, int fallback) {
    return value == null || value <= 0 ? fallback : value;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private StitchRealtimeConflationMode conflationMode = StitchRealtimeConflationMode.NONE;
    private Integer dispatchIntervalMillis = 100;
    private Integer maxBatchSize = 128;
    private Integer maxQueueSize = 2_000;
    private Integer staleTimeoutMillis = 15_000;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withConflationMode(StitchRealtimeConflationMode value) {
      this.conflationMode = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDispatchIntervalMillis(int value) {
      this.dispatchIntervalMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxBatchSize(int value) {
      this.maxBatchSize = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxQueueSize(int value) {
      this.maxQueueSize = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStaleTimeoutMillis(int value) {
      this.staleTimeoutMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy build() {
      return new StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy(this);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;

/**
 * Shared watcher/detail realtime shell with status, controls, and selection-aware detail region.
 */
public final class StitchRealtimeWatcherShell<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar = new StitchRealtimeStatusBar();
  private final StitchSubscriptionControls controls = new StitchSubscriptionControls();
  private final Span selectionContext = new Span("Selection: -");
  private final Div detailHost = new Div();
  private final StitchEmptyState empty =
      new StitchEmptyState("No live selection", "Select a context and start watching to view updates.");

  private Function<T, Component> detailRenderer = value -> value == null ? null : new Span(String.valueOf(value));

  public StitchRealtimeWatcherShell() {
    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime watcher shell");

    selectionContext.getStyle().set("font-weight", "600");
    selectionContext.getElement().setAttribute("aria-live", "polite");

    detailHost.setSizeFull();
    detailHost.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("role", "region");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime watcher details");

    add(statusBar, controls, selectionContext, detailHost);
    setFlexGrow(1, detailHost);
    clearDetail();
  }

  public StitchRealtimeStatusBar statusBar() {
    return statusBar;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls controls() {
    return controls;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeWatcherShell<T> setSelectionContext(String value) {
    selectionContext.setText(
        value == null || value.isBlank() ? "Selection: -" : "Selection: " + value.trim());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchRealtimeWatcherShell<T> setDetailRenderer(Function<T, Component> renderer) {
    detailRenderer =
        Objects.requireNonNullElse(
            renderer, value -> value == null ? null : new Span(String.valueOf(value)));
    return this;
  }

  public void showDetail(T value) {
    detailHost.removeAll();
    Component content = detailRenderer.apply(value);
    detailHost.add(content == null ? empty : content);
  }

  public void clearDetail() {
    detailHost.removeAll();
    detailHost.add(empty);
  }

  public AutoCloseable bindController(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<T> controller) {
    if (controller == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    Registration statusRegistration = statusBar.bind(controller);
    Registration controlsRegistration = controls.bind(controller);
    AutoCloseable updatesHandle =
        controller.addListener(
            new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Listener<>() {
              @Override
              public void onUpdates(List<StitchRealtimeUpdate<T>> updates) {
                if (updates == null || updates.isEmpty()) {
                  return;
                }
                runUi(
                    () -> {
                      StitchRealtimeUpdate<T> last = updates.get(updates.size() - 1);
                      showDetail(last == null ? null : last.payload());
                      statusBar.setLastUpdate(controller.lastUpdateAt());
                      statusBar.setDispatchMetrics(controller.dispatchMetrics());
                    });
              }
            });
    return () -> {
      StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(updatesHandle);
      statusRegistration.remove();
      controlsRegistration.remove();
    };
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(() -> action.run());
  }
}
