package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchCloseables;

/** Reusable subscription lifecycle controls for realtime screens. */
public final class StitchSubscriptionControls extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final Button start = new Button("START");
  private final Button stop = new Button("STOP");
  private final Button restart = new Button("RESTART");
  private final Button clear = new Button("CLEAR");

  private Runnable onStart = () -> {};
  private Runnable onStop = () -> {};
  private Runnable onRestart = () -> {};
  private Runnable onClear = () -> {};

  public StitchSubscriptionControls() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(true);
    setWidthFull();
    setAlignItems(Alignment.CENTER);
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Realtime subscription controls");

    style(start, "Start realtime subscription");
    style(stop, "Stop realtime subscription");
    style(restart, "Restart realtime subscription");
    style(clear, "Clear transient realtime state");

    start.addClickListener(event -> onStart.run());
    stop.addClickListener(event -> onStop.run());
    restart.addClickListener(event -> onRestart.run());
    clear.addClickListener(event -> onClear.run());

    add(start, stop, restart, clear);
    setState(StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED);
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls onStart(Runnable callback) {
    onStart = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls onStop(Runnable callback) {
    onStop = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls onRestart(Runnable callback) {
    onRestart = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls onClear(Runnable callback) {
    onClear = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls clearEnabled(boolean value) {
    clear.setEnabled(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchSubscriptionControls setState(StitchRealtimeConnectionState value) {
    StitchRealtimeConnectionState resolved =
        value == null ? StitchRealtimeConnectionState.DISCONNECTED : value;
    boolean active =
        resolved == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTED
            || resolved == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.CONNECTING
            || resolved == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STALE;
    runUi(
        () -> {
          start.setEnabled(!active);
          stop.setEnabled(active);
          restart.setEnabled(
              active
                  || resolved == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.ERROR
                  || resolved == StitchRealtimeConnectionState.STOPPED);
        });
    return this;
  }

  public Registration bind(StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController<?> controller) {
    if (controller == null) {
      return () -> {};
    }
    onStart(controller::start);
    onStop(controller::stop);
    onRestart(controller::restart);
    setState(controller.state());
    try {
      AutoCloseable handle =
          controller.addObserver(
              new StitchRealtimeSubscriptionController.Observer() {
                @Override
                public void onStateChanged(
                    StitchRealtimeConnectionState state, StitchSubscriptionScope scope) {
                  setState(state);
                }
              });
      return () -> StitchCloseables.closeQuietly(handle);
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
      return () -> {};
    }
  }

  private void runUi(Runnable action) {
    if (action == null) {
      return;
    }
    UI ui = getUI().orElse(null);
    if (ui == null || !ui.isAttached()) {
      action.run();
      return;
    }
    ui.access(() -> action.run());
  }

  private static void style(Button button, String ariaLabel) {
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_PRIMARY);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
  }

}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/realtime/StitchUiUpdateDispatcher.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.realtime;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.UI;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.Executors;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledFuture;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import java.util.function.Consumer;

/**
 * Shared UI-thread dispatch queue with configurable conflation and bounded-rate flush behavior.
 */
public final class StitchUiUpdateDispatcher<T> implements AutoCloseable {
  private final Object lock = new Object();
  private final ArrayDeque<T> queue = new ArrayDeque<>();
  private final ScheduledExecutorService scheduler;
  private final AtomicBoolean closed = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final Consumer<List<T>> onFlush;
  private final boolean ownsScheduler;

  private volatile StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy;
  private volatile UI ui;
  private volatile ScheduledFuture<?> scheduledFlush;

  private volatile long droppedUpdates;
  private volatile long flushCount;
  private volatile Instant lastFlushAt;

  public StitchUiUpdateDispatcher(
      StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy, Consumer<List<T>> onFlush, UI ui) {
    this(policy, onFlush, ui, null);
  }

  public StitchUiUpdateDispatcher(
      StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy,
      Consumer<List<T>> onFlush,
      UI ui,
      ScheduledExecutorService scheduler) {
    this.policy = Objects.requireNonNullElse(policy, StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.defaults());
    this.onFlush = Objects.requireNonNull(onFlush, "onFlush");
    this.ui = ui;
    if (scheduler == null) {
      this.scheduler =
          Executors.newSingleThreadScheduledExecutor(
              task -> {
                Thread thread = new Thread(task, "stitch-ui-update-dispatcher");
                thread.setDaemon(true);
                return thread;
              });
      this.ownsScheduler = true;
    } else {
      this.scheduler = scheduler;
      this.ownsScheduler = false;
    }
  }

  public void setUi(UI value) {
    this.ui = value;
  }

  public void setPolicy(StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy value) {
    this.policy = Objects.requireNonNullElse(value, StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy.defaults());
  }

  public StitchRealtimeUpdatePolicy policy() {
    return policy;
  }

  public void enqueue(T update) {
    if (closed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    if (update == null) {
      return;
    }
    synchronized (lock) {
      if (closed.get()) {
        return;
      }
      applyConflationLocked(update, policy.conflationMode());
      trimQueueLocked();
      scheduleLocked();
    }
  }

  public void flushNow() {
    if (closed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    List<T> batch = drainBatch();
    if (batch.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    dispatch(batch);
    synchronized (lock) {
      if (!queue.isEmpty() && !closed.get()) {
        scheduleLocked();
      }
    }
  }

  public Metrics metrics() {
    int pending;
    synchronized (lock) {
      pending = queue.size();
    }
    return new Metrics(flushCount, droppedUpdates, pending, lastFlushAt);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (!closed.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    ScheduledFuture<?> flush = scheduledFlush;
    if (flush != null) {
      flush.cancel(false);
    }
    synchronized (lock) {
      queue.clear();
    }
    if (ownsScheduler) {
      scheduler.shutdownNow();
    }
  }

  private void applyConflationLocked(T update, StitchRealtimeConflationMode mode) {
    StitchRealtimeConflationMode resolved =
        mode == null ? StitchRealtimeConflationMode.NONE : mode;
    if (resolved == StitchRealtimeConflationMode.LATEST_ONLY) {
      int prior = queue.size();
      queue.clear();
      if (prior > 0) {
        droppedUpdates += prior;
      }
      queue.addLast(update);
      return;
    }
    queue.addLast(update);
  }

  private void trimQueueLocked() {
    int maxQueue = Math.max(1, policy.maxQueueSize());
    while (queue.size() > maxQueue) {
      queue.removeFirst();
      droppedUpdates++;
    }
  }

  private void scheduleLocked() {
    if (scheduledFlush != null && !scheduledFlush.isDone()) {
      if (policy.conflationMode() == StitchRealtimeConflationMode.DEBOUNCE) {
        scheduledFlush.cancel(false);
      } else {
        return;
      }
    }
    int interval = Math.max(1, policy.dispatchIntervalMillis());
    scheduledFlush = scheduler.schedule(this::flushNow, interval, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
  }

  private List<T> drainBatch() {
    synchronized (lock) {
      int take = Math.max(1, policy.maxBatchSize());
      if (queue.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<T> batch = new ArrayList<>(Math.min(take, queue.size()));
      for (int index = 0; index < take && !queue.isEmpty(); index++) {
        batch.add(queue.removeFirst());
      }
      return List.copyOf(batch);
    }
  }

  private void dispatch(List<T> batch) {
    if (batch == null || batch.isEmpty() || closed.get()) {
      return;
    }
    Runnable runnable =
        () -> {
          onFlush.accept(batch);
          flushCount++;
          lastFlushAt = Instant.now();
        };
    UI activeUi = ui;
    if (activeUi == null || !activeUi.isAttached()) {
      runnable.run();
      return;
    }
    activeUi.access(() -> runnable.run());
  }

  public record Metrics(
      long flushCount, long droppedUpdates, int pendingUpdates, Instant lastFlushAt) {}
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/ServletSsoRequestAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import jakarta.servlet.http.Cookie;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoRequest;

/** Servlet adapter for {@link FabricSsoRequest}. */
public final class ServletSsoRequestAdapter implements FabricSsoRequest {

  private final HttpServletRequest request;
  private final boolean forwardedHeadersEnabled;

  public ServletSsoRequestAdapter(HttpServletRequest request, boolean forwardedHeadersEnabled) {
    this.request = Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    this.forwardedHeadersEnabled = forwardedHeadersEnabled;
  }

  @Override
  public String method() {
    return request.getMethod();
  }

  @Override
  public String path() {
    return request.getRequestURI();
  }

  @Override
  public String fullUrl() {
    String fallback = fullUrlFromServlet(request);
    if (!forwardedHeadersEnabled) {
      return fallback;
    }
    String rebuilt =
        buildFullUrl(
            fallback,
            request.getRequestURI(),
            request.getQueryString(),
            request.getScheme(),
            request.getServerName(),
            request.getServerPort(),
            request.getHeader("Forwarded"),
            request.getHeader("X-Forwarded-Proto"),
            request.getHeader("X-Forwarded-Host"),
            request.getHeader("X-Forwarded-Port"));
    return rebuilt == null ? fallback : rebuilt;
  }

  @Override
  public String queryParam(String name) {
    return name == null ? null : request.getParameter(name);
  }

  @Override
  public String header(String name) {
    return name == null ? null : request.getHeader(name);
  }

  @Override
  public String cookie(String name) {
    if (name == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Cookie[] cookies = request.getCookies();
    if (cookies == null || cookies.length == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    for (Cookie cookie : cookies) {
      if (cookie != null && name.equals(cookie.getName())) {
        return cookie.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  @Override
  public String remoteAddr() {
    return request.getRemoteAddr();
  }

  private static String fullUrlFromServlet(HttpServletRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      return null;
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    builder.append(request.getRequestURL());
    String query = request.getQueryString();
    if (query != null && !query.isBlank()) {
      builder.append("?").append(query);
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  static String buildFullUrl(
      String fallbackFullUrl,
      String path,
      String queryString,
      String scheme,
      String serverName,
      int serverPort,
      String forwardedHeader,
      String xForwardedProto,
      String xForwardedHost,
      String xForwardedPort) {
    if (path == null || path.isBlank()) {
      return fallbackFullUrl;
    }
    ForwardedValues forwarded = parseForwarded(forwardedHeader);
    String effectiveScheme = firstToken(forwarded.proto());
    HostPort forwardedHost = parseHostPort(firstToken(forwarded.host()));
    if (effectiveScheme == null || effectiveScheme.isBlank()) {
      effectiveScheme = firstToken(xForwardedProto);
    }
    if (forwardedHost == null || forwardedHost.host() == null || forwardedHost.host().isBlank()) {
      forwardedHost = parseHostPort(firstToken(xForwardedHost));
    }
    Integer forwardedPort = parsePort(firstToken(xForwardedPort));
    String host = forwardedHost == null ? null : forwardedHost.host();
    Integer port = forwardedHost == null ? null : forwardedHost.port();
    if (port == null && forwardedPort != null) {
      port = forwardedPort;
    }
    if (effectiveScheme == null || effectiveScheme.isBlank()) {
      effectiveScheme = scheme;
    }
    if (host == null || host.isBlank()) {
      host = serverName;
    }
    if (host == null || host.isBlank()) {
      return fallbackFullUrl;
    }
    int effectivePort = port == null || port <= 0 ? serverPort : port;
    boolean includePort = effectivePort > 0 && !isDefaultPort(effectiveScheme, effectivePort);
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    builder.append(effectiveScheme).append("://").append(host);
    if (includePort) {
      builder.append(":").append(effectivePort);
    }
    builder.append(path);
    if (queryString != null && !queryString.isBlank()) {
      builder.append("?").append(queryString);
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private static boolean isDefaultPort(String scheme, int port) {
    if (scheme == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if ("http".equalsIgnoreCase(scheme)) {
      return port == 80;
    }
    if ("https".equalsIgnoreCase(scheme)) {
      return port == 443;
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static String firstToken(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    int comma = trimmed.indexOf(',');
    if (comma >= 0) {
      return trimmed.substring(0, comma).trim();
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  private static ForwardedValues parseForwarded(String header) {
    if (header == null || header.isBlank()) {
      return new ForwardedValues(null, null);
    }
    String first = firstToken(header);
    if (first == null || first.isBlank()) {
      return new ForwardedValues(null, null);
    }
    String proto = null;
    String host = null;
    String[] parts = first.split(";");
    for (String part : parts) {
      if (part == null || part.isBlank()) {
        continue;
      }
      String[] kv = part.trim().split("=", 2);
      if (kv.length != 2) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = kv[0].trim().toLowerCase();
      String value = stripQuotes(kv[1].trim());
      if (key.equals("proto")) {
        proto = value;
      } else if (key.equals("host")) {
        host = value;
      }
    }
    return new ForwardedValues(proto, host);
  }

  private static String stripQuotes(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.length() >= 2 && trimmed.startsWith("\"") && trimmed.endsWith("\"")) {
      return trimmed.substring(1, trimmed.length() - 1);
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  private static HostPort parseHostPort(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.startsWith("[")) {
      int end = trimmed.indexOf(']');
      if (end > 0) {
        String host = trimmed.substring(0, end + 1);
        String rest = trimmed.substring(end + 1).trim();
        Integer port = null;
        if (rest.startsWith(":")) {
          port = parsePort(rest.substring(1));
        }
        return new HostPort(host, port);
      }
      return new HostPort(trimmed, null);
    }
    int colon = trimmed.lastIndexOf(':');
    if (colon > 0 && colon < trimmed.length() - 1) {
      Integer port = parsePort(trimmed.substring(colon + 1));
      if (port != null) {
        return new HostPort(trimmed.substring(0, colon), port);
      }
    }
    return new HostPort(trimmed, null);
  }

  private static Integer parsePort(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      int port = Integer.parseInt(value.trim());
      return port > 0 ? port : null;
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private record ForwardedValues(String proto, String host) {}

  private record HostPort(String host, Integer port) {}
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/ServletSsoResponseAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoResponse;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoCookieAttributes;

/** Servlet adapter for {@link FabricSsoResponse}. */
public final class ServletSsoResponseAdapter implements FabricSsoResponse {

  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = new ObjectMapper();

  private final HttpServletResponse response;
  private boolean halted;

  public ServletSsoResponseAdapter(HttpServletResponse response) {
    this.response = Objects.requireNonNull(response, "response");
  }

  @Override
  public void setStatus(int status) {
    response.setStatus(status);
  }

  @Override
  public void setHeader(String name, String value) {
    if (name != null && value != null) {
      response.setHeader(name, value);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void setJson(Object payload) {
    try {
      response.setContentType("application/json");
      response.setCharacterEncoding(StandardCharsets.UTF_8.name());
      response.getWriter().write(MAPPER.writeValueAsString(payload));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to write JSON response", ex);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void setText(String payload) {
    try {
      response.setContentType("text/plain");
      response.setCharacterEncoding(StandardCharsets.UTF_8.name());
      response.getWriter().write(payload == null ? "" : payload);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to write text response", ex);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void redirect(String location) {
    if (location == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      response.sendRedirect(location);
      halted = true;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to send redirect", ex);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void addCookie(SsoCookieAttributes cookie) {
    if (cookie == null || cookie.name() == null) {
      return;
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
    builder.append(cookie.name()).append("=");
    if (cookie.value() != null) {
      builder.append(cookie.value());
    }
    if (cookie.path() != null) {
      builder.append("; Path=").append(cookie.path());
    }
    if (cookie.domain() != null) {
      builder.append("; Domain=").append(cookie.domain());
    }
    if (cookie.maxAgeSeconds() != null) {
      builder.append("; Max-Age=").append(cookie.maxAgeSeconds());
    }
    if (cookie.httpOnly()) {
      builder.append("; HttpOnly");
    }
    if (cookie.secure()) {
      builder.append("; Secure");
    }
    if (cookie.sameSite() != null) {
      builder.append("; SameSite=").append(cookie.sameSite());
    }
    response.addHeader("Set-Cookie", builder.toString());
  }

  @Override
  public void halt() {
    halted = true;
  }

  public boolean halted() {
    return halted;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/StitchGroupAccess.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple.PlatformModelMembership;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Resolves group visibility for Stitch pages from the platform model and current SSO subject.
 */
public final class StitchGroupAccess {
  public static final String PLATFORM_ADMIN_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String PLATFORM_NAME = "platform";

  private final SessionImpl session;

  public StitchGroupAccess(Fabric.Session session) {
    this.session = session instanceof SessionImpl resolved ? resolved : null;
  }

  public GroupScope scopeForSubject(String subject) {
    String normalizedSubject = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    Optional<DefinitionPlatform> platformModel = platformModel();
    if (platformModel.isEmpty()) {
      return new GroupScope(normalizedSubject, false, List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
    }
    DefinitionPlatform model = platformModel.get();
    Map<String, Set<String>> membership = PlatformModelMembership.buildMembershipIndex(model);
    List<String> configuredGroups = configuredGroups(model);
    List<String> subjectGroups = normalizeSorted(groupsForSubjectCandidates(membership, normalizedSubject));
    boolean admin = containsIgnoreCase(subjectGroups, PLATFORM_ADMIN_GROUP);
    List<String> visible = admin ? configuredGroups : subjectGroups;
    return new GroupScope(normalizedSubject, admin, visible, configuredGroups, subjectGroups);
  }

  private Optional<DefinitionPlatform> platformModel() {
    if (session == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    try {
      DiscoveryCache cache = session.internal().discoveryCache();
      return cache == null
          ? Optional.empty()
          : cache.get(DefinitionPlatform.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, PLATFORM_NAME);
    } catch (RuntimeException ignore) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
  }

  private static Set<String> groupsForSubjectCandidates(
      Map<String, Set<String>> membership, String subject) {
    if (membership == null || membership.isEmpty() || Strings.isBlank(subject)) {
      return Set.of();
    }
    Set<String> candidates = PlatformModelMembership.membershipSubjectCandidates(subject);
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String candidate : candidates) {
      if (candidate == null) {
        continue;
      }
      Set<String> resolved = membership.get(candidate);
      if (resolved != null) {
        groups.addAll(resolved);
      }
    }
    return Set.copyOf(groups);
  }

  private static List<String> configuredGroups(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    if (model == null || model.root() == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> groups = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    collectConfiguredGroups(model.root(), groups);
    return normalizeSorted(groups);
  }

  private static void collectConfiguredGroups(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, LinkedHashSet<String> groups) {
    if (node == null || groups == null) {
      return;
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> orgGroups = node.groups();
    if (orgGroups != null) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : orgGroups) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String id = normalizeGroup(Strings.trimToNull(group.name()));
        if (id == null) {
          id = normalizeGroup(Strings.trimToNull(group.nodeName()));
        }
        if (id != null) {
          groups.add(id);
        }
      }
    }
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = node.ous();
    if (children == null || children.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
      collectConfiguredGroups(child, groups);
    }
  }

  private static boolean containsIgnoreCase(List<String> values, String candidate) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || Strings.isBlank(candidate)) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value != null && candidate.equalsIgnoreCase(value.trim())) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeSorted(Set<String> groups) {
    if (groups == null || groups.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String group : groups) {
      String value = normalizeGroup(group);
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(normalized);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String normalizeGroup(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("group:")
        && normalized.length() > "group:".length()) {
      normalized = normalized.substring("group:".length());
    }
    normalized = normalized.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }

  public record GroupScope(
      String subject,
      boolean admin,
      List<String> visibleGroups,
      List<String> configuredGroups,
      List<String> subjectGroups) {
    public GroupScope {
      visibleGroups = visibleGroups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(visibleGroups);
      configuredGroups = configuredGroups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(configuredGroups);
      subjectGroups = subjectGroups == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(subjectGroups);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/StitchIdentityContext.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import com.vaadin.flow.server.VaadinServletRequest;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import java.net.http.HttpRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchIdentityContext {

  private StitchIdentityContext() {}

  public static String currentSubject() {
    return resolveSubject("service:stitch");
  }

  public static String resolveSubject(String fallback) {
    String fromThread = Strings.trimToNull(SsoContext.currentSubject());
    if (fromThread != null) {
      return fromThread;
    }
    VaadinServletRequest current = VaadinServletRequest.getCurrent();
    HttpServletRequest request = current == null ? null : current.getHttpServletRequest();
    if (request != null) {
      Object value = request.getAttribute(StitchSsoFilter.ATTR_SUBJECT);
      if (value instanceof String text && !text.isBlank()) {
        return text.trim();
      }
    }
    return Strings.isBlank(fallback) ? null : fallback.trim();
  }

  public static HttpRequest.Builder addSubjectHeader(HttpRequest.Builder builder, String fallback) {
    if (builder == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String subject = resolveSubject(fallback);
    if (subject != null) {
      builder.header("fabric-user", subject);
    }
    return builder;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/StitchSsoFilter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import jakarta.servlet.FilterChain;
import jakarta.servlet.ServletException;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import jakarta.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.FabricSsoRequest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoAttributes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.sso.SsoService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;
import org.springframework.web.filter.OncePerRequestFilter;

public final class StitchSsoFilter extends OncePerRequestFilter {

  public static final String ATTR_SUBJECT = "stitch.subject";
  public static final String ATTR_CONTEXT = "stitch.sso.context";

  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StitchSsoFilter.class);
  private static final List<String> STATIC_PREFIXES =
      List.of("/VAADIN/", "/favicon.ico", "/icons/", "/images/", "/robots.txt");
  private static final List<String> QUIET_LOG_PATHS =
      List.of("/sw.js", "/sw-runtime-resources-precache.js", "/manifest.webmanifest");

  private final SsoService ssoService;
  private final SsoConfig ssoConfig;
  private final String fallbackSubject;

  public StitchSsoFilter(SsoService ssoService, SsoConfig ssoConfig, String fallbackSubject) {
    this.ssoService = ssoService;
    this.ssoConfig = ssoConfig;
    this.fallbackSubject = Strings.isBlank(fallbackSubject) ? "service:stitch" : fallbackSubject.trim();
  }

  @Override
  protected boolean shouldNotFilter(HttpServletRequest request) {
    if (request == null) {
      return true;
    }
    String path = request.getRequestURI();
    if (Strings.isBlank(path)) {
      return true;
    }
    for (String prefix : STATIC_PREFIXES) {
      if (path.startsWith(prefix)) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  @Override
  protected void doFilterInternal(
      HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response, FilterChain filterChain)
      throws ServletException, IOException {
    String path = request == null ? null : request.getRequestURI();
    ServletSsoResponseAdapter responseAdapter = new ServletSsoResponseAdapter(response);
    try {
      FabricSsoRequest ssoRequest =
          new ServletSsoRequestAdapter(request, ssoConfig != null && ssoConfig.forwardedHeadersEnabled());
      SsoResult result = safeResolve(ssoRequest, responseAdapter);
      SsoContext context = result == null ? null : result.context();
      if (context == null) {
        context = fallbackContext();
      }
      String subject = normalizeSubject(context.subject());
      boolean authenticated = context.authenticated() && Strings.isNotBlank(subject);
      if (!authenticated) {
        context =
            new SsoContext(
                null,
                context.mode() == null ? SsoMode.NONE : context.mode(),
                false,
                fallbackSubject,
                null);
        subject = fallbackSubject;
      }
      request.setAttribute(ATTR_CONTEXT, context);
      request.setAttribute(ATTR_SUBJECT, subject);
      request.setAttribute(SsoAttributes.CURRENT_CONTEXT, context);
      request.setAttribute(SsoAttributes.CURRENT_PRINCIPAL, context.principal());
      request.setAttribute(SsoAttributes.CURRENT_ATTRIBUTES, result == null ? null : result.attributes());
      SsoContext.set(context);
      if (shouldLogRequest(request, path)) {
        LOGGER.info(
            "[Stitch][SSO] mode={} subject={} actor={} authenticated={} path={}",
            context.mode(),
            subject,
            context.actor(),
            authenticated,
            path);
      }
      if (responseAdapter.halted() || response.isCommitted()) {
        return;
      }
      filterChain.doFilter(request, response);
    } finally {
      SsoContext.clear();
    }
  }

  private SsoResult safeResolve(FabricSsoRequest request, ServletSsoResponseAdapter response) {
    try {
      return ssoService.resolve(request, response);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.warn(
          "[Stitch][SSO][ResolveFailed] mode={} path={} message={}",
          ssoService.mode(),
          request == null ? null : request.path(),
          ex.getMessage());
      return SsoResult.empty(ssoService.mode());
    }
  }

  private SsoContext fallbackContext() {
    return new SsoContext(null, ssoService.mode(), false, fallbackSubject, null);
  }

  private String normalizeSubject(String subject) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(subject)) {
      return fallbackSubject;
    }
    return subject.trim();
  }

  private boolean shouldLogRequest(HttpServletRequest request, String path) {
    if (request == null || Strings.isBlank(path)) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String quietPath : QUIET_LOG_PATHS) {
      if (path.equals(quietPath)) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    if (!Strings.isBlank(request.getHeader("X-Vaadin-Request"))) {
      return false;
    }
    if ("/".equals(path)) {
      String requestType = request.getParameter("v-r");
      if (!Strings.isBlank(requestType)) {
        return false;
      }
      String query = request.getQueryString();
      if (!Strings.isBlank(query) && query.contains("v-r=")) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/security/StitchSsoUsers.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.security;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;

public final class StitchSsoUsers {
  private final StitchSettings settings;

  public StitchSsoUsers(StitchSettings settings) {
    this.settings = Objects.requireNonNull(settings, "settings");
  }

  public List<String> listUsers() {
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : settings.sso().spoofUsers()) {
      String normalized = normalizeUserId(value);
      if (normalized != null) {
        values.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    String fallback = normalizeUserId(settings.sso().spoofDefaultUsername());
    if (fallback != null) {
      values.add(fallback);
    }
    return values.stream().distinct().sorted(Comparator.comparing(value -> value.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))).toList();
  }

  private static String normalizeUserId(String value) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    if (trimmed.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("user:")) {
      String id = trimmed.substring("user:".length()).trim();
      return id.isEmpty() ? null : id;
    }
    return trimmed;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;

public final class StitchFabricSettings {
  private final String group;
  private final String name;
  private final String instance;
  private final String discoveryUrls;
  private final String kerberosKeytab;
  private final String kerberosUsername;
  private final String kekFile;
  private final String trustCert;
  private final SessionType sessionType;
  private final boolean directDataEnabled;
  private final boolean serviceDataEnabled;

  private StitchFabricSettings(Builder builder) {
    this.group = require(builder.group, "group");
    this.name = require(builder.name, "name");
    this.instance = require(builder.instance, "instance");
    this.discoveryUrls = require(builder.discoveryUrls, "discoveryUrls");
    this.kerberosKeytab = require(builder.kerberosKeytab, "kerberosKeytab");
    this.kerberosUsername = require(builder.kerberosUsername, "kerberosUsername");
    this.kekFile = optional(builder.kekFile);
    this.trustCert = optional(builder.trustCert);
    this.sessionType = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.sessionType, "sessionType");
    this.directDataEnabled = builder.directDataEnabled;
    this.serviceDataEnabled = builder.serviceDataEnabled;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public String group() {
    return group;
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public String instance() {
    return instance;
  }

  public String discoveryUrls() {
    return discoveryUrls;
  }

  public String kerberosKeytab() {
    return kerberosKeytab;
  }

  public String kerberosUsername() {
    return kerberosUsername;
  }

  public String kekFile() {
    return kekFile;
  }

  public String trustCert() {
    return trustCert;
  }

  public SessionType sessionType() {
    return sessionType;
  }

  public boolean directDataEnabled() {
    return directDataEnabled;
  }

  public boolean serviceDataEnabled() {
    return serviceDataEnabled;
  }

  public Fabric.Session createSession() throws Exception {
    Fabric.Session session = toSessionBuilder().build();
    session.start();
    return session;
  }

  public org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session.SessionImpl.Builder toSessionBuilder() {
    DataOptions dataOptions =
        DataOptions.builder()
            .withDirectEnabled(directDataEnabled)
            .withServiceEnabled(serviceDataEnabled)
            .build();

    var builder =
        Fabric.newSession()
            .withGroup(group)
            .withName(name)
            .withInstance(instance)
            .withType(sessionType)
            .withDiscoveryUrls(discoveryUrls)
            .withKerberosKeytab(Path.of(kerberosKeytab))
            .withKerberosUsername(kerberosUsername)
            .withDataOptions(dataOptions);
    if (trustCert != null) {
      builder.withTlsTrustCert(Path.of(trustCert));
    }
    if (kekFile != null) {
      builder.withKekFile(Path.of(kekFile));
    }
    return builder;
  }

  private static String require(String value, String fieldName) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(fieldName + " is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String optional(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String group = "platform";
    private String name = "stitch";
    private String instance = "instance2";
    private String discoveryUrls = "";
    private String kerberosKeytab = "";
    private String kerberosUsername = "";
    private String kekFile;
    private String trustCert;
    private SessionType sessionType = SessionType.PLATFORM;
    private boolean directDataEnabled = true;
    private boolean serviceDataEnabled = false;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withGroup(String value) {
      this.group = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withName(String value) {
      this.name = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withInstance(String value) {
      this.instance = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDiscoveryUrls(String value) {
      this.discoveryUrls = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withKerberosKeytab(String value) {
      this.kerberosKeytab = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withKerberosUsername(String value) {
      this.kerberosUsername = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withKekFile(String value) {
      this.kekFile = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTrustCert(String value) {
      this.trustCert = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSessionType(SessionType value) {
      this.sessionType = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDirectDataEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.directDataEnabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceDataEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.serviceDataEnabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StitchFabricSettings build() {
      return new StitchFabricSettings(this);
    }
  }
}


===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/session/StitchGroupSelectionContext.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session;

import com.vaadin.flow.server.VaadinSession;
import java.io.Serializable;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Lightweight per-session cache for the last selected Group context. */
public final class StitchGroupSelectionContext {
  private static final String ATTRIBUTE_KEY =
      StitchGroupSelectionContext.class.getName() + ".group";

  private StitchGroupSelectionContext() {}

  public static void remember(String group) {
    VaadinSession session = VaadinSession.getCurrent();
    if (session == null) {
      return;
    }
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    if (normalized == null) {
      session.setAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY, null);
      return;
    }
    session.setAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY, new GroupSelection(normalized));
  }

  public static String current() {
    VaadinSession session = VaadinSession.getCurrent();
    if (session == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Object value = session.getAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_KEY);
    if (value instanceof GroupSelection selection) {
      return selection.group();
    }
    return null;
  }

  private record GroupSelection(String group) implements Serializable {
    private GroupSelection {
      group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/session/StitchRuntimeContext.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.Stitch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.app.StitchSettings;

public final class StitchRuntimeContext {
  private final StitchSettings settings;
  private final Supplier<Fabric.Session> sessionSupplier;
  private volatile Fabric.Session session;

  public StitchRuntimeContext(StitchSettings settings, Fabric.Session session) {
    this(settings, () -> Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session"));
  }

  public StitchRuntimeContext(StitchSettings settings, Supplier<Fabric.Session> sessionSupplier) {
    this.settings = Objects.requireNonNull(settings, "settings");
    this.sessionSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(sessionSupplier, "sessionSupplier");
  }

  public static StitchRuntimeContext of(Stitch stitch, Fabric.Session session) {
    return of(stitch, () -> Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session"));
  }

  public static StitchRuntimeContext of(Stitch stitch, Supplier<Fabric.Session> sessionSupplier) {
    return new StitchRuntimeContext(
        Objects.requireNonNull(stitch, "stitch").stitch(),
        Objects.requireNonNull(sessionSupplier, "sessionSupplier"));
  }

  public StitchSettings settings() {
    return settings;
  }

  public Fabric.Session session() {
    Fabric.Session existing = session;
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    synchronized (this) {
      if (session == null) {
        session = Objects.requireNonNull(sessionSupplier.get(), "session");
      }
      return session;
    }
  }

  public String appTitle() {
    return settings.appTitle();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support;

public final class StitchCloseables {
  private StitchCloseables() {}

  public static void closeQuietly(AutoCloseable handle) {
    if (handle == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      handle.close();
    } catch (Exception ignored) {
    }
  }

  public static void closeAllQuietly(AutoCloseable... handles) {
    if (handles == null || handles.length == 0) {
      return;
    }
    for (AutoCloseable handle : handles) {
      closeQuietly(handle);
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/support/StitchDetailsDialogSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.formlayout.FormLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchDetailsDialogSupport {
  private StitchDetailsDialogSupport() {}

  public static FormLayout buildForm(
      List<String> orderedKeys, Map<String, String> values, Map<String, String> labels) {
    FormLayout form = new FormLayout();
    form.setWidthFull();
    form.setResponsiveSteps(
        new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("0", 1), new FormLayout.ResponsiveStep("42em", 2));
    for (String key : orderedKeys) {
      String label = labelFor(key, labels);
      String value = trimToEmpty(values == null ? null : values.get(key));
      Span content = new Span(value.isBlank() ? "-" : value);
      content.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", label + " value");
      form.addFormItem(content, label);
    }
    return form;
  }

  public static List<String> orderedKeys(
      List<String> configuredKeys, List<String> defaultKeys, Map<String, String> values) {
    LinkedHashSet<String> ordered = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    if (configuredKeys != null && !configuredKeys.isEmpty()) {
      addNonBlankKeys(ordered, configuredKeys);
    } else {
      addNonBlankKeys(ordered, defaultKeys);
    }
    if (values != null && !values.isEmpty()) {
      addNonBlankKeys(ordered, values.keySet());
    }
    return List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public static String summarize(List<String> keys, Function<String, String> valueResolver) {
    if (keys == null || keys.isEmpty() || valueResolver == null) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> values = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String key : keys) {
      String value = trimToEmpty(valueResolver.apply(key));
      if (!value.isBlank()) {
        values.add(value);
      }
    }
    return values.isEmpty() ? "" : String.join(" | ", values);
  }

  public static String trimToEmpty(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  public static String displayValue(String value) {
    String text = trimToEmpty(value);
    return text.isBlank() ? "-" : text;
  }

  public static String defaultSummaryLabel(String configuredLabel) {
    String label = Strings.trimToNull(configuredLabel);
    return label == null ? "Summary" : label;
  }

  public static String joinPath(String... segments) {
    if (segments == null || segments.length == 0) {
      return "";
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>(segments.length);
    for (String segment : segments) {
      normalized.add(trimToEmpty(segment));
    }
    return String.join("/", normalized);
  }

  private static void addNonBlankKeys(LinkedHashSet<String> out, Iterable<String> keys) {
    if (out == null || keys == null) {
      return;
    }
    for (String key : keys) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (normalized != null) {
        out.add(normalized);
      }
    }
  }

  private static String labelFor(String key, Map<String, String> labels) {
    String fromMap = labels == null ? null : labels.get(key);
    if (Strings.isNotBlank(fromMap)) {
      return fromMap.trim();
    }
    String normalized =
        key == null ? "" : key.trim().replace('_', ' ').replace('-', ' ').replace('.', ' ');
    if (normalized.isBlank()) {
      return "Field";
    }
    return normalized.substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT) + normalized.substring(1);
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/support/StitchTextSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StitchTextSupport {
  private StitchTextSupport() {}

  public static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    String message = rootMessageOrNull(error);
    return message == null ? "Unknown error" : message;
  }

  public static String rootMessageOrEmpty(Throwable error) {
    String message = rootMessageOrNull(error);
    return message == null ? "" : message;
  }

  public static String trimToEmpty(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized;
  }

  private static String rootMessageOrNull(Throwable error) {
    Throwable current = error;
    while (current != null && current.getCause() != null && current.getCause() != current) {
      current = current.getCause();
    }
    Throwable root = current == null ? error : current;
    return Strings.trimToNull(root == null ? null : root.getMessage());
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchDirtyStateSupport.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveEvent;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.dialog.StitchUnsavedChangesDialog;

/** Shared unsaved-changes guard behavior for editor workflows. */
public final class StitchDirtyStateSupport {

  public void guard(BooleanSupplier onSave, Runnable onDiscard, Runnable onCancel) {
    BooleanSupplier save = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSave, () -> false);
    Runnable discard = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onDiscard, () -> {});
    Runnable cancel = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onCancel, () -> {});
    StitchUnsavedChangesDialog.open(
        "Save, discard, or cancel before continuing.",
        () -> {
          save.getAsBoolean();
        },
        discard,
        cancel);
  }

  public void guardBeforeLeave(
      BeforeLeaveEvent event,
      BooleanSupplier hasUnsavedChanges,
      BooleanSupplier onSave,
      Runnable onDiscard) {
    if (!safe(hasUnsavedChanges)) {
      return;
    }
    BeforeLeaveEvent.ContinueNavigationAction action = event.postpone();
    guard(
        () -> {
          if (safe(onSave)) {
            action.proceed();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          run(onDiscard);
          action.proceed();
        },
        () -> {});
  }

  private static boolean safe(BooleanSupplier supplier) {
    return supplier != null && supplier.getAsBoolean();
  }

  private static void run(Runnable action) {
    if (action != null) {
      action.run();
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchEditableDetailPanel.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.function.Predicate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchActionStyles;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSection;

/** Shared read-only/editable detail panel shell for tree-driven editors. */
public final class StitchEditableDetailPanel<T> {

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface ContentRenderer<T> {
    Component render(T node, boolean editMode);
  }

  private final StitchEditorModeController modeController;
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport;
  private final Function<T, String> sectionTitleResolver;
  private final ContentRenderer<T> contentRenderer;
  private final Consumer<T> onEnterEdit;
  private final BooleanSupplier onSave;
  private final Runnable onDiscard;
  private Predicate<T> editablePredicate = node -> true;
  private Function<T, List<Component>> readOnlyActionsProvider = node -> List.of();
  private Function<T, List<Component>> editActionsProvider = node -> List.of();

  private Runnable onStateChange = () -> {};

  public StitchEditableDetailPanel(
      StitchEditorModeController modeController,
      StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport,
      Function<T, String> sectionTitleResolver,
      ContentRenderer<T> contentRenderer,
      Consumer<T> onEnterEdit,
      BooleanSupplier onSave,
      Runnable onDiscard) {
    this.modeController = Objects.requireNonNull(modeController, "modeController");
    this.dirtyStateSupport = Objects.requireNonNull(dirtyStateSupport, "dirtyStateSupport");
    this.sectionTitleResolver = Objects.requireNonNull(sectionTitleResolver, "sectionTitleResolver");
    this.contentRenderer = Objects.requireNonNull(contentRenderer, "contentRenderer");
    this.onEnterEdit = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onEnterEdit, node -> {});
    this.onSave = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSave, () -> false);
    this.onDiscard = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onDiscard, () -> {});
  }

  public StitchEditableDetailPanel<T> onStateChange(Runnable callback) {
    onStateChange = Objects.requireNonNullElse(callback, () -> {});
    return this;
  }

  public StitchEditableDetailPanel<T> withEditablePredicate(Predicate<T> predicate) {
    editablePredicate = Objects.requireNonNullElse(predicate, node -> true);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchEditableDetailPanel<T> withReadOnlyActions(
      Function<T, List<Component>> actionsProvider) {
    readOnlyActionsProvider = Objects.requireNonNullElse(actionsProvider, node -> List.of());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchEditableDetailPanel<T> withEditActions(
      Function<T, List<Component>> actionsProvider) {
    editActionsProvider = Objects.requireNonNullElse(actionsProvider, node -> List.of());
    return this;
  }

  public Component render(T node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }

    StitchSection section = new StitchSection(sectionTitleResolver.apply(node));
    section.addSectionAction(buildActions(node));

    Component content = contentRenderer.render(node, modeController.isEditMode());
    if (content != null) {
      section.addToBody(content);
    }
    return section;
  }

  private Component[] buildActions(T node) {
    List<Component> readOnlyActions = sanitizeActions(readOnlyActionsProvider.apply(node));
    boolean editable = editablePredicate.test(node);

    if (!modeController.isEditMode()) {
      if (!editable) {
        return readOnlyActions.toArray(Component[]::new);
      }
      Button edit = new Button("EDIT", event -> enterEditMode(node));
      edit.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
      StitchActionStyles.applySecondary(edit);
      edit.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Edit selected item");
      List<Component> actions = new ArrayList<>();
      actions.add(edit);
      actions.addAll(readOnlyActions);
      return actions.toArray(Component[]::new);
    }

    List<Component> editActions = sanitizeActions(editActionsProvider.apply(node));
    if (!editActions.isEmpty()) {
      return editActions.toArray(Component[]::new);
    }

    Button save = new Button("SAVE", event -> saveRequested());
    save.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyPrimary(save);
    save.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Save changes");

    Button cancel = new Button("CANCEL", event -> cancelRequested());
    cancel.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchActionStyles.applyNeutral(cancel);
    cancel.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Cancel editing");

    return new Component[] {save, cancel};
  }

  private static List<Component> sanitizeActions(List<Component> actions) {
    if (actions == null || actions.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return actions.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
  }

  private void enterEditMode(T node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return;
    }
    modeController.enterEditMode();
    onEnterEdit.accept(node);
    onStateChange.run();
  }

  private void saveRequested() {
    if (!modeController.isEditMode()) {
      return;
    }
    if (onSave.getAsBoolean()) {
      modeController.clear();
      onStateChange.run();
    }
  }

  private void cancelRequested() {
    if (!modeController.hasUnsavedChanges()) {
      modeController.clear();
      onStateChange.run();
      return;
    }

    dirtyStateSupport.guard(
        () -> {
          if (onSave.getAsBoolean()) {
            modeController.clear();
            onStateChange.run();
            return true;
          }
          return false;
        },
        () -> {
          onDiscard.run();
          modeController.clear();
          onStateChange.run();
        },
        () -> {});
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchEditorModeController.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

/**
 * Shared edit mode state holder for detail editors.
 *
 * <p>Tracks whether a panel is in read-only or edit mode and whether unsaved changes exist.
 */
public final class StitchEditorModeController {
  private boolean editMode;
  private boolean dirty;

  public boolean isEditMode() {
    return editMode;
  }

  public boolean isReadOnly() {
    return !editMode;
  }

  public boolean hasUnsavedChanges() {
    return editMode && dirty;
  }

  public void enterEditMode() {
    editMode = true;
    dirty = false;
  }

  public void exitEditMode() {
    editMode = false;
  }

  public void markDirty() {
    if (editMode) {
      dirty = true;
    }
  }

  public void clearDirty() {
    dirty = false;
  }

  public void clear() {
    editMode = false;
    dirty = false;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.ButtonVariant;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveObserver;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.function.Predicate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchInspectorPreviewPanel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.support.StitchTextSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view.StitchPage;

/** Shared browser shell for hierarchical tree + inspector screens. */
public abstract class StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen extends StitchPage
    implements BeforeLeaveObserver {
  private final StitchEditorModeController editorMode = new StitchEditorModeController();
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport = new StitchDirtyStateSupport();
  private final StitchInspectorPreviewPanel inspectorPanel;
  private final StitchTreeNodeAdapter<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> nodeAdapter =
      new StitchTreeNodeAdapter<>() {
        @Override
        public String nodeId(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode node) {
          return node == null ? null : node.id();
        }

        @Override
        public StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode nodeById(String nodeId) {
          return nodeId == null ? null : nodesById.get(nodeId);
        }
      };

  private StitchEditableDetailPanel<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> detailPanel;
  private StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> browserShell;
  private Map<String, StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> nodesById = Map.of();

  protected StitchHierarchicalBrowserScreen(
      String pageTitle,
      String pageSubtitle,
      String refreshAriaLabel,
      String refreshTitle,
      String previewLabel,
      String previewAriaLabel) {
    super(
        Objects.requireNonNull(pageTitle, "pageTitle"),
        pageSubtitle == null ? "" : pageSubtitle);
    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();

    Button refresh = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRequested());
    refresh.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL);
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refresh);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", Strings.firstNonBlank(refreshAriaLabel, "Refresh"));
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", Strings.firstNonBlank(refreshTitle, "Refresh"));
    addPageAction(refresh);

    this.inspectorPanel =
        new StitchInspectorPreviewPanel(
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previewLabel, "Preview"),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(previewAriaLabel, "Inspector preview"));
  }

  protected final void initBrowser(
      BrowserConfig config,
      EditConfig editConfig,
      Function<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode, String> detailTitleResolver,
      StitchEditableDetailPanel.ContentRenderer<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode>
          detailContentBuilder,
      Function<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode, List<Component>> readOnlyActionsProvider,
      Consumer<String> selectionApplied) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(config, "config");
    Objects.requireNonNull(editConfig, "editConfig");
    Objects.requireNonNull(detailTitleResolver, "detailTitleResolver");
    Objects.requireNonNull(detailContentBuilder, "detailContentBuilder");

    detailPanel =
        new StitchEditableDetailPanel<>(
                editorMode,
                dirtyStateSupport,
                detailTitleResolver,
                detailContentBuilder,
                node -> {},
                editConfig.saveChanges(),
                editConfig.discardChanges())
            .withEditablePredicate(editConfig.editablePredicate())
            .withReadOnlyActions(
                readOnlyActionsProvider == null ? node -> List.of() : readOnlyActionsProvider)
            .withEditActions(editConfig.editActionsProvider())
            .onStateChange(this::rerenderDetails);

    browserShell =
        new StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<>(
            nodeAdapter,
            dirtyStateSupport,
            editConfig.hasUnsavedChanges(),
            editConfig.saveChanges(),
            editConfig.discardChanges(),
            nodeId -> {
              editorMode.clear();
              rerenderDetails();
              if (selectionApplied != null) {
                selectionApplied.accept(nodeId);
              }
            });
    browserShell
        .setNavHeaderTitle(config.navHeaderTitle())
        .setDetailHeaderTitle(config.detailHeaderTitle())
        .setNoSelectionContent(config.noSelectionContent())
        .setNoDetailsContent(config.noDetailsContent())
        .setChildResolver(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode::children)
        .setLabelResolver(StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode::label)
        .setNodeIconRenderer(config.nodeIconRenderer())
        .setNodeDecoratorRenderer(config.nodeDecoratorRenderer())
        .setDetailRenderer(detailPanel::render);

    if (config.toolbarActions() != null && config.toolbarActions().length > 0) {
      browserShell.addToolbarActions(config.toolbarActions());
    }
    browserShell.treeNav().searchField().setPlaceholder(config.searchPlaceholder());
    browserShell.treeNav().searchField().setAriaLabel(config.searchAriaLabel());

    addToBody(browserShell);
  }

  protected abstract void refreshRequested();

  @Override
  public final void beforeLeave(BeforeLeaveEvent event) {
    if (browserShell != null) {
      browserShell.guardBeforeLeave(event);
    }
  }

  protected final StitchInspectorPreviewPanel inspectorPanel() {
    return inspectorPanel;
  }

  protected final StitchEditorModeController editorMode() {
    return editorMode;
  }

  protected final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport() {
    return dirtyStateSupport;
  }

  protected final StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> browserShell() {
    return browserShell;
  }

  protected final StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode selectedNode() {
    String selectedNodeId = browserShell == null ? null : browserShell.selectedNodeId();
    return selectedNodeId == null ? null : nodesById.get(selectedNodeId);
  }

  protected final void applyTree(
      Collection<? extends StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> roots,
      Map<String, StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> byId,
      Component noSelectionContent,
      Component noDetailsContent,
      String desiredSelectionId,
      Predicate<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> preferredSelection) {
    this.nodesById = byId == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(byId);
    browserShell.setNoSelectionContent(noSelectionContent);
    browserShell.setNoDetailsContent(noDetailsContent);
    browserShell.setRoots(roots == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(roots));
    String nextSelection = chooseSelection(roots, desiredSelectionId, preferredSelection);
    editorMode.clear();
    browserShell.applySelectionById(nextSelection);
  }

  protected final void clearTree(Component noSelectionContent, Component noDetailsContent) {
    applyTree(List.of(), Map.of(), noSelectionContent, noDetailsContent, null, null);
  }

  protected final void rerenderDetails() {
    if (browserShell != null && detailPanel != null) {
      browserShell.setDetailRenderer(detailPanel::render);
    }
  }

  protected static String rootMessage(Throwable error) {
    return StitchTextSupport.rootMessage(error);
  }

  protected static String formatBytes(long bytes) {
    if (bytes < 0L) {
      return "-";
    }
    if (bytes < 1024L) {
      return bytes + " B";
    }
    double kb = bytes / 1024.0d;
    if (kb < 1024.0d) {
      return String.format(java.util.Locale.ROOT, "%.1f KB", kb);
    }
    double mb = kb / 1024.0d;
    if (mb < 1024.0d) {
      return String.format(java.util.Locale.ROOT, "%.1f MB", mb);
    }
    double gb = mb / 1024.0d;
    return String.format(java.util.Locale.ROOT, "%.2f GB", gb);
  }

  private String chooseSelection(
      Collection<? extends StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> roots,
      String desiredSelectionId,
      Predicate<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> preferredSelection) {
    if (desiredSelectionId != null && nodesById.containsKey(desiredSelectionId)) {
      return desiredSelectionId;
    }
    return null;
  }

  public record BrowserConfig(
      String navHeaderTitle,
      String detailHeaderTitle,
      Component noSelectionContent,
      Component noDetailsContent,
      String searchPlaceholder,
      String searchAriaLabel,
      Function<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode, Component> nodeIconRenderer,
      Function<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode, Component> nodeDecoratorRenderer,
      Component... toolbarActions) {}

  public record EditConfig(
      BooleanSupplier hasUnsavedChanges,
      BooleanSupplier saveChanges,
      Runnable discardChanges,
      Predicate<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> editablePredicate,
      Function<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode, List<Component>> editActionsProvider) {

    public EditConfig(
        BooleanSupplier hasUnsavedChanges,
        BooleanSupplier saveChanges,
        Runnable discardChanges,
        Predicate<StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.TreeNode> editablePredicate) {
      this(
          hasUnsavedChanges,
          saveChanges,
          discardChanges,
          editablePredicate,
          node -> List.of());
    }

    public EditConfig {
      hasUnsavedChanges = hasUnsavedChanges == null ? () -> false : hasUnsavedChanges;
      saveChanges = saveChanges == null ? () -> true : saveChanges;
      discardChanges = discardChanges == null ? () -> {} : discardChanges;
      editablePredicate = editablePredicate == null ? node -> false : editablePredicate;
      editActionsProvider = editActionsProvider == null ? node -> List.of() : editActionsProvider;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.router.BeforeLeaveEvent;
import com.vaadin.flow.shared.Registration;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BooleanSupplier;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import java.util.function.Predicate;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Shared mid-level shell for hierarchical tree browsers.
 *
 * <p>Combines tree layout and selection/dirty-state orchestration so browser screens only provide
 * domain-specific data loading and detail rendering.
 */
public final class StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchTreeLayout<T> layout = new StitchTreeLayout<>();
  private final StitchTreeNodeAdapter<T> nodeAdapter;
  private final StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport;
  private final BooleanSupplier hasUnsavedChanges;
  private final BooleanSupplier saveChanges;
  private final Runnable discardChanges;
  private final Consumer<String> onSelectionApplied;

  private String selectedNodeId;
  private String pendingSelectionId;
  private boolean suppressSelectionEvents;

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell(
      StitchTreeNodeAdapter<T> nodeAdapter,
      StitchDirtyStateSupport dirtyStateSupport,
      BooleanSupplier hasUnsavedChanges,
      BooleanSupplier saveChanges,
      Runnable discardChanges,
      Consumer<String> onSelectionApplied) {
    this.nodeAdapter = Objects.requireNonNull(nodeAdapter, "nodeAdapter");
    this.dirtyStateSupport = Objects.requireNonNull(dirtyStateSupport, "dirtyStateSupport");
    this.hasUnsavedChanges = Objects.requireNonNullElse(hasUnsavedChanges, () -> false);
    this.saveChanges = Objects.requireNonNullElse(saveChanges, () -> false);
    this.discardChanges = Objects.requireNonNullElse(discardChanges, () -> {});
    this.onSelectionApplied = Objects.requireNonNullElse(onSelectionApplied, value -> {});

    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    layout.setSizeFull();
    add(layout);
    setFlexGrow(1, layout);

    layout.treeNav().onSelectionChange(this::handleSelectionRequest);
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setNavHeaderTitle(String value) {
    layout.setNavHeaderTitle(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setDetailHeaderTitle(String value) {
    layout.setDetailHeaderTitle(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setDetailHeaderActions(Component... components) {
    layout.setDetailHeaderActions(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setNoSelectionContent(Component value) {
    layout.setNoSelectionContent(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setNoDetailsContent(Component value) {
    layout.setNoDetailsContent(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setChildResolver(
      Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> value) {
    layout.setChildResolver(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setLabelResolver(Function<T, String> value) {
    layout.setLabelResolver(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setNodeIconRenderer(Function<T, Component> value) {
    layout.setNodeIconRenderer(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setNodeDecoratorRenderer(Function<T, Component> value) {
    layout.setNodeDecoratorRenderer(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> addToolbarActions(Component... components) {
    layout.addToolbarActions(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(boolean enabled) {
    layout.withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(enabled);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> withCheckboxSelectionMode(
      StitchTreeNav.CheckboxSelectionMode mode) {
    layout.withCheckboxSelectionMode(mode);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> withCheckboxAutoTriggerCount(Integer count) {
    layout.withCheckboxAutoTriggerCount(count);
    return this;
  }

    layout.withCheckboxMaxCheckedCount(count);

  public Registration onCheckedItemsChanged(Consumer<List<T>> listener) {
    return layout.treeNav().onCheckedItemsChanged(listener);
  }

  public Registration onAutoThresholdReached(Consumer<List<T>> listener) {
    return layout.treeNav().onAutoThresholdReached(listener);
  }

  public List<T> checkedItems() {
    return layout.treeNav().checkedItems();
  }

    layout.setCheckedItems(checkedItems);
    return this;

    layout.clearCheckedItems();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setDetailRenderer(
