    layout.setDetailRenderer(renderer);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchHierarchicalBrowserShell<T> setRoots(Collection<? extends T> roots) {
    layout.setRoots(roots);
    return this;
  }

  public String selectedNodeId() {
    return selectedNodeId;
  }

  public void setSelectedNodeId(String value) {
    selectedNodeId = value;
  }

  public void applySelectionById(String value) {
    selectedNodeId = value;
    pendingSelectionId = null;
    restoreTreeSelection(value);
    onSelectionApplied.accept(value);
  }

  public void syncSelection() {
    layout.treeNav().expandAll();
    restoreTreeSelection(selectedNodeId);
  }

  public void guardBeforeLeave(BeforeLeaveEvent event) {
    dirtyStateSupport.guardBeforeLeave(event, hasUnsavedChanges, saveChanges, discardChanges);
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> treeNav() {
    return layout.treeNav();
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> layout() {
    return layout;
  }

  private void handleSelectionRequest(T requestedNode) {
    if (suppressSelectionEvents) {
      return;
    }

    String requestedId = requestedNode == null ? null : nodeAdapter.nodeId(requestedNode);
    if (requestedId != null && requestedId.equals(selectedNodeId)) {
      return;
    }

    if (hasUnsavedChanges.getAsBoolean() && selectedNodeId != null) {
      pendingSelectionId = requestedId;
      restoreTreeSelection(selectedNodeId);
      dirtyStateSupport.guard(
          () -> {
            if (saveChanges.getAsBoolean()) {
              applySelectionById(pendingSelectionId);
              return true;
            }
            return false;
          },
          () -> {
            discardChanges.run();
            applySelectionById(pendingSelectionId);
          },
          () -> restoreTreeSelection(selectedNodeId));
      return;
    }

    applySelectionById(requestedId);
  }

  private void restoreTreeSelection(String nodeId) {
    suppressSelectionEvents = true;
    T node = nodeId == null ? null : nodeAdapter.nodeById(nodeId);
    layout.treeNav().select(node);
    suppressSelectionEvents = false;
  }

  public static <T> String firstNodeId(
      Collection<? extends T> roots, Function<T, String> idResolver) {
    if (roots == null || roots.isEmpty() || idResolver == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (T root : roots) {
      if (root != null) {
        return idResolver.apply(root);
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public static <T> String firstMatchingNodeId(
      Collection<? extends T> roots,
      Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> childResolver,
      Function<T, String> idResolver,
      Predicate<T> predicate) {
    if (roots == null || roots.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> children;
    if (childResolver == null) {
      children = value -> List.of();
    } else {
      children = childResolver;
    }
    Function<T, String> resolveId = Objects.requireNonNullElse(idResolver, value -> null);
    Predicate<T> matcher = Objects.requireNonNullElse(predicate, value -> false);
    for (T root : roots) {
      String found = firstMatchingNodeId(root, children, resolveId, matcher);
      if (found != null) {
        return found;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static <T> String firstMatchingNodeId(
      T node,
      Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> childResolver,
      Function<T, String> idResolver,
      Predicate<T> predicate) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (predicate.test(node)) {
      return idResolver.apply(node);
    }
    Collection<? extends T> children = childResolver.apply(node);
    if (children == null || children.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (T child : children) {
      String found = firstMatchingNodeId(child, childResolver, idResolver, predicate);
      if (found != null) {
        return found;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public static boolean copyText(Component source, String text) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(source, "source");
    String value = Strings.trimToNull(text);
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    source
        .getUI()
        .ifPresent(
            ui ->
                ui.getPage()
                    .executeJs(
                        """
                        const text = $0;
                        const fallbackCopy = (value) => {
                          const area = document.createElement('textarea');
                          area.value = value;
                          area.style.position = 'fixed';
                          area.style.left = '-9999px';
                          document.body.appendChild(area);
                          area.focus();
                          area.select();
                          try { document.execCommand('copy'); } finally { document.body.removeChild(area); }
                        };
                        if (navigator.clipboard && window.isSecureContext) {
                          navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(() => fallbackCopy(text));
                        } else {
                          fallbackCopy(text);
                        }
                        """,
                        value));
    return true;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/**
 * Builds a reusable hierarchical tree from flat slash-delimited keys.
 *
 * <p>Example input keys:
 *
 * <pre>
 * core/APP/client
 * lab/CONFIG/movies
 * </pre>
 *
 * <p>Produces a stable tree and by-id map suitable for {@link StitchTreeNav}.
 */
public final class StitchHierarchicalKeyAdapter {

  public Model build(List<String> keys) {
    MutableNode root = new MutableNode("", "");
    if (keys != null) {
      for (String rawKey : keys) {
        String key = normalizeKey(rawKey);
        if (key == null) {
          continue;
        }
        MutableNode cursor = root;
        StringBuilder path = new StringBuilder();
        for (String segment : splitSegments(key)) {
          if (path.length() > 0) {
            path.append('/');
          }
          path.append(segment);
          String nodeId = path.toString();
          cursor =
              cursor.children.computeIfAbsent(
                  nodeId, missingNodeId -> new MutableNode(missingNodeId, segment));
        }
        cursor.leafKey = key;
      }
    }

    LinkedHashMap<String, TreeNode> byId = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<TreeNode> roots = freezeNodes(root.children.values(), byId);
    return new Model(List.copyOf(roots), Map.copyOf(byId));
  }

  public static String normalizeKey(String key) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String collapsed = normalized.replace('\\', '/').replaceAll("/+", "/");
    while (collapsed.startsWith("/")) {
      collapsed = collapsed.substring(1);
    }
    while (collapsed.endsWith("/")) {
      collapsed = collapsed.substring(0, collapsed.length() - 1);
    }
    return collapsed.isBlank() ? null : collapsed;
  }

  public static List<String> splitSegments(String normalizedKey) {
    if (normalizedKey == null || normalizedKey.isBlank()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    String[] rawParts = normalizedKey.split("/");
    List<String> parts = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String raw : rawParts) {
      String part = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
      if (part != null) {
        parts.add(part);
      }
    }
    if (parts.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of(normalizedKey);
    }
    return List.copyOf(parts);
  }

  private static List<TreeNode> freezeNodes(
      java.util.Collection<MutableNode> mutableNodes, LinkedHashMap<String, TreeNode> byId) {
    List<MutableNode> ordered = new ArrayList<>(mutableNodes);
    ordered.sort(Comparator.comparing(node -> node.label.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)));
    List<TreeNode> frozen = new ArrayList<>();
    for (MutableNode mutable : ordered) {
      List<TreeNode> children = freezeNodes(mutable.children.values(), byId);
      TreeNode node =
          new TreeNode(
              mutable.id, mutable.label, mutable.leafKey, List.copyOf(children), mutable.leafKey != null);
      byId.put(node.id(), node);
      frozen.add(node);
    }
    return frozen;
  }

  public record TreeNode(
      String id, String label, String fullKey, List<TreeNode> children, boolean payloadNode) {}

  public record Model(List<TreeNode> roots, Map<String, TreeNode> byId) {}

  private static final class MutableNode {
    private final String id;
    private final String label;
    private String leafKey;
    private final LinkedHashMap<String, MutableNode> children = new LinkedHashMap<>();

    private MutableNode(String id, String label) {
      this.id = id;
      this.label = label;
    }
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/tree/StitchTreeLayout.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.splitlayout.SplitLayout;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.stream.Stream;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchSectionHeader;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchTreeLayout<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchTreeNav<T> treeNav;
  private final SplitLayout split = new SplitLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout navPanel = new VerticalLayout();
  private final VerticalLayout detailPanel = new VerticalLayout();
  private final StitchSectionHeader navHeader = new StitchSectionHeader("Navigation");
  private final StitchSectionHeader detailHeader = new StitchSectionHeader("Details");
  private final Div detailHost = new Div();
  private final StitchEmptyState noSelectionState =
      new StitchEmptyState("No node selected", "Select a tree node to view details.");
  private final StitchEmptyState noDetailsState =
      new StitchEmptyState("No details available", "No detail view is configured for this node.");

  private Component noSelectionContent = noSelectionState;
  private Component noDetailsContent = noDetailsState;
  private Function<T, Component> detailRenderer = value -> null;
  private boolean autoNavSizingEnabled;
  private int autoNavMinWidthPx = 280;
  private int autoNavMaxWidthPx = 620;

  public StitchTreeLayout() {
    this(new StitchTreeNav<>());
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout(StitchTreeNav<T> treeNav) {
    this.treeNav = Objects.requireNonNull(treeNav, "treeNav");
    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    addClassName("stitch-tree-layout");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_LAYOUT);

    split.setSizeFull();
    split.setSplitterPosition(26);
    split.addClassName("stitch-tree-layout-split");
    split.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Tree navigation layout");
    StitchComponents.withCode(split, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_SPLIT);

    navPanel.setSizeFull();
    navPanel.setPadding(false);
    navPanel.setSpacing(false);
    navPanel.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-panel");
    StitchComponents.withCode(navPanel, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_PANEL);
    navHeader.addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header");
    navHeader.left().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-left");
    navHeader.right().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-actions");
    navHeader.title().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-title");
    navHeader.withRight(treeNav.headerActions());
    navPanel.add(navHeader, treeNav);
    navPanel.setFlexGrow(1, treeNav);

    detailPanel.setSizeFull();
    detailPanel.setPadding(false);
    detailPanel.setSpacing(false);
    detailPanel.addClassName("stitch-tree-detail-panel");
    StitchComponents.withCode(detailPanel, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_DETAIL_PANEL);
    detailHeader.addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header");
    detailHeader.left().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-left");
    detailHeader.right().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-actions");
    detailHeader.title().addClassName("stitch-tree-panel-header-title");
    detailHeader.withRight();

    detailHost.setSizeFull();
    detailHost.addClassName("stitch-tree-detail-host");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("role", "region");
    detailHost.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Selected node details");
    StitchComponents.withCode(detailHost, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_DETAIL_CONTENT);
    detailPanel.add(detailHeader, detailHost);
    detailPanel.setFlexGrow(1, detailHost);

    split.addToPrimary(navPanel);
    split.addToSecondary(detailPanel);
    add(split);
    setFlexGrow(1, split);

    this.treeNav.onSelectionChange(this::renderSelectionDetails);
    this.treeNav.onVisibleContentMetricsChanged(this::applyAutoNavSizing);
    renderSelectionDetails(null);
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setRoots(Collection<? extends T> roots) {
    treeNav.setRoots(roots);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> withAutoNavSizing(int minWidthPx, int maxWidthPx) {
    int normalizedMin = Math.max(220, minWidthPx);
    int normalizedMax = Math.max(normalizedMin + 80, maxWidthPx);
    this.autoNavSizingEnabled = true;
    this.autoNavMinWidthPx = normalizedMin;
    this.autoNavMaxWidthPx = normalizedMax;
    split
        .getElement()
        .executeJs(
            "this.style.setProperty('--stitch-tree-nav-min-width', `${Math.round($0)}px`);"
                + "this.style.setProperty('--stitch-tree-nav-max-width', `${Math.round($1)}px`);",
            normalizedMin,
            normalizedMax);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setChildResolver(
      Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> childResolver) {
    treeNav.setChildResolver(childResolver);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setLabelResolver(Function<T, String> labelResolver) {
    treeNav.setLabelResolver(labelResolver);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setNodeIconRenderer(Function<T, Component> iconRenderer) {
    treeNav.setNodeIconRenderer(iconRenderer);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setNodeDecoratorRenderer(Function<T, Component> decoratorRenderer) {
    treeNav.setNodeDecoratorRenderer(decoratorRenderer);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> addToolbarActions(Component... components) {
    treeNav.addToolbarActions(components);
    return this;
  }

    treeNav.clearToolbarActions();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(boolean enabled) {
    treeNav.withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(enabled);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> withCheckboxSelectionMode(StitchTreeNav.CheckboxSelectionMode mode) {
    treeNav.withCheckboxSelectionMode(mode);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> withCheckboxAutoTriggerCount(Integer count) {

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> onCheckedItemsChanged(Consumer<List<T>> listener) {
    treeNav.onCheckedItemsChanged(listener);

  }

    treeNav.onAutoThresholdReached(listener);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> clearCheckedItems() {
    treeNav.clearCheckedItems();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setCheckedItems(Collection<? extends T> checkedItems) {
    treeNav.setCheckedItems(checkedItems);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setDetailRenderer(Function<T, ? extends Component> renderer) {
    if (renderer == null) {
      detailRenderer = value -> null;
    } else {
      detailRenderer = value -> renderer.apply(value);
    }
    renderSelectionDetails(treeNav.selectedItem());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setNoSelectionContent(Component content) {
    noSelectionContent = content == null ? noSelectionState : content;
    renderSelectionDetails(treeNav.selectedItem());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setNoDetailsContent(Component content) {
    noDetailsContent = content == null ? noDetailsState : content;
    renderSelectionDetails(treeNav.selectedItem());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setNavHeaderTitle(String value) {
    navHeader.withTitle(value);
    navHeader.setVisible(value != null && !value.trim().isBlank());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setDetailHeaderTitle(String value) {
    detailHeader.withTitle(value);
    detailHeader.setVisible(value != null && !value.trim().isBlank());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeLayout<T> setDetailHeaderActions(Component... components) {
    detailHeader.withRight();
    if (components != null) {
      Stream.of(components).filter(Objects::nonNull).forEach(detailHeader::addRight);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> treeNav() {
    return treeNav;
  }

  public SplitLayout split() {
    return split;
  }

  public Div detailHost() {
    return detailHost;
  }

  private void renderSelectionDetails(T selected) {
    detailHost.removeAll();
    if (selected == null) {
      detailHost.add(noSelectionContent);
      return;
    }
    Component details = detailRenderer.apply(selected);
    if (details == null) {
      detailHost.add(noDetailsContent);
      return;
    }
    detailHost.add(details);
  }

  private void applyAutoNavSizing(StitchTreeNav.VisibleContentMetrics metrics) {
    if (!autoNavSizingEnabled || metrics == null) {
      return;
    }
    int suggestedWidth =
        autoNavMinWidthPx
            + (metrics.maxLabelLength() * 7)
            + (metrics.maxDepth() * 22)
            + (metrics.visibleNodeCount() > 40 ? 12 : 0);
    int targetWidth = Math.max(autoNavMinWidthPx, Math.min(autoNavMaxWidthPx, suggestedWidth));
    split
        .getElement()
        .executeJs(
            """
            const split = this;
            const minPx = Number($0);
            const maxPx = Number($1);
            const targetPx = Number($2);
            split.style.setProperty('--stitch-tree-nav-min-width', `${Math.round(minPx)}px`);
            split.style.setProperty('--stitch-tree-nav-max-width', `${Math.round(maxPx)}px`);
            const width = split.getBoundingClientRect().width;
            if (!width || width <= 0) {
              return;
            }
            const bounded = Math.max(minPx, Math.min(maxPx, targetPx));
            const targetPct = Math.max(14, Math.min(66, (bounded / width) * 100));
            const raw = String(split.splitterPosition || '').trim();
            const currentPct = parseFloat(raw.endsWith('%') ? raw.slice(0, -1) : raw);
            if (!Number.isFinite(currentPct) || currentPct + 0.6 < targetPct) {
              split.splitterPosition = `${targetPct.toFixed(2)}%`;
            }
            """,
            autoNavMinWidthPx,
            autoNavMaxWidthPx,
            targetWidth);
  }
}

public class StitchTreeNav<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchResultsSearch search = new StitchResultsSearch("Search tree", "Search tree nodes");
  private final HorizontalLayout toolbar = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout customActions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout builtInActions = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final Button expandAllButton =
      new Button(VaadinIcon.PLUS_SQUARE_O.create(), event -> expandAll());
  private final Button collapseAllButton =
      new Button(VaadinIcon.MINUS_SQUARE_O.create(), event -> collapseAll());
  private final TreeGrid<T> tree = new TreeGrid<>();
  private final List<Consumer<T>> selectionListeners = new ArrayList<>();
  private final List<Consumer<List<T>>> checkedItemsChangedListeners = new ArrayList<>();
  private final List<Consumer<List<T>>> autoThresholdReachedListeners = new ArrayList<>();
  private final Map<T, T> parentByNode = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final Map<T, List<T>> childrenByNode = new LinkedHashMap<>();
  private final List<T> nodeOrder = new ArrayList<>();
  private final List<T> checkedItems = new ArrayList<>();
  private final Set<T> checkedNodes = newIdentitySet();
  private final Set<T> visibleNodes = newIdentitySet();

  private List<T> rootNodes = List.of();
  private Function<T, Collection<? extends T>> childResolver = value -> List.of();
  private Function<T, String> labelResolver = value -> value == null ? "" : value.toString();
  private Function<T, Component> iconRenderer = value -> null;
  private Function<T, Component> decoratorRenderer = value -> null;
  private Function<T, String> labelClassNameProvider = value -> null;
  private NodeIconClickBehavior nodeIconClickBehavior = NodeIconClickBehavior.SELECT;
  private boolean customActionsTrailing;
  private boolean checkboxSelectionEnabled;
  private CheckboxSelectionMode checkboxSelectionMode = CheckboxSelectionMode.LEAF_ONLY;
  private Integer checkboxAutoTriggerCount;
  private Integer checkboxMaxCheckedCount;
  private Consumer<VisibleContentMetrics> visibleContentMetricsListener = metrics -> {};

  public StitchTreeNav() {
    setSizeFull();
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    addClassName("stitch-tree-nav");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV);

    search.setWidthFull();
    search.onQueryChange(value -> applyFilter());

    configureToolbar();
    configureTree();

    add(search, tree);
    setFlexGrow(1, tree);
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setRoots(Collection<? extends T> roots) {
    rootNodes = normalizeNodes(roots);
    rebuildIndex();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withCheckboxSelectionEnabled(boolean enabled) {
    checkboxSelectionEnabled = enabled;
    reconcileCheckedItems();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public boolean checkboxSelectionEnabled() {
    return checkboxSelectionEnabled;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withCheckboxSelectionMode(CheckboxSelectionMode mode) {
    checkboxSelectionMode = mode == null ? CheckboxSelectionMode.LEAF_ONLY : mode;
    reconcileCheckedItems();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public CheckboxSelectionMode checkboxSelectionMode() {
    return checkboxSelectionMode;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withCheckboxAutoTriggerCount(Integer count) {
    checkboxAutoTriggerCount = normalizePositive(count);
    return this;
  }

  public Integer checkboxAutoTriggerCount() {
    return checkboxAutoTriggerCount;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withCheckboxMaxCheckedCount(Integer count) {
    checkboxMaxCheckedCount = normalizePositive(count);
    reconcileCheckedItems();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public Integer checkboxMaxCheckedCount() {
    return checkboxMaxCheckedCount;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setChildResolver(Function<T, ? extends Collection<? extends T>> resolver) {
    if (resolver == null) {
      childResolver = value -> List.of();
    } else {
      childResolver = value -> {
        Collection<? extends T> resolved = resolver.apply(value);
        return resolved == null ? List.of() : resolved;
      };
    }
    rebuildIndex();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setLabelResolver(Function<T, String> resolver) {
    labelResolver = resolver == null ? value -> value == null ? "" : value.toString() : resolver;
    rebuildIndex();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setNodeIconRenderer(Function<T, Component> renderer) {
    iconRenderer = renderer == null ? value -> null : renderer;
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setNodeDecoratorRenderer(Function<T, Component> renderer) {
    decoratorRenderer = renderer == null ? value -> null : renderer;
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setNodeLabelClassNameProvider(Function<T, String> provider) {
    labelClassNameProvider = provider == null ? value -> null : provider;
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withNodeIconClickBehavior(NodeIconClickBehavior behavior) {
    nodeIconClickBehavior =
        behavior == null ? NodeIconClickBehavior.SELECT : behavior;
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public NodeIconClickBehavior nodeIconClickBehavior() {
    return nodeIconClickBehavior;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> addToolbarActions(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      customActions.add(components);
    }
    syncToolbarOrder();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> clearToolbarActions() {
    customActions.removeAll();
    syncToolbarOrder();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> withCustomActionsTrailing(boolean trailing) {
    customActionsTrailing = trailing;
    syncToolbarOrder();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setSearchQuery(String value) {
    search.setValue(value == null ? "" : value);
    return this;
  }

  public String searchQuery() {
    return search.getValue();
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> expandAll() {
    List<T> roots = visibleRootNodes();
    if (!roots.isEmpty()) {
      tree.expandRecursively(roots, Integer.MAX_VALUE);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> collapseAll() {
    List<T> roots = visibleRootNodes();
    if (!roots.isEmpty()) {
      tree.collapseRecursively(roots, Integer.MAX_VALUE);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> select(T value) {
    if (value == null || !visibleNodes.contains(value)) {
      tree.deselectAll();
      return this;
    }
    expandAncestors(value);
    tree.select(value);
    return this;
  }

  public boolean selectFirstMatching(Predicate<T> predicate) {
    Predicate<T> matcher = Objects.requireNonNull(predicate, "predicate");
    for (T candidate : nodeOrder) {
      if (candidate != null && visibleNodes.contains(candidate) && matcher.test(candidate)) {
        select(candidate);
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  public T selectedItem() {
    return tree.asSingleSelect().getValue();
  }

  public Registration onSelectionChange(Consumer<T> listener) {
    Consumer<T> callback = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    selectionListeners.add(callback);
    return () -> selectionListeners.remove(callback);
  }

  public Registration onCheckedItemsChanged(Consumer<List<T>> listener) {
    Consumer<List<T>> callback = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    checkedItemsChangedListeners.add(callback);
    return () -> checkedItemsChangedListeners.remove(callback);
  }

  public Registration onAutoThresholdReached(Consumer<List<T>> listener) {
    Consumer<List<T>> callback = Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    autoThresholdReachedListeners.add(callback);
    return () -> autoThresholdReachedListeners.remove(callback);
  }

  public List<T> checkedItems() {
    return List.copyOf(checkedItems);
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> clearCheckedItems() {
    if (checkedItems.isEmpty()) {
      return this;
    }
    checkedItems.clear();
    checkedNodes.clear();
    notifyCheckedItemsChanged();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setCheckedItems(Collection<? extends T> values) {
    clearCheckedItems();
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty() || !checkboxSelectionEnabled) {
      return this;
    }
    for (T value : values) {
      if (!canCheckNode(value)) {
        continue;
      }
      checkedItems.add(value);
      checkedNodes.add(value);
      if (hasReachedMaxCheckedCount()) {
        break;
      }
    }
    notifyCheckedItemsChanged();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsSearch searchField() {
    return search;
  }

  public TreeGrid<T> tree() {
    return tree;
  }

  public Component headerActions() {
    return toolbar;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> setExpandCollapseEnabled(boolean enabled) {
    expandAllButton.setEnabled(enabled);
    collapseAllButton.setEnabled(enabled);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchTreeNav<T> onVisibleContentMetricsChanged(
      Consumer<VisibleContentMetrics> listener) {
    visibleContentMetricsListener = Objects.requireNonNullElse(listener, metrics -> {});
    notifyVisibleContentMetrics();
    return this;
  }

  private void configureToolbar() {
    toolbar.setPadding(false);
    toolbar.setSpacing(false);
    toolbar.setWidth(null);
    toolbar.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    toolbar.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-toolbar");
    StitchComponents.withCode(toolbar, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_TOOLBAR);

    customActions.setPadding(false);
    customActions.setSpacing(false);
    customActions.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    customActions.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-toolbar-custom");
    StitchComponents.withCode(customActions, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_ACTIONS);

    builtInActions.setPadding(false);
    builtInActions.setSpacing(false);
    builtInActions.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    builtInActions.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-toolbar-expand-collapse");
    StitchComponents.withCode(builtInActions, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_EXPAND_COLLAPSE);

    configureToolbarButton(
        expandAllButton,
        "Expand all tree nodes",
        StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_EXPAND_BUTTON);
    configureToolbarButton(
        collapseAllButton,
        "Collapse all tree nodes",
        StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_COLLAPSE_BUTTON);

    builtInActions.add(expandAllButton, collapseAllButton);
    syncToolbarOrder();
  }

  private void configureToolbarButton(Button button, String ariaLabel, String code) {
    button.addThemeVariants(ButtonVariant.LUMO_SMALL, ButtonVariant.LUMO_TERTIARY);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", ariaLabel);
    button.getElement().setAttribute("title", ariaLabel);
    button.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-button");
    StitchComponents.withCode(button, code);
  }

  private void syncToolbarOrder() {
    toolbar.removeAll();
    if (customActionsTrailing) {
      toolbar.add(builtInActions, customActions);
      return;
    }
    toolbar.add(customActions, builtInActions);
  }

  private void configureTree() {
    tree.setSizeFull();
    tree.setWidthFull();
    tree.setSelectionMode(Grid.SelectionMode.SINGLE);
    tree.addThemeVariants(GridVariant.LUMO_COMPACT, GridVariant.LUMO_NO_BORDER);
    tree.addClassName("stitch-tree-nav-grid");
    tree.setAriaLabel("Tree navigation");
    StitchComponents.withCode(tree, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_TREE_NAV_GRID);

    tree.addComponentHierarchyColumn(this::buildNodeContent).setHeader("Name").setFlexGrow(1).setKey("name");

    tree.addSelectionListener(event -> notifySelection(event.getFirstSelectedItem().orElse(null)));
    applyFilter();
  }

  private Component buildNodeContent(T node) {
    HorizontalLayout content = new HorizontalLayout();
    content.setPadding(false);
    content.setSpacing(false);
    content.setWidthFull();
    content.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    content.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-content");

    if (checkboxSelectionEnabled) {
      content.add(buildSelectionCheckbox(node));
    }

    HorizontalLayout lead = new HorizontalLayout();
    lead.setPadding(false);
    lead.setSpacing(false);
    lead.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    lead.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-leading");

    Component icon = iconRenderer.apply(node);
    if (icon != null) {
      icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-hidden", "true");
      icon.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-icon");
      if (nodeIconClickBehavior == NodeIconClickBehavior.TOGGLE_EXPAND_COLLAPSE) {
        icon.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-icon-toggle");
        if (hasChildren(node)) {
          stopClickPropagation(icon);
          icon.getElement().setAttribute("title", "Expand/collapse");
          icon.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Expand/collapse");
          icon.getElement().addEventListener("click", event -> toggleExpanded(node));
        }
      }
      lead.add(icon);
    }

    Span label = new Span(labelOf(node));
    label.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-label");
    applyClassNames(label, labelClassNameProvider.apply(node));
    stopClickPropagation(label);
    label.addClickListener(event -> select(node));
    lead.add(label);
    if (nodeIconClickBehavior == NodeIconClickBehavior.SELECT) {
      lead.addClickListener(event -> select(node));
    }

    Div spacer = new Div();
    spacer.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-spacer");
    content.add(lead, spacer);
    content.expand(spacer);

    Component decorator = decoratorRenderer.apply(node);
    if (decorator != null) {
      decorator.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-decorator");
      content.add(decorator);
    }

    return content;
  }

  private Checkbox buildSelectionCheckbox(T node) {
    Checkbox checkbox = new Checkbox();
    checkbox.addClassName("stitch-tree-node-checkbox");
    checkbox.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Select " + labelOf(node));
    boolean checked = checkedNodes.contains(node);
    checkbox.setValue(checked);

    boolean eligible = isCheckboxEligible(node);
    boolean disabledByLimit = hasReachedMaxCheckedCount() && !checked;
    checkbox.setEnabled(eligible && !disabledByLimit);
    checkbox.setIndeterminate(false);
    checkbox.addValueChangeListener(
        event -> {
          if (!event.isFromClient()) {
            return;
          }
          if (!event.getValue()) {
            removeCheckedNode(node);
            return;
          }
          if (!canCheckNode(node) || hasReachedMaxCheckedCount()) {
            checkbox.setValue(false);
            return;
          }
          addCheckedNode(node);
        });
    return checkbox;
  }

  private void rebuildIndex() {
    parentByNode.clear();
    childrenByNode.clear();
    nodeOrder.clear();

    Set<T> visited = newIdentitySet();
    for (T root : rootNodes) {
      indexNode(root, null, visited);
    }
    reconcileCheckedItems();
    applyFilter();
  }

  private void indexNode(T node, T parent, Set<T> visited) {
    if (node == null || visited.contains(node)) {
      return;
    }
    visited.add(node);
    parentByNode.put(node, parent);
    nodeOrder.add(node);
    List<T> children = normalizeNodes(childResolver.apply(node));
    childrenByNode.put(node, children);
    for (T child : children) {
      indexNode(child, node, visited);
    }
  }

  private void applyFilter() {
    String query = search.normalizedQuery();
    T selected = tree.asSingleSelect().getValue();

    TreeData<T> treeData = new TreeData<>();
    visibleNodes.clear();
    Set<T> visibleFilter = query.isBlank() ? null : visibleFromQuery(query);
    for (T root : rootNodes) {
      addVisibleNode(treeData, null, root, visibleFilter);
    }

    tree.setDataProvider(new TreeDataProvider<>(treeData));

    if (query.isBlank()) {
      tree.collapseRecursively(visibleRootNodes(), Integer.MAX_VALUE);
    } else {
      tree.expandRecursively(visibleRootNodes(), Integer.MAX_VALUE);
    }

    if (selected != null && visibleNodes.contains(selected)) {
      tree.select(selected);
    } else {
      tree.deselectAll();
    }
    notifyVisibleContentMetrics();
  }

  private void addVisibleNode(TreeData<T> treeData, T parent, T node, Set<T> visibleFilter) {
    if (node == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (visibleFilter != null && !visibleFilter.contains(node)) {
      return;
    }
    treeData.addItem(parent, node);
    visibleNodes.add(node);
    for (T child : childrenByNode.getOrDefault(node, List.of())) {
      addVisibleNode(treeData, node, child, visibleFilter);
    }
  }

  private Set<T> visibleFromQuery(String query) {
    Set<T> matches = newIdentitySet();
    for (T node : nodeOrder) {
      if (!matchesQuery(node, query)) {
        continue;
      }
      T cursor = node;
      while (cursor != null && !matches.contains(cursor)) {
        matches.add(cursor);
        cursor = parentByNode.get(cursor);
      }
    }
    return matches;
  }

  private boolean matchesQuery(T node, String query) {
    return StitchResultsSearch.normalize(labelOf(node)).contains(query);
  }

  private List<T> visibleRootNodes() {
    List<T> visibleRoots = new ArrayList<>();
    for (T root : rootNodes) {
      if (root != null && visibleNodes.contains(root)) {
        visibleRoots.add(root);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(visibleRoots);
  }

  private void expandAncestors(T value) {
    List<T> ancestors = new ArrayList<>();
    T cursor = parentByNode.get(value);
    while (cursor != null) {
      ancestors.add(cursor);
      cursor = parentByNode.get(cursor);
    }
    Collections.reverse(ancestors);
    if (!ancestors.isEmpty()) {
      tree.expand(ancestors);
    }
  }

  private boolean hasChildren(T node) {
    return node != null && !childrenByNode.getOrDefault(node, List.of()).isEmpty();
  }

  private void toggleExpanded(T node) {
    if (!hasChildren(node)) {
      return;
    }
    if (tree.isExpanded(node)) {
      tree.collapse(node);
    } else {
      tree.expand(node);
    }
  }

  private void notifySelection(T value) {
    for (Consumer<T> listener : List.copyOf(selectionListeners)) {
      listener.accept(value);
    }
  }

  private void addCheckedNode(T node) {
    if (checkedNodes.contains(node)) {
      return;
    }
    checkedItems.add(node);
    checkedNodes.add(node);
    notifyCheckedItemsChanged();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
  }

  private void removeCheckedNode(T node) {
    if (!checkedNodes.contains(node)) {
      return;
    }
    checkedNodes.remove(node);
    checkedItems.removeIf(value -> value == node);
    notifyCheckedItemsChanged();
    tree.getDataProvider().refreshAll();
  }

  private boolean canCheckNode(T node) {
    return checkboxSelectionEnabled
        && node != null
        && isCheckboxEligible(node)
        && (!checkedNodes.contains(node) || !hasReachedMaxCheckedCount());
  }

  private boolean isCheckboxEligible(T node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (checkboxSelectionMode == CheckboxSelectionMode.NODE_AND_LEAF) {
      return true;
    }
    boolean leaf = childrenByNode.getOrDefault(node, List.of()).isEmpty();
    if (checkboxSelectionMode == CheckboxSelectionMode.LEAF_ONLY) {
      return leaf;
    }
    return !leaf;
  }

  private boolean hasReachedMaxCheckedCount() {
    return checkboxMaxCheckedCount != null && checkedItems.size() >= checkboxMaxCheckedCount;
  }

  private void reconcileCheckedItems() {
    boolean changed = false;
    List<T> retained = new ArrayList<>();
    Set<T> retainedSet = newIdentitySet();
    for (T item : checkedItems) {
      if (item == null || !parentByNode.containsKey(item) || !isCheckboxEligible(item)) {
        changed = true;
        continue;
      }
      retained.add(item);
      retainedSet.add(item);
      if (checkboxMaxCheckedCount != null && retained.size() >= checkboxMaxCheckedCount) {
        changed = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    if (checkedItems.size() != retained.size()) {
      changed = true;
    }
    checkedItems.clear();
    checkedItems.addAll(retained);
    checkedNodes.clear();
    checkedNodes.addAll(retainedSet);
    if (changed) {
      notifyCheckedItemsChanged();
    }
  }

  private void notifyCheckedItemsChanged() {
    List<T> snapshot = List.copyOf(checkedItems);
    for (Consumer<List<T>> listener : List.copyOf(checkedItemsChangedListeners)) {
      listener.accept(snapshot);
    }
    maybeNotifyAutoThresholdReached(snapshot);
  }

  private void notifyVisibleContentMetrics() {
    int maxLabelLength = 0;
    int maxDepth = 0;
    for (T node : visibleNodes) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      maxLabelLength = Math.max(maxLabelLength, labelOf(node).length());
      maxDepth = Math.max(maxDepth, depthOf(node));
    }
    int visualUnits = maxLabelLength + (maxDepth * 2);
    visibleContentMetricsListener.accept(
        new VisibleContentMetrics(visibleNodes.size(), maxLabelLength, maxDepth, visualUnits));
  }

  private int depthOf(T node) {
    if (node == null) {
      return 0;
    }
    int depth = 0;
    T cursor = parentByNode.get(node);
    while (cursor != null) {
      depth++;
      cursor = parentByNode.get(cursor);
    }
    return depth;
  }

  private void maybeNotifyAutoThresholdReached(List<T> snapshot) {
    if (checkboxAutoTriggerCount == null || snapshot.size() != checkboxAutoTriggerCount) {
      return;
    }
    for (Consumer<List<T>> listener : List.copyOf(autoThresholdReachedListeners)) {
      listener.accept(snapshot);
    }
  }

  private String labelOf(T node) {
    String resolved = labelResolver.apply(node);
    return resolved == null ? "" : resolved;
  }

  private List<T> normalizeNodes(Collection<? extends T> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<T> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (T value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static <T> Set<T> newIdentitySet() {
    return Collections.newSetFromMap(new IdentityHashMap<>());
  }

  private static Integer normalizePositive(Integer value) {
    if (value == null || value <= 0) {
      return null;
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static void stopClickPropagation(Component component) {
    component.getElement().setAttribute("onclick", "event.stopPropagation();");
    component.getElement().setAttribute("onmousedown", "event.stopPropagation();");
    component.getElement().setAttribute("onmouseup", "event.stopPropagation();");
  }

  private static void applyClassNames(Component component, String classes) {
    if (component == null || classes == null || classes.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String token : classes.trim().split("\\s+")) {
      if (!token.isBlank()) {
        component.addClassName(token);
      }
    }
  }

  public enum CheckboxSelectionMode {
    LEAF_ONLY,
    NODE_ONLY,
    NODE_AND_LEAF
  }

  public enum NodeIconClickBehavior {
    SELECT,
    TOGGLE_EXPAND_COLLAPSE
  }

  public record VisibleContentMetrics(
      int visibleNodeCount, int maxLabelLength, int maxDepth, int visualUnits) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.tree;

/** Small adapter for mapping tree nodes to stable ids and resolving by id. */
public interface StitchTreeNodeAdapter<T> {
  String nodeId(T node);

  T nodeById(String nodeId);
}


org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/util/StitchComponents.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;

public final class StitchComponents {
  public static final String ATTR_COMPONENT_CODE = "data-stitch-code";
  public static final String ATTR_COMPONENT_ID = "data-stitch-id";
  public static final String ATTR_DEBUG_TOOLTIP = "data-stitch-debug-tooltip";
  private static volatile boolean debugLabelsEnabled;

  private StitchComponents() {}

  public static void configureDebugLabels(boolean enabled) {
    debugLabelsEnabled = enabled;
  }

  public static boolean debugLabelsEnabled() {
    return debugLabelsEnabled;
  }

  public static <T extends Component> T withCode(T component, String componentCode) {
    Component target = Objects.requireNonNull(component, "component");
    String code = requireCode(componentCode);
    target.getElement().setAttribute(ATTR_COMPONENT_CODE, code);
    target.getElement().setAttribute(ATTR_COMPONENT_ID, toStableId(code));
    if (debugLabelsEnabled) {
      target.getElement().setAttribute(ATTR_DEBUG_TOOLTIP, code);
      target.getElement().getClassList().add("stitch-debug-labeled");
    } else {
      target.getElement().removeAttribute(ATTR_DEBUG_TOOLTIP);
      target.getElement().getClassList().remove("stitch-debug-labeled");
    }
    return component;
  }

  private static String requireCode(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("componentCode is required");
    }
    return value.trim();
  }

  private static String toStableId(String code) {
    return code.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/view/StitchGroupedResultsPage.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.button.Button;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchFiltersBar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchGroupFilter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsSearch;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.session.StitchRuntimeContext;

public abstract class StitchGroupedResultsPage<R> extends StitchPage {
  private final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext;
  private final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar = new StitchFiltersBar();
  private final StitchResultsView<R> results = new StitchResultsView<>();
  private final StitchGroupFilter groupFilter;
  private final StitchResultsSearch searchField;
  private List<R> loadedRows = List.of();

  protected StitchGroupedResultsPage(
      StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext,
      String pageTitle,
      String pageSubtitle,
      String searchPlaceholder,
      String searchAriaLabel) {
    super(Objects.requireNonNull(pageTitle, "pageTitle"), Strings.firstNonBlank(pageSubtitle, ""));
    this.runtimeContext = Objects.requireNonNull(runtimeContext, "runtimeContext");
    this.groupFilter = new StitchGroupFilter(runtimeContext);
    this.searchField = new StitchResultsSearch(searchPlaceholder, searchAriaLabel);

    setSizeFull();
    body().setSizeFull();
    results.setWidthFull();
    results.setHeight(null);
    results.setPaginationEnabled(true);
    results.setPageSizeOptions(10, 25, 50, 100);
    results.setPageSize(10);
    results.setResultCountVisible(false);
    results.toolbar().setVisible(false);

    groupFilter.addValueChangeListener(event -> applyFilters());
    searchField.onQueryChange(query -> applyFilters());
  }

  protected final void initializeResultsScreen(
      String emptyTitle, String emptyMessage, String refreshAriaLabel) {
    results.setEmptyState(emptyTitle, emptyMessage);
    configureGrid(results.grid());

    Button refresh = new Button("REFRESH", event -> refreshRows());
    StitchResultsToolbar.stylePrimaryAction(refresh);
    refresh.addClassName("stitch-refresh-action");
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", refreshAriaLabel);
    refresh.getElement().setAttribute("title", refreshAriaLabel);

    configureFiltersBar(filtersBar, groupFilter, searchField, refresh);

    addToBody(filtersBar, results);
    refreshRows();
  }

  protected final StitchRuntimeContext runtimeContext() {
    return runtimeContext;
  }

  protected final StitchFiltersBar filtersBar() {
    return filtersBar;
  }

  protected final StitchGroupFilter groupFilter() {
    return groupFilter;
  }

  protected final StitchResultsSearch searchField() {
    return searchField;
  }

  protected final String selectedGroupFilterValue() {
    return groupFilter.selectedGroup();
  }

  protected final StitchResultsView<R> resultsView() {
    return results;
  }

  protected final void refreshRows() {
    List<R> rows = loadRows();
    Comparator<R> comparator = rowComparator();
    List<R> filtered = rows == null ? List.of() : rows.stream().filter(Objects::nonNull).toList();
    loadedRows =
        comparator == null
            ? filtered
            : filtered.stream().sorted(comparator).toList();
    onRowsRefreshed(loadedRows);
    applyFilters();
  }

  protected final void applyCurrentFilters() {
    applyFilters();
  }

  protected abstract void configureGrid(StitchGrid<R> grid);

  protected abstract List<R> loadRows();

  protected abstract Comparator<R> rowComparator();

  protected abstract String groupValue(R row);

  protected abstract boolean matchesSearch(R row, String normalizedQuery);

  protected boolean matchesAdditionalFilters(R row) {
    return true;
  }

  protected void onRowsRefreshed(List<R> rows) {}

  protected void configureFiltersBar(
      StitchFiltersBar filtersBar,
      StitchGroupFilter groupFilter,
      StitchResultsSearch searchField,
      Button refreshAction) {
    filtersBar.withGroupSelector(groupFilter).withFilter(searchField).withRightAction(refreshAction);
  }

  protected final String normalize(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? "" : normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  protected final boolean contains(String text, String normalizedQuery) {
    return normalize(text).contains(normalizedQuery);
  }

  private void applyFilters() {
    String query = searchField.normalizedQuery();
    List<String> effectiveGroups = groupFilter.effectiveGroups();
    List<R> filtered = loadedRows.stream().filter(row -> matchesGroup(row, effectiveGroups)).toList();
    filtered = filtered.stream().filter(this::matchesAdditionalFilters).toList();
    if (!query.isBlank()) {
      filtered = filtered.stream().filter(row -> matchesSearch(row, query)).toList();
    }
    results.setItems(filtered);
    results.setEmpty(filtered.isEmpty());
  }

  private boolean matchesGroup(R row, List<String> effectiveGroups) {
    if (row == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (effectiveGroups == null || effectiveGroups.isEmpty()) {
      return true;
    }
    String value = normalize(groupValue(row));
    for (String group : effectiveGroups) {
      if (value.equals(normalize(group))) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/view/StitchPage.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchPage extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchPageHeader header = new StitchPageHeader();
  private final VerticalLayout body = new VerticalLayout();

  public StitchPage() {
    this("", "");
  }

  public StitchPage(String pageTitle, String pageSubtitle) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setSizeFull();
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    getStyle().set("gap", "1.5rem");
    addClassName("stitch-page");

    header.setTitle(pageTitle);
    header.setSubtitle(pageSubtitle);

    body.setPadding(false);
    body.setSpacing(false);
    body.setSizeFull();
    body.setWidthFull();
    body.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    body.getStyle().set("gap", "1rem");
    body.addClassName("stitch-page-body");
    body.getElement().setAttribute("role", "main");

    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE);
    StitchComponents.withCode(body, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_BODY);

    add(header, body);
    setFlexGrow(1, body);
  }

  public StitchPage setPageTitle(String value) {
    header.setTitle(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPage setPageSubtitle(String value) {
    header.setSubtitle(value);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPage addPageAction(Component... components) {
    header.addAction(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPage addToBody(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      body.add(components);
    }
    return this;
  }

  public VerticalLayout body() {
    return body;
  }

  public StitchPageHeader header() {
    return header;
  }

  public StitchPageActions actions() {
    return header.actions();
  }
}

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchPageActions extends HorizontalLayout {

  public StitchPageActions() {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.4rem");
    setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    getStyle().set("flex-wrap", "wrap");
    addClassName("stitch-page-actions");
    getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Page actions");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_ACTIONS);
  }

  public StitchPageActions addActions(Component... components) {
    if (components != null) {
      add(components);
    }
    return this;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/view/StitchPageHeader.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.H1;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Paragraph;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchPageHeader extends HorizontalLayout {
  private final H1 title = new H1();
  private final Paragraph subtitle = new Paragraph();
  private final StitchPageActions actions = new StitchPageActions();

  public StitchPageHeader() {
    this("", "");
  }

  public StitchPageHeader(String headerTitle, String headerSubtitle) {
    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.8rem");
    addClassName("stitch-page-header");
    title.addClassName("stitch-page-title");
    subtitle.addClassName("stitch-page-subtitle");

    VerticalLayout titleBlock = new VerticalLayout(title, subtitle);
    titleBlock.setPadding(false);
    titleBlock.setSpacing(false);
    titleBlock.setWidthFull();
    titleBlock.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    titleBlock.getStyle().set("gap", "0.2rem");
    titleBlock.addClassName("stitch-page-title-block");

    setTitle(headerTitle);
    setSubtitle(headerSubtitle);

    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_HEADER);
    StitchComponents.withCode(title, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_TITLE);
    StitchComponents.withCode(subtitle, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_PAGE_SUBTITLE);

    add(titleBlock, actions);
    setFlexShrink(0, actions);
    expand(titleBlock);
  }

  public StitchPageHeader setTitle(String value) {
    title.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPageHeader setSubtitle(String value) {
    subtitle.setText(value == null ? "" : value.trim());
    subtitle.setVisible(!subtitle.getText().isBlank());
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPageHeader addAction(Component... components) {
    actions.addActions(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchPageActions actions() {
    return actions;
  }
}

===== FILE: fabric-lite-stitch/src/main/java/org/pronzato/fabric/stitch/view/StitchResultsView.java =====
package org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.view;

import com.vaadin.flow.component.Component;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Div;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.html.Span;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.FlexComponent.Alignment;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.HorizontalLayout;
import com.vaadin.flow.component.orderedlayout.VerticalLayout;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchComponentCodes;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchEmptyState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsPagination;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.component.StitchResultsToolbar;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.grid.StitchGrid;
import org.pronzato.fabric.stitch.util.StitchComponents;

public class StitchResultsView<T> extends VerticalLayout {
  private final StitchResultsToolbar toolbar = new StitchResultsToolbar();
  private final Div resultsArea = new Div();
  private final StitchGrid<T> grid;
  private final StitchEmptyState emptyState = new StitchEmptyState();
  private final HorizontalLayout footer = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout footerStart = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final HorizontalLayout footerEnd = new HorizontalLayout();
  private final StitchResultsPagination pagination = new StitchResultsPagination();
  private final Span resultCount = new Span();
  private List<T> allItems = List.of();
  private boolean empty;
  private boolean resultCountVisible;
  private boolean paginationEnabled = true;
  private int currentPage;

  public StitchResultsView() {
    this(new StitchGrid<>());
  }

  public StitchResultsView(StitchGrid<T> stitchGrid) {
    grid = Objects.requireNonNull(stitchGrid, "stitchGrid");

    setPadding(false);
    setSpacing(false);
    setWidthFull();
    applyShrinkToContentLayout();
    getStyle().set("gap", "0.7rem");
    getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    addClassName("stitch-results-view");
    StitchComponents.withCode(this, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_VIEW);
    toolbar.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Results toolbar");

    resultsArea.addClassName("stitch-results-area");
    resultsArea.setWidthFull();
    resultsArea.setHeight(null);
    resultsArea.getStyle().set("min-width", "0");
    resultsArea.getElement().setAttribute("role", "region");
    resultsArea.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Results panel");
    StitchComponents.withCode(resultsArea, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_AREA);

    emptyState.setVisible(false);
    grid.setVisible(true);
    grid.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Results grid");

    footer.setPadding(false);
    footer.setSpacing(false);
    footer.getStyle().set("gap", "0.7rem");
    footer.setWidthFull();
    footer.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    footer.setVisible(false);
    footer.addClassName("stitch-results-footer");
    footer.getElement().setAttribute("aria-label", "Results footer");
    StitchComponents.withCode(footer, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_FOOTER);

    footerStart.setPadding(false);
    footerStart.setSpacing(false);
    footerStart.getStyle().set("gap", "0.45rem");
    footerStart.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    footerStart.addClassName("stitch-results-footer-start");
    StitchComponents.withCode(footerStart, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_FOOTER_START);

    pagination
        .onPrevious(this::goToPreviousPage)
        .onNext(this::goToNextPage)
        .onPageSizeChange(
            value -> {
              currentPage = 0;
              refreshGridPage();
            });

    resultCount.setVisible(false);
    resultCount.addClassName("stitch-results-count");
    StitchComponents.withCode(resultCount, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_COUNT);

    footerEnd.setPadding(false);
    footerEnd.setSpacing(false);
    footerEnd.getStyle().set("gap", "0.4rem");
    footerEnd.setDefaultVerticalComponentAlignment(Alignment.CENTER);
    footerEnd.addClassName("stitch-results-status-bar");
    StitchComponents.withCode(footerEnd, StitchComponentCodes.STITCH_RESULTS_STATUS_BAR);

    Div footerSpacer = new Div();
    footerStart.add(pagination, resultCount);
    footer.add(footerStart, footerSpacer, footerEnd);
    footer.expand(footerSpacer);

    resultsArea.add(grid, emptyState, footer);
    add(toolbar, resultsArea);
    refreshGridPage();
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> addToolbarStart(Component... components) {
    toolbar.addStart(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> addToolbarFilters(Component... components) {
    toolbar.addFilters(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> addToolbarFilter(String label, Component component) {
    toolbar.addLabeledFilter(label, component);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> addToolbarEnd(Component... components) {
    toolbar.addEnd(components);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setItems(Collection<? extends T> items) {
    allItems = items == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(items);
    setEmpty(allItems.isEmpty());
    currentPage = Math.min(currentPage, maxPage());
    refreshGridPage();
    return this;
  }

  @SafeVarargs
  public final StitchResultsView<T> setItems(T... items) {
    if (items == null || items.length == 0) {
      return setItems(List.of());
    }
    return setItems(List.of(items));
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setEmpty(boolean value) {
    empty = value;
    emptyState.setVisible(empty);
    grid.setVisible(!empty);
    refreshGridPage();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setEmptyState(String title, String message) {
    emptyState.setTitle(title);
    emptyState.setMessage(message);
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> clearStatus() {
    footerEnd.removeAll();
    updateFooterVisibility();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setStatus(Component... components) {
    footerEnd.removeAll();
    if (components != null) {
      footerEnd.add(components);
    }
    updateFooterVisibility();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setResultCountVisible(boolean value) {
    resultCountVisible = value;
    resultCount.setVisible(resultCountVisible && !resultCount.getText().isBlank());
    updateFooterVisibility();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setResultCount(int value) {
    int normalized = Math.max(0, value);
    resultCount.setText(normalized + " result(s)");
    resultCount.setVisible(resultCountVisible && !resultCount.getText().isBlank());
    updateFooterVisibility();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setPaginationEnabled(boolean value) {
    paginationEnabled = value;
    currentPage = 0;
    refreshGridPage();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setPageSizeOptions(int... options) {
    pagination.setPageSizeOptions(options);
    currentPage = 0;
    refreshGridPage();
    return this;
  }

  public StitchResultsView<T> setPageSize(int value) {
    pagination.setPageSize(value);
    currentPage = 0;
    refreshGridPage();
    return this;
  }

  public boolean empty() {
    return empty;
  }

  public StitchResultsToolbar toolbar() {
    return toolbar;
  }

  public StitchGrid<T> grid() {
    return grid;
  }

  public StitchEmptyState emptyState() {
    return emptyState;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout statusBar() {
    return footerEnd;
  }

  public StitchResultsPagination pagination() {
    return pagination;
  }

  public HorizontalLayout footer() {
    return footer;
  }

  public Span resultCount() {
    return resultCount;
  }

  @Override
  public void setSizeFull() {
    setWidthFull();
    applyShrinkToContentLayout();
  }

  @Override
  public void setHeightFull() {
    applyShrinkToContentLayout();
  }

  private void applyShrinkToContentLayout() {
    super.setHeight(null);
    getStyle().set("height", "auto");
    getStyle().set("flex-grow", "0");
  }

  private void updateFooterVisibility() {
    boolean hasCount = resultCount.isVisible() && !resultCount.getText().isBlank();
    boolean hasPagination = pagination.isVisible();
    footerStart.setVisible(hasCount || hasPagination);
    footer.setVisible(footerStart.isVisible() || footerEnd.getComponentCount() > 0);
  }

  private int maxPage() {
    if (!paginationEnabled || allItems.isEmpty()) {
      return 0;
    }
    int pageSize = Math.max(1, pagination.pageSize());
    return Math.max(0, (allItems.size() - 1) / pageSize);
  }

  private void goToPreviousPage() {
    if (!paginationEnabled || currentPage <= 0) {
      return;
    }
    currentPage--;
    refreshGridPage();
  }

  private void goToNextPage() {
    if (!paginationEnabled || currentPage >= maxPage()) {
      return;
    }
    currentPage++;
    refreshGridPage();
  }

  private void refreshGridPage() {
    int total = allItems.size();
    if (total == 0 || !paginationEnabled) {
      currentPage = 0;
    } else {
      currentPage = Math.min(currentPage, maxPage());
    }

    List<T> pageItems;
    int totalPages;
    if (!paginationEnabled || total == 0) {
      totalPages = 1;
      pageItems = allItems;
    } else {
      int pageSize = Math.max(1, pagination.pageSize());
      int start = Math.min(currentPage * pageSize, total);
      int end = Math.min(start + pageSize, total);
      totalPages = Math.max(1, (int) Math.ceil((double) total / pageSize));
      pageItems = allItems.subList(start, end);
    }

    grid.setItems(pageItems);
    pagination.setVisible(paginationEnabled && !empty);
    pagination.setPageState(currentPage, totalPages, total);
    setResultCount(total);
  }
}
